sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgraha ed. by Horiuchi

(STT volume, page, section*)

*the numbers in the margin

sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ (STT 1,1,0)

vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ (STT 1,1,0)

evaṃ mayā śrutam (STT 1,1,1)

ekasmin samaye (STT 1,1,2)
bhagavān
sarvataghāgatavajrādhiṣṭhānasamayajñānavividhaviśeṣasamanvāgataḥ /(STT 1,1,2)
sarvatathāgataratnamukuṭatraidhātukadharmarājyābhiṣekaprāptaḥ /(STT 1,1,2)
sarvatathāgatasarvajñajñānamahāyogīśvaraḥ /(STT 1,2,2)
sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāsamatādhigataviśvakāryakaraṇatāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvāśāparipūrakaḥ /(STT 1,2,2)

mahākṛpo vairocanaḥ śāśvatas tryadhvasamayavyavasthitaḥ sarvakāryavākcittavajras tathāgataḥ (STT 1,2,3)

sarvatathāgatādhyuṣitapraśastastavite mahāmaṇiratnapratyupte vicitravarṇaghaṇṭāvasaktamārutoddhūtapaṭṭasrakcāmarahārārdhahārārdhacandropaśobhite 'kaniṣṭhadevarājasya
bhavane vijahāra /(STT 1,2,4)

navanavatibhir bodhisattvakoṭibhiḥ sārdhaṃ /(STT 1,2,5)
tad yathā :(STT 1,2,5)
vajrapāṇinā ca bodhisattvena /(STT 1,2,5)
avalokiteśvareṇa ca bodhisattvena /(STT 1,2,5)
ākāśagarbheṇa ca /(STT 1,2,5)
vajramuṣṭinā ca /(STT 1,2,5)
mañjuśriyā ca /(STT 1,2,5)
sahacittotpādadharmacakrapravartinā ca /(STT 1,2,5)
gaganagañjena ca /(STT 1,2,5)
sarvamārabalapramardinā ca /(STT 1,2,5)
evaṃpramukhair navanavatibhir bodhisattvakoṭibhiḥ /(STT 1,2,5)

gaṅgānadīvālukāsamākhyātaiś ca tathāgatais, tad yathāpi nāma tilabimbam iva, paripūrṇaṃ jambūdvīpesaṃdṛśyate /(STT 1,2,6)
taiś cāprameyais tathāgatakāyair ekaikasmāc ca tathāgatakāyād aprameyāsaṃkhyenāni buddhakṣetrāṇi saṃdṛśyante teṣu ca buddhakṣetreṣv imam eva dharmanayaṃ deśayanti sma //(STT 1,23,6)

atha bhagavān mahāvairocanaḥ (STT 1,9,7)
sarvākāśadhātusadāvasthitakāyavākcittavajraḥ /(STT 1,9,7)

sarvatathāgatasamavasaraṇatayā sarvavajradhātvavabodhanajñānasattvaḥ /(STT 1,9,8)
sarvākāśadhātuparamāṇurajovajrādhiṣṭhānasaṃbhavajñānagarbhaḥ /(STT 1,9,8)
sarvatathāgatānantatayā mahāvajrajñānābhiṣekaratnaḥ /(STT 1,9,8)
sarvākāśaspharaṇatathatājñānābhisaṃbodhyabhisaṃbodhibhūtaḥ sarvatathāgatātmabhāvaśuddhitayā svabhāvaśuddhasarvadharmaḥ /(STT 1,910,8)
sarvākāśavyāpisarvarūpasaṃdarśanajñānāśeṣā=navaśeṣasattvadhātuvinayanacaryāgryaḥ sarvatathāgatāmoghājñākāritayā sarvāsamānuttaraviśvakarmā //(STT 1,10,8)

sarvatathāgatamahābodhidṛḍhasattvaḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayaḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇajñāneśvaraḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatasādhukāraḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatamahābhiṣekaratnaḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatasūryaprabhāmaṇḍalaḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatacintārājamaṇiratnaketuḥ (STT 1,10,9)
sarvatathāgatamahāhāsaḥ (STT 1,10,9)

sarvatathāgatamahāśuddhadharmaḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgataprajñājñānaḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatacakraḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatasaṃdhābhāṣaḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatāmoghaviśvakāryaḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatamahāvīryasudṛḍhakavacaḥ /(STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatarakṣāparipālanavajrayakṣaḥ (STT 1,10,10)
sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajrabandhamudrājñānaḥ //(STT 1,10,10)

samantabhadraḥ svamogho māraḥ prāmodyanāyakaḥ /(STT 1,12,11)
khagarbhaḥ sumahātejāḥ ratnaketur mahāsmitaḥ /(STT 1,12,11)
avalokita maheśaś ca mañjuśrīḥ sarvamaṇḍalaḥ /(STT 1,12,11)
avāco viśvakarmā ca vīryaś caṇḍo dṛḍhagarbhaḥ //(STT 1,13,11)

vajro 'ṅkuśaḥ śaras tuṣṭī ratnaḥ sūryo dhvajaḥ smitaḥ /(STT 1,1314,12)
padmaḥ kośaḥ sucakro vāk karma varma bhayo grahaḥ //(STT 1,14,12)

anādinidhanaḥ śāntaḥ krūraḥ krodho mahākṣamaḥ /(STT 1,14,13)
yakṣaḥ surākṣaso dhīraḥ sauriḥ śaurir mahāvibhuḥ //(STT 1,1415,13)
umāpatiḥ prajñānātho viṣṇujiṣṇur mahāmuniḥ /(STT 1,15,13)
lokapālo nabho bhūmis trilokas tu tridhātukaḥ //(STT 1,15,13)

mahābhūtaḥ susattvārthaḥ sarvaḥ śarvaḥ pitāmahaḥ /(STT 1,15,14)
saṃsāro nirvṛtiḥ śaśvat śaśvān samyagvṛttir mahāmahaḥ //(STT 1,15,14)
buddhaḥ śuddho mahāyānas tribhavaḥ śāśvato hi saḥ /(STT 1,15,14)
trilokavijayī śaṃbhuḥ śaṃbhunāthaḥ pradāmakaḥ //(STT 1,15,14)

vajranāthaḥ subhūmyagryo jñānaḥ pāramitānayaḥ /(STT 1,15,15)
vimokṣo bodhisattvaś ca caryaḥ sarvatathāgataḥ //(STT 1,15,15)
buddhārtho buddhahṛdayaḥ sarvabodhir anuttaraḥ /(STT 1,15,15)
vairocano jino nāthaḥ svayambhūr dhāraṇī smṛtiḥ //(STT 1,15,15)

mahāsattvo mahāmudraḥ samādhir buddhakarmakṛt /(STT 1,15,16)
sarvabuddh'ātmako bhūtaḥ sattvo nityārthabodhakaḥ //(STT 1,15,16)
mahāsthāṇur mahākālo mahārāgo mahāsukhaḥ /(STT 1,15,16)
mahopāyo mahāgryāgryaḥ sarvāgryo bhuvaneśvaraḥ //(STT 1,15,16)

bhagavān mahābodhicittaḥ samantabhadro mahābodhisattvaḥ
sarvatathāgatahṛdayeṣu vijahāra //.(STT 1,22,17)

atha sarvatathāgatair idaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ, tad yathā tilabimbam iva, paripūrṇam /.(STT 1,22,172)

atha khalu sarvatathāgatāḥ mahāsamājam āpadya yena sarvārthasiddhir bodhisattvo mahāsattvo bodhimaṇḍaniṣaṇṇas, tenopajagmuḥ /. upetya bodhisattvasya sāṃbhogikaiḥ kāyair darśanaṃ dattvaivam āhuḥ /:(STT 1,23,18)
" kathaṃ kulaputrānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbhotsyase, yas tvaṃ sarvatathāgatatattvānabhijñatayā sarvaduṣkarāṇy utsahasīti //.(STT 1,23,18)

atha sarvārthasiddhir bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvatathāgataiś coditaḥ samānas tataḥ āsphānakasamādhito vyutthāya sarvatathāgatān praṇipatyāhūyaivam āha/:(STT 1,24,19)
" bhagavantas tathāgatāḥ ājñāpayata !: ' kathaṃ pratipadyāmi ? kīdṛśaṃ tattvam ?" iti //(STT 1,24,19)

evam ukte sarvatathāgatās taṃ bodhisattvam ekakaṇṭhenaivam āhuḥ //:(STT 1,24,20)
" pratipadyasva, kulaputra, svacittapratyavekṣaṇasamādhānena prakṛtisiddhena rucijaptena mantreṇe ! " 'ti //.(STT 1,24,20)
' oṃ cittaprativedhaṃ karomi ' // ".(STT 1,24,20)

atha bodhisattvah sarvatathāgatān evam āha /:(STT 1,25,21)
" ājñātaṃ me, bhagavantas tathāgatāḥ, svahṛdi candramaṇḍalākāraṃ paśyāmī " 'ti sarvatathāgatāḥ procuḥ :(STT 1,25,21)
" prakṛtiprabhāsvaram idaṃ, kulaputra, cittam. tad yathā parikarmyate tat tathaiva bhavati //:(STT 1,25,21)
tad yathāpi nāma śvetavastrarāgarañjanam ' iti /(STT 1,25,21)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaracittajñānasya sphīṭīkaraṇahetoḥ punar api tasmai bodhisattvāya, oṃ bodhicittam utpādayāmīty anena prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa bodhicittam utpāditavantaḥ /.(STT 1,25,22)

atha bodhisattvaḥ punar api sarvatathāgatājñayā bodhicittam utpādyaivam āha /:(STT 1,25,23)
" yat tac candramaṇḍalākāraṃ tac candramaṇḍalam eva paśyāmi /."(STT 1,25,23)

sarvatathāgatāḥ āhuḥ /:(STT 1,25,24)
" sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ te samantabhadraś cittotpādaḥ sāmīcībhūtaḥ /.(STT 1,25,24)
tad sādhu pratipadyasva ! sarvatathāgatasamantabhadracittotpādasya dṛḍhīkaraṇahetoḥ svahṛdi candramaṇḍale vajrabimbaṃ cintayānena mantreṇa! //:(STT 1,2526,24)
' oṃ tiṣṭha ! vajra ! //"(STT 1,26,24)

bodhisattva āha /:(STT 1,27,25)
" paśyāmi, bhagavantas tathāgatāś, candramaṇḍale vajram //"(STT 1,27,25)

sarvatathāgatāḥ āhuḥ /:(STT 1,27,25-2)
" dṛḍhīkurv idaṃ sarvatathāgatasamantabhadracittavajram anena mantreṇa !//:(STT 1,27,252)
'oṃ vajrātmako 'ham !'//"(STT 1,27,25-2)

atha yāvantaḥ sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇāḥ sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajradhātavas, te sarve sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena tasmin sattvavajre praviṣṭāḥ //.(STT 1,27,26)
tataḥ sarvatathāgataiḥ sa bhagavān sarvārthasiddhir mahābodhisattvo 'vajradhātur vajradhātur !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇaibhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,27,26)

atha vajradhātur mahābodhisattvas tān sarvatathāgatān evam āha /:(STT 1,28,27)
" paśyāmi, bhagavantas tathāgatāḥ, sarvatathāgatakāyam ātmānam //"(STT 1,28,27)

sarvatathāgatāḥ prāhuḥ /:(STT 1,27,28)
" tena hi mahāsattvaḥ ! sattvavajraṃ sarvākāravaropetaṃ buddhabimbam ātmānaṃ bhāvayā ! 'nena prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa rucitaḥ parijāpya //:(STT 1,28,28)
'oṃ yathā sarvatathāgatās tathā 'ham ' "//(STT 1,28,28)

athaivam ukte vajradhātur mahābodhisattvas tathāgatam ātmānam abhisaṃbudhya tān sarvatathāgatān praṇipatyāhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,28,29)
" adhitiṣṭhata māṃ ! bhagavantas tathāgatāḥ ! imām abhisaṃbodhiṃ dṛdhīkuruta ce !" 'ti //(STT 1,2829,29)

athaivam ukte sarvatathāgatāḥ vajradhātos tathāgatasya tasmin sattvavajre praviṣṭāḥ iti //.(STT 1,29,30)

atha bhagavān vajradhātus tathāgatas tasminn eva kṣaṇe sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhisaṃbuddhaḥ sarvatathāgatavajrasamatājñānamudrāguhyasamayapraviṣṭaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmasamatājñānādhigamasvabhāvaśuddhaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvasamatāprakṛtiprabhāsvarajñānākārabhūtas tathāgato 'rhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ iti //.(STT 1,29,31)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punar api tataḥ sarvatathāgatasattvavajrān niḥsṛtyākāśagarbhamahāmaṇiratnābhiṣekeṇābhiṣcyāvalokiteśvaradharmajñānam utpādya, sarvatathāgataviśvakarmatāyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya,yena sumerugirimūrdhā, yena ca vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgāras, tenopasaṃkrāntāḥ /.(STT 1,30,32)
upasaṃkramya vajradhātuṃ tathāgataṃ sarvatathāgatatve 'dhiṣṭhāya, sarvatathāgatasiṃhāsane sarvato mukhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayām āsur iti //(STT 1,30,32)

atha khalv akṣobhyas tathāgato, ratnasaṃbhavaś ca tathāgato, lokeśvararājaś ca tathāgato, 'moghasiddhiś ca tathāgataḥ, sarvatathāgatatvaṃ svayam ātmany adhiṣṭhāya bhagavataḥ śākyamunes tathāgatasya sarvasamatāsuprativedhatvāt /(STT 1,31,33)
sarvadiksamatām adhyālambya catasṛṣu dikṣu niṣaṇṇāḥ //.(STT 1,31,33)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgato 'cirābhisaṃbuddhaḥ sarvatathāgatasamantabhadrahṛdayaḥ sarvatathāgatākāśasaṃbhavamahāmaṇiratnābhiṣekābhiṣiktaḥ sarvatathāgatāvalokiteśvaradharmajñānaparamapāramiprāptaḥ sarvatathāgataviśvakarmatāmoghāpratihataśāsanaḥ paripūraṇakāryaḥ paripūrṇamanorathaḥ /(STT 1,32,34)
sarvatathāgatatvaṃ svayam ātmany adhiṣṭhāya,(STT 1,32,34)

sarvatathāgatasamantabhadramahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃsvahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,32,35)
'vajrasattva '/(STT 1,32,35)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān samantabhadraś candramaṇḍalāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya sarvasattvānāṃ mahābodhicittāni saṃśodhya sarvatathāgatānāṃ sarvapārśveṣv avasthitaḥ /.(STT 1,36,36)
atha tebhyaś candramaṇḍalebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatajñānavajrāṇi viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya hṛdaye praviṣṭāni /.(STT 1,36,36)

sudṛḍhatvāc ca vajrasattvasamādheḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena caikaghanaḥ sakalākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo raśmimālī pañcamūrdhā sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajramayo vajravigrahaḥ prādur bhūya, sarvatathāgatahṛdayān niṣkramya pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,36,37)

atha tato vajrād vajr'ākārāḥ raśmayo vicitravarṇarūpaḥ sarvalokadhātvābhāsanaspharaṇāh viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,36,38)

tebhyaś ca vajraraśmimukhebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahāḥ viniḥsṛtya sakaladharmadhātusamavasaraṇeṣu sarv'ākāśadhātuparyavasāneṣu sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudreṣu sarvatathāgatasamantājñānābhijñāsvabhisaṃbodhāt /(STT 1,36,39)
sarvatathāgatamahābodhicittotpādana,samantabhadravividhacaryāniṣpādana, sarvatathāgatakulārāgaṇa, mahābodhimaṇḍopasaṃkramaṇa,saddharmacakrapravartanādīni yāvad aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātu, paritrāṇa, sarvahitasukha, sarvatathāgatajñānābhijñottamasiddhiniṣpādanādīni sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni saṃdarśya /,(STT 1,3637,39)

samantabhadratvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ, sudṛdhatvāc caikaghanaḥ samantabhadramahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //.(STT 1,37,40)
" aho samantabhadro 'ham dṛḍhasattvaḥ svayaṃbhuvām /(STT 1,37,40)
yad dṛḍhatvād akāyo 'pi sattvakāyatvam āgataḥ "//(STT 1,37,40)

atha samantabhadramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,3940,41)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatajñānasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgataśīlasamādhiprajñāvimuktivimuktijñānadarśanadharmacakrapravartanasattvārthamahopāyabalavīryamahājñānasamayam, aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvādhipatyasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhijñānuttaramahāyānābhisamayottamasiddhyavāptiphalahetos, tat sarvatathāgatasiddhivajraṃ tasmai samantabhadrāya mahābodhisattvāya sarvatathāgatacakravartitve sarvabuddhakāyaratnamukuṭapaṭṭābhiṣekeṇabhiṣicya pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,40,42)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajrapāṇir vajrapāṇir !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣitaḥ //(STT 1,40,42)

atha vajrapāṇir bodhisattvo mahāsattvo vāmavajragarvollālanatayā tad vajraṃ svahṛdy utkarṣaṇayogena dhārayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,40,43)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ siddhivajram anuttaram /(STT 1,40,43)
ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ vajraṃ vajrapratiṣṭhitam " iti // //(STT 1,40,43)

atha bhagavām punar apy amogharājamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,41,44)
' vajrarāja '//(STT 1,41,44)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatamahāṅkuśāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭavaikaghano vajrāṅkuśamahāvigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,41,45)

atha tato vajrāṅkuśamahāvigrahāt /(STT 1,41,46)
sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurājaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahāḥ viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, svamogharājatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano 'mogharājamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,4142,46)
" aho hy amogharāja 'haṃ vajrasaṃbhavam aṅkuśaḥ /(STT 1,42,46)
yat sarvavyāpino buddhāḥ samākṛṣyanti siddhaya " iti //(STT 1,42,46)

atha so 'mogharājamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍal'āśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñānaṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,42,47)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇasamayam, aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvākarṣaṇasarva sukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasamājādhiṣṭhānottamasiddhyarthaṃ tad vajrāṅkuśaṃ tasmā amogharājāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,4243,48)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajrākarṣo vajr'ākarṣaḥ !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,43,48)

atha vajrākarṣo bodhisattvas tena vajrāṅkuśena sarvatathāgatān ākarṣayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrajñānam anuttaram /(STT 1,43,49)
yat sarvabuddhārthasiddhyarthaṃ samākarṣaṇam uttamam " iti // //(STT 1,43,49)
atha bhagavān punar api māramahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,43,50)
' vajrarāga '//(STT 1,43,50)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatakusumānyudhāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭaikaghano mahāvajravāṇavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,43,51)

atha tato vajravāṇavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sumāraṇatāvad vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano māramahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āha //:(STT 1,44,52)
" aho svabhāvaśuddho 'ham anurāgaḥ svayaṃbhuvām /(STT 1,44,52)
yac chuddhyarthaṃ viraktānāṃ rāgeṇa vinayanti hi // "(STT 1,44,52)

atha sa māramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,44,53)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatamāraṇavajrasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhāṭvanurāgaṇasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatamārakarmottamasiddhyavāptiphalahetos tad vajravāṇaṃ tasmai mārāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,44,54)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajradhanur vajradhanur !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhisiktaḥ /.(STT 1,44,54)

atha vajradhanur bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajravāṇena sarvatathāgatān mārayann idam udanam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,44,55)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ rāgajñānam anāvilam /(STT 1,44,55)
hatvā virāgaṃ rāgeṇa sarvasaukhyaṃ dadanti hi // //(STT 1,44,55)

atha bhagavān punar api prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatapramodasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,45,56)
' vajrasādhu '//(STT 1,45,56)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sādhukārāṇi bhūtvā bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭaikaghano bhūtvā vajratuṣṭivigrahaḥ prādur bhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,45,57)

atha tato vajratuṣṭivigrahaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇuparamāṇurājaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatasādhukār'ādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, supramodyatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //(STT 1,45,58)
" aho hi sādhukāro 'haṃ sarvaḥ sarvavidāṃ varaḥ /(STT 1,45,58)
yad vikalpaprahīṇānāṃ tuṣṭiṃ janayate dhruvam " //(STT 1,45,58)

atha sa prāmodyarājamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,45,59)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasaṃtoṣaṇavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya sarvatathāgatānuttaraprāmodyajñānasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvasattvasaṃtoṣaṇamahāsukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatānuttaraharṣarasottamasiddhiprāptiphalahetos tad vajratuṣṭiṃ tasmai prāmodyarājāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /. (STT 1,4546,60)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajraharṣo vajraharṣa !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,46,60)

atha vajraharṣo bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajratuṣṭinā sarvatathāgatān sādhukāraiḥ praharṣayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,46,61)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sādhukārapravartakam/(STT 1,46,61)
sarvatuṣṭikaraṃ vajraṃ divyaṃ prāmodyavardhanam " iti //(STT 1,46,61)

mahābodhicittaṃ sarvatathāgat'ākarṣaṇasamayaḥ sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇajñānaṃ mahātuṣṭiś ce 'ti /(STT 1,46,62)
sarvatathāgatamahāsamayasattvāḥ // //(STT 1,46,62)

atha bhagavān punar apy ākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,4647,63)
' vajraratna " //(STT 1,47,63)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātresarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvākāśasamatājñānasuprativedhatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvākāśaraśmayo bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /. taiḥ sarvākāśaraśmibhiḥ sarvalokadhātavo 'vabhāsitāḥ /(STT 1,47,64)
 sarvākāśadhātumayāḥ saṃvṛttā abhūvān //.(STT 1,47,64)

atha sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena *sarvo 'sāv ākāśa(sarvāsāvākāśā)dhātur bhagavato  vairocanasya hṛdaye pratiṣṭaḥ /,(STT 1,47,65)
suparibhāvitatvāc ca vajrasattvasamādheḥ sarvākāśadhātugarbhamayaḥ, sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇa*pramāṇo(pramāṇā) mahāvajraratnavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya/ bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /(STT 1,47,65)

atha tasmād vajraratnavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahāḥ prādurbhūya sarvatathāgatābhiṣekādīni sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni sarvalokadhātuṣu kṛtvā sarvākāśadhātugarbhasusaṃbhavatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghana ākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,47,66)
" aho hi svabhiṣeko 'haṃ vajraratnam anuttaram /(STT 1,47,66)
yan niḥsaṅgā api jinās tridhātupatayaḥ smṛtāḥ " //(STT 1,47,66)

atha sa ākāśagarbhamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvataghāgatānāṃ purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām asa //(STT 1,48,67)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatamaṇiratnavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatābhiprāyaparipūraṇasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvārthapariprāptisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatārthasaṃpaduttamasiddhiprāptyai tad vajramaṇiṃ tasmā ākāśagarbhāya mahābodhisattvāya vajraratnacakravartitve vajraratnāṅkuśābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,4849,68)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajragarbho vajragarbha !! " iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,49,68)

atha vajragarbho mahābodhisattvas tad vajramaṇiṃ svābhiṣekasthāne sthāpayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,49,69)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sattvadhātvabhiṣecanam /(STT 1,49,69)
ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ ratne ratnaṃ niyojitam " iti // //(STT 1,49,69)

atha bhagavān punar api mahātejamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgataraśmisamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,50,70)
' vajrateja ' //(STT 1,50,70)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahāsūryamaṇḍalāni bhūtvā bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭaikaghano vajrasūryavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,50,71)

atha tato vajrasūryamaṇḍalāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgataraśmipramāñcan'ādīni sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sumahātejastvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano mahātejamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,50,72)
" aho hy anupamaṃ tejaḥ sattvadhātvavabhāsanam /(STT 1,50,72)
yac chodhayati śuddhānāṃ buddhānām api tāyinām " //(STT 1,50,72)

atha sa vimalatejamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,50,73)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataprabhāmaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgataraśmisamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātvanupamatejaḥsarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasvayaṃprabhāvāptyuttamasiddhaye tad vajrasūryaṃ tasmaimahātejāya mahābodhisattvāya tataiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,5051,732)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajraprabho vajraprabha ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,51,732)

atha vajraprabho mahābodhisattvas tena vajrasūryeṇa sarvatathāgatān avabhāsayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //(STT 1,51,74)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānām ajñānadhvāntanāśanam /(STT 1,51,74)
paramāṇurajaḥsaṃkhyasūryādhikataraprabham " iti // //(STT 1,51,74)

atha bhagavān punar api ratnaketubodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatāśaparipūraṇasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,52,75)
' vajraketu '//(STT 1,52,75)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharo vicitravarṇarūpālaṅkārasaṃsthānāḥ patākā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭaikaghano vajradhvajavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,52,76)

atha tato vajradhvajavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā, sarvatathāgataratnadhvajocchrayaṇādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, mahāratnaketutvād vajrasarvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano ratnaketumahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,52,77)
" aho hy asadṛśaḥ ketur ahaṃ sarvārthasiddhinām /(STT 1,52,77)
yat sarvāśāparipūrṇānāṃ sarvārthaparipūraṇam " iti //(STT 1,52,77)

atha sa ratnaketur mahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād a vatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,52,78)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatocchrayādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya sarvatathāgatacintārājamaṇidhvajocchrayaṇsamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvasarvāśāparipūrisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatamahārthottamasiddhiprāptiphalahetos tad vajradhvajaṃ tasmai ratnaketave mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,5253,79)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajrayaṣṭir vajrayaṣṭir !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //.(STT 1,53,79)

atha vajrayaṣṭir bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajradhvajena sarvatathāgatān dānapāramitāyāṃ niyojanann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,53,80)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvāśāparipūraṇam /(STT 1,53,80)
cintāmaṇidhvajaṃ nāma dānapāramitānayam " iti // //(STT 1,53,80)

atha bhagavān punar api nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgataprītisamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,5354,81)
' vajrahāsa '//(STT 1,54,81)

asthāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasmitāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrasmitavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya, pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,54,82)

atha tato vajrasmitavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya sarvatathāgatādbhutādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā /(STT 1,54,83)
nityaprītipramuditendriyatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya /(STT 1,54,83)
bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,54,83)
" aho mahāhāsam ahaṃ sarvāgryāṇāṃ mahādbhutam /(STT 1,54,83)
yat prayuñjanti buddhārthaṃ sadaiva susamāhitāḥ " //(STT 1,54,83)

atha sa nityaprītipramuditendriyamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,54,84)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatādbhutādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya sarvatathāgatābhūtopādasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvendriyānuttarasukhasamuanasyānubhavanārhaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatendriyapariśodhanajñānābhijñāvāptiphalahetos tad vajrasmitaṃ tasmai nityaprītipramuditendriyāya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /. (STT 1,5455,85)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajraprītir vajraprītir !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇabhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,55,85)

atha vajraprītir bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajrasmitena sarvatathāgatān praharṣyann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,55,86)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānām adbhutotpādadarśakam /(STT 1,55,86)
mahāharṣakaraṃ jñānam ajñātaṃ parasāmitir śāstribhir " iti //(STT 1,55,86)

mahābhiṣeko vyāmaprabhāmaṇḍalaṃ mahāsattvārtho mahāhāsaś ce 'ti /(STT 1,55,87)
sarvatathāgatamahābhiṣekasattvāḥ // //(STT 1,55,87)

atha bhagavān punar apy avalokiteśvaramahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatadharmasamayaṃ nāma
sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //(STT 1,56,88)
' vajradharma ' //(STT 1,56,88)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ svabhāvaśuddhadharmasamatājñānasuprativedhatvad vajrasattvasamādheḥ saddharmaraśmayo bhūtvā viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,56,89)
taiḥ saddharmaraśmibhiḥ sarvalikadhātavo 'vabhāsitāḥ /,(STT 1,56,89)
dharmadhātumayāḥ saṃvṛttā abhūvan //.(STT 1,56,89)

sa ca sakalo dharmadhātur bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghanaḥ sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāpadmavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,56,90)

atha tasmād vajrapadmavigrahāt /(STT 1,56,91)
sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajahsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānābhijñādīni sarvabuddhārddhivikurvitāni sarvalokadhātuṣu kṛtvā svavalokanaiśvaryatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano 'valokiteśvaramahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //(STT 1,56,91)
" aho hi paramārtho 'haṃ ādiśuddhaḥ svayaṃbhuvām /(STT 1,56,91)
yat kolopamadharmāṇāṃ viśuddhir upalabhyate " //(STT 1,56,91)

atha so 'valokiteśvaramahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,57,92)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgataviśodhanasamayam aśeṣānvaśeṣasattvātmapariśuddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatadharmajñānābhijñāvāptiphalahetos tad vajrapadmaṃ tasmā avalokiteśvarāya mahābodhisattvāya saddharmacakravartitve sarvatathāgatadharmakāyābhiṣekeṇabhiṣicya pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,57,93)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajranetro vajranetra !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,57,93)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tad vajrapadmaṃ pattravikāsanatayā rāgaviśuddhinirlepasvabhāvāvalokanatayā 'valokayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,57,94)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ rāgatattvāvabodhanam /(STT 1,57,94)
ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ dharmaṃ dharmapratiṣṭhitam " iti // //(STT 1,5758,94)

atha bhagavān punar api mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatamahāprajñājñānasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,58,95)
' vajratīkṣṇa ' //(STT 1,58,95)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ prajñāśatrāṇi bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrakośavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,5859,96)

atha tato vajrakośavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā sarvatathāgataprajñājñānādīni sarvabhuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sumañjuśriyatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,59,97)
" aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ mañjughoṣam ahaṃ smṛtaḥ //(STT 1,59,97)
yat prajñāyā arūpiṇyā ghoṣattvam upalabhyate " //(STT 1,59,97)

atha sa mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍal'āśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,59,98)

atha bhagavan sarvatathāgataprajñājñānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatakleśacchedanasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvaduḥkhacchedanasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgataghoṣānugaprajñāpāripūryuttamasiddhyarthaṃ tad vajrakośaṃ tasmai mañjuśriye mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt/.(STT 1,60,99)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajrabuddhir vajrabuddhir !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,60,99)

atha sa vajrabuddhir bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajrakośena sarvatathāgatān praharann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,60,100)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ prajñāpāramitānayam /(STT 1,60,100)
chettāraṃ sarvaśatrūṇāṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param " iti // //(STT 1,60,100)

atha bhagavān punar api sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatacakrasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,60,101)
' vajrahetu ' //(STT 1,61,101)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharo vajradhātumahāmaṇḍal'ādīni sarvatathāgatamaṇḍalāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajracakravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,61,102)

atha tato vajracakravigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā sahacittotpādadharmacakrapravartanatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa /:(STT 1,61,103)
" aho vajramayaṃ cakram ahaṃ vajrāgradharmiṇām /(STT 1,61,103)
yac cittotpādamātreṇa dharmacakraṃ pravartate " //(STT 1,61,103)

atha sa sahacittopāditadharmacakrapravartimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,62,104)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatacakravajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatamahāmaṇḍalasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātupraveṣāvaivartikacakrasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhagavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasaddharmacakrapravartanottamasiddhinimittaṃ tad vajracakraṃ tasmai sahacittotpāditadharmacakrapravartine mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,62,105)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajramaṇḍo vajramaṇḍa !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,62,105)

atha vajramaṇḍo bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajracakreṇa sarvatathāgatān avaivartikatve pratiṣṭhāpayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,62,106)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvadharmaviśodhakam /(STT 1,62,106)
avaivartikacakraṃ tu bodhimaṇḍam iti smṛtam " iti // //(STT 1,62-63,106)

atha bhagavān punar apy avācamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavadharmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatajāpasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,63,107)
' vajrabhāṣa ' //(STT 1,63,107)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatadharmākṣarāṇi bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrajāpavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhi=taḥ /.(STT 1,6364,108)

atha tato vajrajāpavagrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇuraraḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatadharmatādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, svavācatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghano 'vācamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,64,109)
" aho svayaṃbhuvāṃ guhyaṃ saṃdhābhāṣam ahaṃ smṛtaḥ /(STT 1,64,109)
yad deśayanti saddharmaṃ vākprapañcavivarjitam " //(STT 1,64,109)

atha so 'vācamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṣṭhataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,65,110)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatavāgvajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya sarvatathāgatavāgjñānasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuvāksiddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatavāgguhyatāprāptyuttamasiddhaye tad vajrajāpaṃ tasmā avacārya mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,65,111)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajravāco vajravāca !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,65,111)

atha vajravāco bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajrajāpena sarvatathāgatān saṃlāpayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,65,112)
idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrajāpau udāhṛtam /(STT 1,65,112)
sarvatathāgatānāṃ tu mantrāṇām āśu sādhanam iti //(STT 1,65,112)

vajradharmatājñānaṃ sarvatathāgataprajñājñānaṃ mahācakrapravartanajñānaṃ sarvatathāgatavākprapañcavinivartana jñānaṃ ce 'ti /(STT 1,67,113)
sarvatathāgatamahājñānasattvāḥ // //(STT 1,67,113)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,67,114)
' vajrakarma ' //(STT 1,67,114)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvakarmasamatājñānasuprativedhatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmaraśmayo bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /.(STT 1,67,115)
taiś ca sarvatathāgatakarmaraśmibhiḥ sarvalokadhātavo 'vabhāsitāḥ sarvatathāgatakarmadhātumayāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ sa sakalaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmadhātur bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvā, sarv'ākāśadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇas, tataḥ sarvatathāgatakarmadhātutaḥ, karmavajravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,67,115)

atha tataḥ karmavajravigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvatathāgatakarm'ādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sarvatathāgatānantakarmatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,6768,116)
" aho hy amoghaṃ buddhānāṃ sarvakarmam ahaṃ bahu /(STT 1,68,116)
yad anābhogabuddhārthaṃ vajrakarma pravartate " //(STT 1,68,116)

atha sa sarvatathāgataviśvakarmamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagvato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,68,117)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatāmoghavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatapūjāpravartanādyaprameyāmoghasarvakarmavidhivistarasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātusarvakarmasiddhisarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatavajrakarmatājñānābhijñottamasiddhiphalahetos tat karmavajraṃ tasmai sarvatathāgatavajrakarmaṇe mahābodhisattvāya sarvakarmacakravartitve sarvatathāgatavajrābhiṣekeṇābhiṣicya pāṇibhyām anuprādāt. tataḥ sarva tathāgatair ' vajraviśvo vajraviśva !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,6869,118)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tad vajraṃ svahṛdi sthāpya sarvatathāgatān karmatāyāṃ niyijayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,69,119)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ viśvakarmakaraṃ param /(STT 1,69,119)
ahaṃ mama kare dattaṃ viśve viśvaṃ niyojitam " iti //(STT 1,69,119)

atha bhagavān duryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatarakṣāsamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,71,120)
' vajrarakṣa '//(STT 1,71,120)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajrapāṇir dṛḍhakavacāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano mahāvajrakavacavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya bhagavataḥ pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,71,121)

atha tato vajrakavacavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatarakṣāvidhivistarakarmādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, duryodhanavīryatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanoduryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvavigrahaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,71,122)
" aho vīryamayo varmaḥ sudṛḍho 'haṃ dṛḍhātmānām /(STT 1,71,122)
yad dṛḍhatvād akāyānāṃ vajrakāyakaraṃ param " iti //(STT 1,71,122)

atha sa duryodhanavīryamahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ dakṣiṇacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,72,123)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatadṛḍhavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatavīryapāramitāsamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatavajrakāyaprāptyuttamasiddhihetos tad vajravarmaṃ tasmai duryodhanavīryāya mahābodhisattvāya pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,72,124)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajramitro vajramitra !! ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,72,124)

atha vajramitro bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajravarmaṇā sarvatathāgatān kavacāyann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,72,125)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ maitrīkavacam uttamam /(STT 1,72,125)
dṛḍhavīryamahārakṣaṃ mahāmitram udāhṛtam " iti // //(STT 1,72,125)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvamārapramardimahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhanavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatopāyasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathā=gatahṛdayaṃ sarvahṛdayāṇ niścacāra //:(STT 1,73,126)
' vajrayakṣa '//(STT 1,73,126)

athāsamin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharo mahādaṃṣṭrāyudhāni bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajradaṃṣṭrāvigrahaḥ prādurbhūya pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,73,127)

atha tato vajradaṃṣṭrāvigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā sarvatathāgataraudravinayādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sarvamarasupramarditvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ sarvamārapramardimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedaṃ udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,73,128)
" aho mahopāyam ahaṃ buddhānāṃ karuṇātmanām /(STT 1,73,128)
yat sattvārthatayā śāntā raudratvam api kurvate //(STT 1,73,128)

atha sa sarvamārapramardimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ vāmacandramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,73,129)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatapracaṇḍavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya sarvatathāgataduṣṭavinayasamayam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātvabhayasarvasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatamahopāyajñānābhijñāvāptyuttamasiddhiphalahetos tad vajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ tasmaisarvamārapramardine mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt /.(STT 1,7374,130)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair ' vajracaṇḍo vajracaṇḍa ' iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,74,130)

atha vajracaṇḍo bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tad vajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ svamukhe pratiṣṭhāpya, sarvatathāgatān bhiṣayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,74,131)
" idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvaduṣṭāgradāmakam /(STT 1,74,131)
vajradaṃṣṭrāyudhaṃ tīkṣṇam upāyaḥ karuṇātmanām " iti //(STT 1,74,131)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavakarmādhiṣṭhānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatakāyavākcittavajrabandhasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //(STT 1,75,132)
vajrasandhi //(STT 1,75,132)

athāsmin vinihṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvamudryābandhā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭvaikaghano vajrabandhavigrahaḥ prādur bhūhya pāṇau pratiṣṭhitaḥ /.(STT 1,75,133)

atha tato vajrabandhavigrahāt sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniścaritvā, sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvatathāgatamudrājñānādīni sarvabuddharddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, sarvatathāgatamahāmuṣṭisubandhatvād vajrasattvasamādheḥ sudṛḍhatvāc caikaghanaḥ sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āha //:(STT 1,7576,134)
aho hi sudṛḍhabandhaḥ samayo 'haṃ dṛḍhātmanām /(STT 1,76,134)
yat sarvāśāprasidhyarthaṃ muktānām api bandhanam //(STT 1,76,134)

atha sarvatathāgatamuṣṭimahābodhisattvakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya sarvatathāgatānāṃ pṛṭhataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā punar apy ājñāṃ mārgāyam āsa //(STT 1,76,135)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadya, sarvatathāgatadevatāsānnidhyakalpanāsarvasiddhisukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasarvajñajñānamudrādhipatyottamasiddhiphalahetos tad vajrabandhaṃ tasmai sarvatathāgatamuṣṭaye mahābodhisattvāya tathaiva pāṇibhyām anuprādāt/.(STT 1,76,136)
tataḥ sarvatathāgatair vajramuṣṭir vajramuṣṭir iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //.

atha vajramuṣṭir bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajrabandhena sarvatathāgatān bandhayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,76,137)
idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ muṣṭibandhaṃ mahādṛḍham /(STT 1,76,137)
yat sarvabuddhās tu siddhyarthaṃ samayo duratikrama iti // //(STT 1,76,137)

sarvatathāgatapūjāvidhivistarakarma mahāvīryadṛḍhakavacaḥ sarvatathāgatamahopāyaḥ sarvamudrājñānaṃ ceti/(STT 1,78,138)
sarvatathāgatamahākarmasattvāḥ //(STT 1,78,138)

atha khalv akṣobhyas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya sarvatathāgatajñānāni niṣpādya, sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ vajrapāramitāsamayodbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatavajrasamayāṃ nāma sarvatathāgatamudrāṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,78,139)
sattvavajri//(STT 1,78,139)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajraraśmayo viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,78,140)
tebhyaś ca vajraraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatavajrapāramitājñānāny āmudrya, punar apy ekaghanaḥ sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa//: (STT 1,7980,140)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ sattvavajram ahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /(STT 1,80,141)
yad dṛdhatvād akāyo vajrakāyatvam āgata iti //(STT 1,80141)

atha bhagavān ratnasaṃbhavas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ ratnapāramitāsamayasaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ vajraratnasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ svahṛdayān niśacāra //:(STT 1,80,142)
ratnavajri //(STT 1,80,142)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo ratnaraśmayo viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,80,143)
tebhyo ratnaraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatajñānāny āmudrya, punar apy ekaghanaḥ sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajraratnavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya dakṣiṇapārśve candramaṇḍalāṛito bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,80,143)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ ratnavajram ahaṃ smṛtam /(STT 1,80,144)
yan mudrāṇāṃ hi sarvāsām abhiṣekanayaṃ dṛḍham iti // //(STT 1,80,144)
atha bhagavān lokeśvararājas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya sarvatathāgatajñānamurdraṇārthaṃ dharmapāramitāsamayodbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ dharmasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ sarvahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,81,145)
dharmavajri(STT 1,81,145)

athāsyāṃ vihiḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ padmaraśmayo viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,81,146)
tebhyaḥ padmaraśmibhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatajñānāny āmudrya, punar apy ekaghanaḥ sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇo mahāvajrapadmavigrahaḥ prādurbhūya bhagavato vairocasya pṛṣṭhataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,8182,146)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ dharmavajram ahaṃ śuciḥ /(STT 1,82,147)
yat svabhāvaviśuddhyā vai rāgo 'pi hi sunirmala iti //(STT 1,82,147)

atha bhagavān amoghasiddhis tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya sarvatathāgatajñānamudraṇārthaṃ sarvapāramitāsamāyasaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayāṃ nāma svamudrāṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,82,148)
karmavajri //(STT 1,82,148)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvakarmaraśmayo viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,82,149)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatakarmaraśmibhyaḥ sa bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatajñānāny āmudrya, punar apy ekaghanaḥ sarvalokadhātusamavasaraṇapramāṇaḥ sarvatomukho mahākarmavajravigrahaḥ prādurbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya vāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,82,145)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ karmavajram ahaṃ bahu /(STT 1,82,150)
yad ekaḥ sann aśeṣasya sattvadhātoḥ sukarmakṛd iti //(STT 1,82,150)

sarvatathāgatajñānasamayā mahābhiṣekā vajradharmatā sarva pūjā ceti /(STT 1,83,151)
sarvatathāgatamahāpāramitāḥ //(STT 1,83,151)

atha bhagavān vairocanaḥ punar api sarvatathāgataratipūjāsamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulumahādevīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,83,152)
vajralāsye //(STT 1,84,152)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajramudrā viniḥsṛtāḥ /.(STT 1,84,153)
tebhyo vajramudrāmukhebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgtavigrahā bhūtvā, punar apy ekaghanā vajralāsyā mahādevī vajrasattvasadṛśātmabhāvā vicitravarṇarūpaliṅgeryāpathā sarvālaṃkāravibhūṣitā sarvatathāgatakulasaṃgrahabhūtā vajrasattvadayitā saṃbhūya, bhagavato 'kṣobhyamaṇḍalavāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,84,153)

aho na sadṛśī me 'sti pūjā hy anyā svayaṃbhuvām /(STT 1,84,154)
yat kāmaratipūjābhiḥ sarvapūjā pravartata iti // //(STT 1,84,154)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgataratnamālābhiṣekasamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,86,155)
vajramāle //(STT 1,86,155)

athāsyāṃ vihiṣṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo mahāratnamudrā vihiṣṛtāḥ /. (STT 1,86,156)
tebhyo mahāratnamudrābhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punar apy eka^ghanā vajramālā mahādevī tathaiva saṃbhūya, bhagavato ratnasaṃbhavamaṇḍalavāmapārśve pūrṇacandramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //: (STT 1,86,156)

aho hy asadṛśā 'haṃ vai ratnapūjeti kīrtitā /(STT 1,86,157)
yat traidhātukarājyāgryaṃ śāsayanti prapūjitā iti //(STT 1,86,157)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatasaṃgītisamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,88,158)
vajragīte //(STT 1,88,158)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmamudrā viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,88,159)
tebhyāś ca sarvatathāgatadharmamudrābhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punar apy ekaghanā vajragītā mahādevī saṃbhūya, bhagavato lokeśvararājamaṇḍalavāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,88,159)

aho hi saṃgītimayī pūjā 'haṃ sarvadarśinām /(STT 1,88,160)
yat toṣayanti pūjābhiḥ pratiśrutkopameṣv apīti //(STT 1,88,160)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatanṛtyapūjāsamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatakulamahādevīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,88,161)
vajranṛtye //(STT 1,88,161)

athāsyāṃ viniṣṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatanṛtyapūjāvidhivistarā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /. (STT 1,88,162)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatasarvanṛttapūjāvidhivistarebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā bhūtvā, punar apy ekaghanā vajranṛttamahādevī saṃbhūya, bhagavato 'moghasiddhes tathāgatasya maṇḍalavāmapārśve pūrṇacandramaṇḍalāśritābhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,8889,162)

aho hy udārapūjā 'haṃ sarvapūjārthakāriṇām /(STT 1,89,163)
yad vajranṛttavidhinā buddhapūjā prakalpyata iti //(STT 1,89,163)

sarvatathāgatānuttarasukhasaumanasyasamayā sarvatathāgatamālā sarvatathāgatagāthā sarvatathāgatānuttarapūjākarmakarī ceti /(STT 1,89,164)
sarvatathāgataguhyapūjāḥ // //(STT 1,89,164)

atha punar api bhagavān akṣobhyas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya pūjāpratipūjārthaṃ sarvatathāgataprahlādanīsamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatagaṇikāṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,90,165)
vajradhūpe //(STT 1,90,165)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharo 'nekavidhā dhūpapūjāmeghavyūhaḥ sarvavajradhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritāḥ. (STT 1,90,166)
tebhyaś ca dhūpapūjāmeghasamudrebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥdhūpadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya koṇe vāmapārśve candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayati sma//(STT 1,90,166)

aho hy ahaṃ mahāpūjā prahlādanavatī śubhā /(STT 1,90,167)
yat sattvāveśayogād dhi kṣipraṃ bodhir avāpyata iti //(STT 1,90,167)

atha bhagavān ratnasaṃbhavas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya pūjāpratipūjārthaṃ ratnābharaṇapūjāsamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatapratīhārīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,91,168)
vajrapuṣpe //(STT 1,91,168)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvapuṣpapūjāvyūhāḥ sarvākāśadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ. (STT 1,91,169)
tebhyaś ca sarvapuṣpapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrapuṣpadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,91,169)

aho hi puṣpapūjā 'haṃ sarvālaṃkārakārikā /(STT 1,91,170)
yat tathāgataratnatvaṃ pūjya kṣipram avāpyata iti //(STT 1,92,170)

atha bhagavān lokeśvararājas tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya pūjāpratipūjārthaṃ sarvatathāgatālokapūjāsamayodbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgatadhūtīṃ svahṛdayān niścacāraḥ //:(STT 1,92,171)
vajrāloke //(STT 1,92,171)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ savālokapūjāvyūhaḥ sakaladharmadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,92,172)
tebhyaś ca sarvālokapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrālokadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,92,172)
aho hy ahaṃ mahodārā pūjā dīpamayī śubhā /(STT 1,92,173)
yad ālokavatī kṣipraṃ sarvabuddhadṛśo labhed iti //(STT 1,92,173)

atha bhagavān amoghasiddhis tathāgato bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya pūjāpratipūjārthaṃ sarvatathāgatagandhapūjāsamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ sarvatathāgataceṭīṃ svahṛdayāṇ niścacāra //:(STT 1,93,174)
vajragandhe //(STT 1,93,174)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ lokadhātuspharaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /.(STT 1,93,175)
tebhyaś ca gandhapūjāvyūhebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajragandhadevatākāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vāmakoṇe candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,93,175)

aho gandhamayī pūjādivyā 'haṃ hi manoramā /(STT 1,93,176)
yat tathāgatagandhaṃ vai sarvakāye dadāti hīti //(STT 1,93,176)

sarvatathāgatajñānāveśā mahābodhyaṅgasaṃcayā sarvatathāgatadharmālokā śīlasamādhipurajñāvimuktivikutijñānadarśanagandhā ceti /(STT 1,94,177)
sarvatathāgatājñākāryaḥ // //(STT 1,94,177)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ punar api sarvatathāgatasamayāṅkuśasamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇapatiṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,94,178)
vajrāṅkuśa //(STT 1,94,178)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ gaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /.(STT 1,95,179)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrāṅkuśamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya vajradvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatasamayān ākarṣayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,95,179)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ samākarṣam aham dṛḍhaḥ /(STT 1,95,180)
yan mayā hi samākṛṣṭā bhajante sarvamaṇḍalam iti //(STT 1,95,180)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamahāsattvasamayasaṃbhavavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatamudrāpraveśapratīhāraṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,96,181)
vajrapāśa //(STT 1,96,181)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritāḥ /.(STT 1,96,182)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatasamayapraveśamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrapāśamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya ratnadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatān praveśayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,9697,182)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrapāśam ahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /(STT 1,97,183)
yat sarvāṇupraviṣṭāpi praveśyante mayā punar iti //(STT 1,97,183)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatasamayasphoṭamahāsattvasamayodbhavasattvavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatasamayabandhaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatadūtaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,98,184)
vajrasphoṭa //(STT 1,98,184)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayabandhamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtāḥ /.(STT 1,98,185)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatasamayabandhasarvamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrasphoṭamahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya dharmadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatān bandhayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,98,185)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrasphoṭam ahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /
yat asrvabandhamuktānāṃ sattvārthād bandha iṣyata iti //

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatāveśamahāsattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatamudrāceṭaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,99,187)
vajrāveśa //(STT 1,99,187)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvamudrāgaṇā bhūtvā viniścaritāḥ /(STT 1,99,188)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatamudrāgaṇebhyaḥ sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatavigrahā viniḥsṛtya, punar apy ekaghano vajrāveśavigrahaḥ prādur bhūya bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya karmadvāramadhye candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, sarvatathāgatān āveśayann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,99100,188)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ vajrāveśam ahaṃ dṛḍhaḥ /(STT 1,100,189)
yat sarvapatayo bhūtvā ceṭā api bhavanti hīti //(STT 1,100,189)

sarvatathāgatasamākarṣaṇaṃ praveśo bandho vaśīkaraṇaṃ ceti /(STT 1,100101,190)
sattvatathāgatājñākarāḥ // //(STT 1,101,191)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamājādhiṣṭhānāya vajrācchaṭikāsaṃjñām akārṣīt /.(STT 1,101,191)
idaṃ ca sarvatathāgatasamājāshiṣṭhānahṛdayam abhāṣata //:(STT 1,101102,191)
vajrasamāja //(STT 1,102,191)

atha tena kṣaralavamuhūrtena sarvatathāgatācchaṭikāsaṃjñāsaṃcoditāḥ sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudreṣu sarvalokadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamās tathāgatāḥ sabodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāḥ samājam āpadya, yena vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgāro, yena bhagavān vairocanas, tenopajagmuḥ /.(STT 1,102,192)
upetya oṃ sarvatathāgatapādavandanāṃ karomīty (STT 1,102,192)

anena prakṛtisiddhena mantreṇa rucijaptena sarvatathāgatapādavandanāṃ kṛtvedam udānam udānayām āsuḥ //:(STT 1,102,193)
aho samantabhadrasya bodhisattvasya satkriyā /(STT 1,102,193)
yat tathāgatacakrasya madhye bhāti tathāgataḥ //(STT 1,102,193)

athedam uktvā te daśadiksarvalokadhātusaṃnipatitāḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sabodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāḥ praviṣṭāḥ /.(STT 1,102,194)
tebhyaś ca sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ svāni svāni bodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāni viniṣṛtya bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya sarvapārśve maṇḍalībhūtvā samāpadyāvasthitā idam udānam udānayām āsuḥ //:(STT 1,102,194)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ mahaudāryam anādijam /(STT 1,102,195)
yat sarvāṇuprasaṃkhyā vai buddhā hy ekatvam āgatā iti //(STT 1,102,195)
atha bhagavataḥ arvatathāgatāḥ punar api samājam āgamyāsya vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalasyādhiṣṭhānāyāśeṣānavaśeṣasya ca sattvadhātoḥ paritrāṇasarvahitasukhāvāptyai yāvat sarvatathāgatasamatājñānābhijñābhisaṃbodhyuttamasiddhaye, bhagavantaṃ sarvatathāgatādhipatiṃ svavajrasattvam anādinidhanaṃ mahāvajradharam anena nāmāṣṭaśatenādhyeṣitavantaḥ //:(STT 1,104,196)

vajrasattva mahāsattva vajra sarvatathāgata /(STT 1,104,197)
samantabhadra vajrādya vajrapāṇe namo 'stu te //(STT 1,104,197)
vajrarāja subuddhāgrya vajrāṅkuśa tathāgata /(STT 1,104,197)
amogharāja vajrāgrya vajrākarṣa namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,197)
vajrarāga mahāsaukhya vajravāṇa vaśaṃkāra /(STT 1,105,197)
mārakāma mahāvajra vajracāpa namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,197)
vajrasādho susattvāgrya vajratuṣṭi mahārate /(STT 1,105,197)
prāmodyarāja vajrāgrya vajraharṣa namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,197)

vajraratna suvajrārtha vajrākāśa mahāmaṇe /(STT 1,105,198)
ākāśagarbha vajrāḍhya vajragarbha namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,198)
vajrateja mahājvāla vajrasūrya jinaprabha /(STT 1,105,198)
vajraraśmi mahāteja vajraprabha namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,198)
vajraketu susarvārtha vajradhvaja sutoṣaka /(STT 1,105,198)
ratnaketo mahāvajra vajrayaṣṭe namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,198)
vajrahāsa mahāhāsa vajrasmita mahādbhuta /(STT 1,105,198)
prītiprāmodya vajrāgrya vajraprīte namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,198)

vajradharma sutattvārtha vajrapadma suśodhaka /(STT 1,105,199)
lokeśvara suvajrākṣa vajranetra namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105,199)
vajratīkṣṇa mahāyāna vajrakośa mahāyudha /(STT 1,105,199)
mañju.śrī vajragāṃbhīrya vajrabuddhe namo 'stu te //(STT 1,105106,199)
vajrahetu mahāmaṇḍa vajracakra mahānaya /(STT 1,106,199)
supravartana vajrottha vajramaṇḍa namo 'stu te //(STT 1,106,199)
vajrabhāṣa suvidyāgra vajrajāpa susiddhida /(STT 1,106,199)
avāca vajrasiddhyagra vajravāca namo 'stu te //(STT 1,106,199)

vajrakarma suvajrājña karmavajra susarvaga /(STT 1,106,200)
vajrāmogha mahaudārya vajraviśva namo 'stu te //(STT 1,106,200)
vajrarakṣa mahādhairya vajravarma mahādṛḍha /(STT 1,106,200)
duryodhana suvīryāgrya vajravīrya namo 'stu te //(STT 1,106,200)
vajrayakṣa mahopāya vajradaṃṣṭra mahābhaya /(STT 1,106,200)
mārapramardi vajrogra vajracaṇḍa namo 'stu te //(STT 1,106,200)

yaḥ kaścid dhārayen nāmnām idaṃ te 'ṣṭaśataṃ śivam /(STT 1,106,201)
vajranāmābhiṣekādyaiḥ sarvāgraiḥ so 'bhiṣicyate //(STT 1,106,201)
yas tu gauṇam idaṃ nāmnāṃ mahāvajradharasya tu /(STT 1,106,201)
śaśvad gāyan stuyāt so 'pi bhaved vajradharopamaḥ //(STT 1,106107,201)
anenābhiṣṭuto 'smābhir nāmnām aṣṭaśatena tu /(STT 1,107,201)
mahāyānābhisamayaṃ visphāraya mahānayaṃ //(STT 1,107,201)
adhyeṣayāmas tvāṃ nātha bhāṣasva paramaṃ vidhim /(STT 1,107,201)
sarvabuddhamahācakraṃ mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam iti //(STT 1,107,201)

atha bhagavān vajradharaḥ sarvatathāgatādhyeṣaṇavacanam upaśrutya, sarvatathāgatasamayasaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ vajradhātuṃ nāma mahāmaṇḍalam udājahāra //:(STT 1,110,202)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,110,203)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ vajradhātur iti smṛtam //(STT 1,110,203)
upaviśya yathānyāyaṃ maṇḍalasya tu madhyataḥ /(STT 1,110,203)
mahāsattvamahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan samadhiṣṭhya ca //(STT 1,110,203)
tathaivotthāya mudrāsthaḥ sarvato vyavalokayan /(STT 1,110,203)
parikramena garveṇa vajrasattvam udāharan //(STT 1,110,203)
navena suniyuktena supramāṇena cāruṇā /(STT 1,110,203)
sūtreṇa sūtrayet prājño yathāśaktyā sumaṇḍalam //(STT 1,110,203)

caturaśraṃ caturdvāraṃ catustoraṇaśobhitam /(STT 1,110,204)
catuḥsūtrasamāyuktaṃ paṭṭasragdāmabhūṣitam //(STT 1,110,204)
koṇabhāgeṣu sarveṣu dvāraniryūhasandhiṣu /(STT 1,111,204)
khacitaṃ vajraratnais tu sūtrayed bāhyamaṇḍalam //(STT 1,111,204)
tasya cakraprtīkāśaṃ praviśyābhyantaraṃ puram /(STT 1,111,204)
vajrasūtraparikṣiptam aṣṭastambhopaśobhitam //(STT 1,111,204)
vajrastambhāgrasaṃsthendupañcamaṇḍalamaṇḍitam /(STT 1,111,204)
madhyamaṇḍalamadhye tu buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet //(STT 1,111,204)

buddhasya sarvapārśveṣu maṇḍalānāṃ tu madhyataḥ /(STT 1,111,205)
samayāgryaś catasro hi saṃlikhed anupūrvaśaḥ //(STT 1,111,205)
vajravegena cākramya maṇḍalānāṃ catuṣṭaye /(STT 1,111,205)
akṣobhyādyāṃs tu caturaḥ sarvabuddhān niveśayet //(STT 1,111,205)
akṣobhyamaṇḍalaṃ kuryāt samaṃ vajradhārādibhiḥ /(STT 1,111,205)
vajragarbhādibhiḥ pūrṇaṃ ratnasaṃbhavamaṇḍalam //(STT 1,111,205)
vajranetrādibhiḥ śuddhaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tv amitāyuṣaḥ /(STT 1,111,205)
amoghasiddheḥ saṃlekhyaṃ vajraviśvādimaṇḍalam iti //(STT 1,111,205)

cakrasya koṇasaṃstheṣu vajradevyaḥ samālikhet /(STT 1,111,206)
bāhyamaṇḍalakoṇeṣu buddhapūjāḥ samālikhet //(STT 1,111,206)
dvāramadhyeṣu sarveṣu dvārpālacatuṣṭayam /(STT 1,112,206)
bāhyamaṇḍalasaṃstheṣu mahāsattvān niveśayet //(STT 1,112,206)

tato vai samayāgrīṃ tu mudrāṃ baddhvā yathāvidhi /(STT 1,114,207)
vajrācāryaḥ praviṣṭvā tu sphoṭya mudrāṃ samāviśet //(STT 1,114,207)
tatredaṃ sarvāveśahṛdayaṃ bhavet //: aḥ //(STT 1,114,207)
ājñāṃ mārgya yathāvat tu svādhiṣṭhānādikaṃ tathā /(STT 1,114,207)
kṛtvoccarya svaṃ nāma tato vajreṇa sādhayet //(STT 1,114,207)

sattvavajrāṅkuśīṃ baddhvā vajrācāryas tataḥ punaḥ /(STT 1,114,208)
kurvann acchaṭasaṃghātaṃ sarvabuddhān samājayet //(STT 1,114,208)
tat kṣaṇaṃ sarvabuddhās tu vajrasattvasamanvitāḥ /(STT 1,114,208)
sarvamaṇḍalasaṃpūrṇāḥ samājaṃ yānti maṇḍale //(STT 1,114,208)
tataḥ śīghraṃ mahāmudrāṃ bhāvya vajradharasya tu /(STT 1,114,208)
uccārayet sakṛdvāraṃ nāmāṣṭaśatam uttamam //(STT 1,114,208)
tatas tuṣṭāḥ samājena dṛḍhaṃ yānti tathāgatāḥ /(STT 1,114,208)
vajrasattvaḥ svayaṃ siddho mitratvenopatiṣṭhati //(STT 1,114,208)

tato dvāreṣu sarveṣu karma kṛtvāṅkuśādibhiḥ /(STT 1,114,209)
mahākarmāgryamudrābhiḥ samayāṃs tu niveśayet //(STT 1,114,209)
mudrābhiḥ samayāgryābhiḥ sattvavajrādibhis tathā /(STT 1,115,209)
sādhyeta mahāsattvāñ jaḥ hūṃ vaṃ hoḥ pravartayan //(STT 1,115,209)
tato buddhādayaḥ sarve mahāsattvāḥ samājataḥ /(STT 1,115,209)
ākṛṣṭāḥ supraviṣṭāś ca baddhā yasyanti tadvaśam //(STT 1,115,209)
tatas tu guhyapūjābhiḥ saṃtoṣya sa mahātmanām /(STT 1,115,209)
vijñāpet sarvasattvārthaṃ kurudhvaṃ sarvasiddhaya iti //(STT 1,115,209)
evaṃ sarvamaṇḍaleṣu vajrācāryakarmeti //(STT 1,115,209)

athātra vajradhātumahāmaṇḍale vajraśiṣyapraveśādividhivistaro bhavati /.(STT 1,119,210)
tatra prathamaṃ tāvat praveśo bhavaty aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvahitasukhottamasiddhikāryakaraṇatayā /.(STT 1,119,210)
atra mahāmaṇḍalapraveśe pātrāpātraparīkṣā na kāryā. (STT 1,119,210)
tat kasmād dhetoḥ:(STT 1,119,210)

santi, bhagavantas tathāgatāḥ, kecit sattvā mahāpāpakāriṇas, ta idaṃ vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalaṃ dṛṣṭvā praviṣṭvā ca, sarvāpāyavigatā bhaviṣyanti /.(STT 1,119,211)
santi ca, bhagavantaḥ, sattvāḥ sarvārthabhojanapānakāmaguṇagṛddhāḥ, samayadviṣṭāḥ puraścaraṇādiṣv aśaktāḥ /,(STT 1,119,211)
teṣām apy atra yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā praviṣṭānāṃ sarvāśāparipūrir bhaviṣyati /.(STT 1,119,211)

santi ca, bhagavantaḥ, sattvāḥ nṛttagāyavihārapriyatayā sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayadharmatānavabodhatvād anyadevakulamaṇḍalāni praviśanti, sarvāśāparipūrisaṃgrahabhūteṣu niruttararatiprītiharṣasaṃbhavakareṣu sarvatathāgatakulamaṇḍaleṣu, śikṣāpadabhayabhītā na praviśanti /,(STT 1,119120,212)
teṣām apāyamaṇḍalapraveśapathāvasthitamukhānām ayam eva vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalapraveśo yujyate /,(STT 1,120,212)
sarvaratiprītiuttamasiddhisukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ sarvāpāyapratipraveśābhimukhapathavinivartanāya ca /.(STT 1,120,212)

santi ca punar, bhagavato, dhārmikāḥ sattvāḥ sarvatathāgataśīlasamādhiprajñottamasiddhyupāyair buddhabodhiṃ prārthayanto dhyānavimokṣādibhir bhūmibhir yatantaḥ kliśyante/,(STT 1,120,213)
teṣām atraiva vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalapraveśamātreṇaiva sarvatathāgatatvam api na durlabhaṃ, kim aṅga punar anyā siddhir iti //(STT 1,120,213)

tatrādita eva tāvat /(STT 1,121,214)
sarvatathāgatapraṇāmacatuṣṭayaṃ kārayet /(STT 1,121,214)
tad yathā /:(STT 1,121,214)
sarvaśarīreṇa vajrāñjaliprasāritena praṇamed anena mantreṇa //:(STT 1,122,214)
oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjopasthānāyātmānaṃ niryātayāmi, sarvatathāgatavajrasattvādhiṣṭhasva mām //(STT 1,122,214)

tathaiva sthito vajrāñjaliṃ hṛdi kṛtvā lalāṭena praṇamed anena mantreṇa //:(STT 1,122,215)
oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjābhiṣekātmānaṃ niryātayāmi, sarvatathāgatavajraratnābhiṣiñca mām //(STT 1,122,215)

tatas tathraivotthāya vajrāñjalibandhena śirasā mukhena praṇamed anena mantreṇa //:(STT 1,122,216)
oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjāpravartanāyātmānaṃ niryātayāmi, sarvatathāgatavajradharma pravartaya mām //(STT 1,122,216)

tatas tathaiva sthito vajrāñjaliṃ śiraso 'vatārya hṛdi kṛtvā mūrdhnā praṇamed anena mantreṇa //:(STT 1,122,217)
oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjākarmaṇa ātmānaṃ niryātayāmi, sarvatathāgatavajrakarma kuru mām //(STT 1,122,217)

tato raktavastrottarīyo raktanaktakāvacchāditamukhaḥ sattvavajrimudrāṃ bandhayed anena hṛdayena //:(STT 1,122,218)
samayas tvam //(STT 1,122,218)

tato madhyāṅgulidvayena mālāṃ granthya praveśayed anena hṛdayena //:(STT 1,122,219)
samaya hūṃ //(STT 1,122,219)

tataḥ praveśyaivaṃ vadet /:(STT 1,123,220)
adya tvaṃ sarvatathāgatakulapraviṣṭaḥ. (STT 1,123,220)
tad ahaṃ te vajrajñānam utpādayiṣyāmi, yena jñānena tvaṃ sarvatathāgatasiddhim api prāpsyasi. (STT 1,123,220)
kim utānyāḥ siddhīḥ //.(STT 1,123,220)
na ca tvayādṛṣṭamahāmaṇḍalasya vaktavyaṃ, mā te samayo vyathed iti //(STT 1,123,220)

tataḥ svayaṃ vajrācāryaḥ sattvavajrimudrām avamūrdhamukhīṃ baddhvā vajraśiṣyasya mūrdhni sthāpyaivaṃ vadet /:(STT 1,123,221)
ayaṃ te samayavajro mūrdhānaṃ sphālayed, yadi tvaṃ kasya cid brūyāt /.(STT 1,123,221)
tatas tathaiva samayamudrayodakaṃ śapathāhṛdayena sakṛt parijāpya tasmai śiṣyāya pāyayed iti /.(STT 1,123,221)

tatredaṃ śapathāhṛdayaṃ bhavati /:(STT 1,123,222)
vajrasattvaḥ svayaṃ te 'dya hṛdaye samavasthitaḥ /(STT 1,123,222)
nirbhidya tatkṣaṇaṃ yāyād yadi brūyād imaṃ nayam //(STT 1,123,222)
vajrodaka ṭhaḥ //(STT 1,123,222)

tataḥ śiṣyāya brūyāt /:(STT 1,123,223)
adyaprabhṛty ahaṃ te vajrapāṇir, yat te 'haṃ brūyām: idaṃ kuru, tat kartavyaṃ /(STT 1,123,223)
na ca tvayāham avamantavyo mā te viṣamāparihāreṇa kālakriyāṃ kṛtvā, narakapatanaṃ syād (STT 1,123124,223)
ity uktvā vaktavyaṃ (STT 1,124,223):
brūhi sarvatathāgatā adhitiṣṭhantāṃ vajrasattvo ma āviśatu //(STT 1,124,223)

tatas tvaramāṇena vajrācāryeṇa sattvavajrimudrāṃ baddhvedam uccārayitavyam //:(STT 1,125,224)
ayaṃ tat samayo vajraṃ vajrasattvam iti smṛtam /(STT 1,125,224)
āveśayatu te 'dyaiva vajrajñānam anuttaram //(STT 1,125,224)
vajrāveśa aḥ //(STT 1,125,224)

tataḥ krodhamuṣṭiṃ baddhvā sattvavajrimudrāṃ sphoṭayet. (STT 1,125,225)
mahāyānābhisamayaṃ ca vajravācā rucita uccārayed iti //(STT 1,125,225)

tataḥ samāviśaty āviṣṭamātrasya divyaṃ jñānam utpadyate /.(STT 1,125,226)
tena jñānena paracittāny avabudhyati /.(STT 1,125,226)
sarvakāryāṇi cātītānāgatavartamānāni jānāti /.(STT 1,125,226)
hṛdayaṃ cāsya dṛḍhībhavati sarvatathāgataśāsane /.(STT 1,125,226)
sarvaduḥkhāni cāsya praṇaśyanti /.(STT 1,125,226)
sarvabhayavigataś ca bhavaty avadhyaḥ sarvasattveṣu sarvatathāgatāś cādhitiṣṭhanti /.(STT 1,125,226)
sarvasiddhayaś cāsyābhimukhībhavanti /.(STT 1,125,226)
apūrvāṇi cāsyākāraṇaharṣaratiprītikarāṇi sukhāny utpadyante /.(STT 1,125,226)
taiḥ sukhaiḥ keṣāṃ cit samādhayo niṣpadyante, keṣāṃ cid dhāraṇyaḥ, keṣāṃ cit sarvāśāparipūrayo yavat keeṣāṃ cit sarvatathāgatatvam api niṣpadyata iti //(STT 1,125,226)

tatas tāṃ mudrāṃ baddhvā, svahṛdi moksayed anena hṛdayena //:(STT 1,125,227)
tiṣṭha vajra dṛḍho me bhava, śāśvato me bhava, hṛdayaṃ me 'dhitiṣṭha sarvasiddhiṃ ca me prayaccha hūṃ ha ha ha ha hoḥ //(STT 1,125,227)

tatas tāṃ mālāṃ mahāmaṇḍale kṣepaed anena hṛdayena //:(STT 1,126,228)
pratīccha vajra hoḥ //(STT 1,126,228)

tato yatra patati, so 'sya sidhyati /.(STT 1,127,229)
tatas tāṃ mālāṃ gṛhya, tasyaiva śirasi bandhayed anena hṛdayena /:(STT 1,127,229)
oṃ pratigṛhṇa tvam imaṃ sattvaṃ mahābalaḥ //(STT 1,127,229)
tayā baddhayā tena mahāsattvena pratīcchito bhavati /.(STT 1,127,229)
śīghraṃ cāsya sidhyati /.(STT 1,127,229)

tatas tathāviṣṭasyaiva mukhabandhaṃ muñced anena hṛdayena //:(STT 1,127,230)
oṃ vajrasattvaḥ svayaṃ te 'dya cakṣūdghāṭanatatparaḥ /(STT 1,127,230)
udghāṭayati sarvākṣo vajracakṣur anuttaram //(STT 1,127,230)
he vajra paśya //(STT 1,127,230)

tato mahāmaṇḍalaṃ yathānupūrvato darśayet /.(STT 1,128,231)
mahāmaṇḍale ca dṛṣṭamātre sarvatathāgatair adhiṣṭhyate. (STT 1,128,231)
vajrasattvaś cāsya hṛdaye tiṣṭhati /.(STT 1,128,231)
nānādyāni ca raśmimaṇḍaladarśanādīni prātihāryavikurvitāni paśyati /.(STT 1,128,231)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatasūkṣmavajra{atha bhagavān punar apy amogharājamahābodhisattvasamayasaṃbhavasattvādhiṣṭhānavajran nāma samādhiṃ samāpadeyaṃ}jñānamudrāsamayamaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ  samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,249,419)
oṃ sūkṣumavajrajñānasamaya hūṃ //(STT 1,249,419)
% -maṃ svavidyottamam] to be emended to -māṃ svavidyottamām following MS
% vowel ā of -māṃ is slightly illegible

atha khalv akṣobhyas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajrasattvasūkṣmasamayamaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,249,420)
oṃ vajrasattvasūkṣmajñānasamaya hūṃ //(STT 1,249,420)

atha khalu ratnasaṃbhavas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajraratnasūkṣmajñānasamayamaṇḍalādhṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,249,421)
oṃ vajraratnasūkṣmajñānasamaya hūṃ //(STT 1,249,421)

atha khalv amitāyus tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajradharmasūkṣmajñānasamayamaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,249,422)
oṃ vajradharmasūkṣmajñānasamaya hūṃ //(STT 1,249,42)

atha khalv amoghasiddhis tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajrakarmasūkṣmajñānasamayamaṇḍalādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,249,423)
oṃ vajrakarmasūkṣmajñānasamaya hūṃ //(STT 1,249,423)

atha bhagavān vairocanaḥ sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ. (STT 1,252,424)
samanantarasamāpanne ca bhagavaty, atha tāvad eva, sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sūkṣmajñānavajraraśmayo viniścaritvā, sarvalokadhātavo 'bhavāsya, sarvasattvānāṃ sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānavajrasamādhisamāpattir dṛḍhīkṛtya,(STT 1,252,424)

punar apy ekadhyībhūtvā, samādhijñānavajrakāyatām adhyālambyaikaghanas tathāgatajñānaḥ saṃbhūya, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye praviṣṭaḥ //.(STT 1,252,425)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatajñānahṛdayebhyaḥ praviṣṭvedaṃ sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānamahāsamayavajram abhāṣat //:(STT 1,252,426)
sūkṣmavajra //(STT 1,252,426)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajrapāṇir viniḥsṛtya, sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānavajrabimbam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāya, sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānavajrabimbam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāya, sarvatathāgatanāsikāgreṣu sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,252,427)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ sūkṣmavajram ahaṃ mahat /(STT 1,252,428)
yat mahattvāt sa sūkṣmo 'pi traidhātukam api sphared iti //(STT 1,253,428)

athedam uktvā bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatanāsikāgrebhyaḥ susūkṣmavajrajñānanimittaspharaṇatayā sarvatathāgatakāyebhyaḥ spharitvā, (STT 1,254,429)

sakaladharmadhātuspharaṇatāyogena sarvākāśadhātuṃ susūkṣmavajrajñānanimittaiḥ saṃspharya, sakalākāśadhātuvisphāritasarvatathāgatajñānavajrabimbam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāyāvasthitaḥ /.(STT 1,254,430)

atha tasminn eva kṣaṇe sarvatathāgatajñānavajramadhye vajradharmatām adhyālambya, sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyavasthitaḥ /.(STT 1,254,431)

atha tataḥ sarvatathāgatajñānavajrāt sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānahṛdayaṃ niścacāra //:(STT 1,254,432)
vajranābhitathāgata hūṃ //(STT 1,254,432)

athāsimin viniḥsṛtamātre, bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ punar api sūkṣmajñānapraveśayogena sarvatathāgatakāyeṣu praviṣṭvā, hṛdaye vajrabimbāni bhūtvāvasthitaḥ /.(STT 1,256,433)

atha tebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatasattvavajrebhya idaṃ mahājñānahṛdayacatuṣṭayaṃ niścacāra //:(STT 1,256,434)

vajrasattvajñānamudraḥ /(STT 1,256,435)

mahātuṣṭijñānamudraś ceti /(STT 1,256,435)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatahṛdayaḥ punar api sūkṣmajñānapraveśayogena svahṛdayaṃ praviṣṭvā, hṛdaye vajrabimbam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāyāvasthitaḥ //(STT 1,257,436)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar api sūkṣmavajrajñānapraveśayogena svahṛdayaṃ vajrahṛdayaṃ praviṣṭvā, vajrabimbam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāyāvasthitaḥ //.(STT 1,258,439)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar api, svahṛdayavajrahṛdayavajrāt, susūkṣmajñānapraveśayogena tad vajrahṛdayaṃ praviṣṭvā. (STT 1,259,443)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ punar api susūkṣmajñānanimittaspharaṇayogena sarvatathāgatakāyebhyo niṣkramya, vajrapāṇimahābodhisattvakāyaḥ saṃbhūya, punar api vajrasattvādimahābodhisattvavigrahāṇi bhūtvā, (STT 1,260,446)

svāni svāni cihnāni hṛdayeṣu pratiṣṭhāpya, vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalasanniveśayogena candramaṇḍalāny āśritya, svahṛdayasamādhayaḥ samāpadyāvasthitā iti //(STT 1,260,447)

atha vajrapāṇir punar api sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānābhijñāniṣpādanārtham idaṃ vajrasūkṣmajñānamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,260,448)

svacittaparikarmamahāmudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,262,453)

vajrakāryakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ(STT 1,277,493)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatānuttarapūjāvidhivistaraspharaṇakarmasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,277,494)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajradhātvanuttarapūjāspharaṇasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,277,494)

atha khalv akṣobhyas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajrasattvānuttarapūjāvidhivistaraspharaṇakarmasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,277,495)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajrasattvānuttarapūjāspharaṇasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,277,495)

atha khalu ratnasaṃbhavas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajraratnānuttarapūjāvidhivistaraspharaṇakarmasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,277,496)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajraratnānuttarapūjāspharaṇasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,277,496)

atha khalv amitāyus tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajradharmānuttarapūjāvidhivistaraspharaṇakarmasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,277278,497)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajradharmānuttarapūjāspharaṇasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,278,497)

atha khalv amoghasiddhis tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajrakarmānuttarapūjāvidhivistaraspharaṇakarmasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,278,498)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajrakarmānuttarapūjāspharaṇasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,278,498)

atha bhagavān vairocanaḥ punar api sarvatathāgatapūjāvidhivistarasakaladharmadhātuspharaṇakarmasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ. (STT 1,279,499)

samantasamāpanne cātha tāvad eva sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ sakaladharmadhātuspharaṇāḥ sarvākāśadhātusamavasaraṇāḥ sarvavividhapūjāvyuāhavidhivistarameghasamudrā devatāḥ saṃbhūya viniḥsṛtya (STT 1,279,500)

sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudrasarvatathāgataparṣanmaṇḍaleṣu sarvatathāgatānuttaramahābodhicittotpādana,sarvatathāgatakulārāgaṇa,samantabhadracaryāniṣpādana,mahābodhimaṇḍopasaṃkrameṇa,sarvamāradharṣaṇa, (STT 1,279,501)

sarvatathāgatasamatābhisaṃbudhyana, sarvatathāgatamahāmaṇḍalotpādana,sakalatrilokavijaya,saddharmacakrapravartanāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātvarthakaraṇādīni sarvabudharddhivikurvitāni saṃdarśayantyo 'vasthitāḥ /.(STT 1,279,502)

tāś ca pūjāmeghasamudradevatāḥ svamudrāvyagrakarayugalāḥ sarvatathāgatān vidhivat saṃpūjya, vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayām āsuḥ //:(STT 1,279280,503)
