caturmudrāmaṇḍala (=vajrasiddhimaṇḍala) vajrasattvamaṇḍala (STT 1,301,562)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahārtham idaṃ tathāgatamudrāhṛdayam abhāṣat //(STT 1,301,563)
oṃ sarvatathāgatamuṣṭi vaṃ //(STT 1,301,563)

atha khalv akṣobhyas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahārtham imāṃ sarvatathāgatamudrāṃ abhāṣat //:(STT 1,301,564)
oṃ vajrasattvamuṣṭi aḥ //(STT 1,301,564)

atha ratnasaṃbhavas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahārtham imāṃ sarvatathāgatamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,301,565)
oṃ vajraratnamuṣṭi traṃ //(STT 1,301,565)

arthāmitāyus tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahārtham imāṃ sarvatathāgatamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,3012,566)
oṃ vajradharmamuṣṭi khaṃ //(STT 1,302,566)

athāmoghasiddhis tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahārtham imāṃ sarvatathāgatamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,301,567)
oṃ vajradharmamuṣṭi hāṃ //(STT 1,302,567)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ svādhiṣṭhānena bhagavato vairocanasya tathāgatasya sarvatathāgatakulam utpādyāsya sarvatathāgatakulamahākalpavidhivistarasya sarvasiddhisaṃgrahāyedaṃ vajrasiddhiṃ nāma caturmudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,302,568)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mudrāmaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,302,569)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ vajrasiddhir iti smṛtam //(STT 1,302,569)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayeta vicakṣṇaḥ /(STT 1,302,570)
buddhabimbaṃ niveśyādau likhen mudrācatuṣṭayam //(STT 1,302,570)

candramaṇḍalamadhyeṣu vajramudrādayo likhed iti //(STT 1,303,571)

athātra vajrasiddhimudrāmaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā, tathaiva praveśyaivaṃ brūyāt /:(STT 1,303,572)
na tvayā kasya cid imaṃ rahasyapaṭalam udghāṭayitavyam //(STT 1,303,572)
tat kasya hetoḥ :(STT 1,303,572)

santi sattvā durdṛṣṭayaḥ pāpakarmāṇo hīnavīryā vai kalparahitāḥ citrakarmāṇy anabhijñās, te vajradhātvādiṣu sarvatathāgatakulamaṇḍaleṣu mahatsv iti kṛtvā, hīnavīryatayā na praviśante. (STT 1,303,573)

teṣām arthāyedaṃ vajrasiddhimudrāmaṇḍalaṃ sarvatathāgatakulamaṇḍalasamayabhūtam aśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇa, sarvahitasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatavajrottamasiddhinimittam adhiṣṭhitam iti /.(STT 1,303,574)

tat tvayaiṣāṃ sarvatathāgatakulasamayamudrārahasyānāṃ nāpratyabhiśraddhānīyaṃ, mā te narakatiryakpretopapattiḥ syād, viṣamāparihāreṇa vākalamaraṇaṃ syād (STT 1,303,575)

ity uktvā mukhabandhaṃ muktvā maṇḍalaṃ darśayet //.(STT 1,303,576)

tataḥ sarvatathāgatamudrāsamayaṃ brūyāt //(STT 1,305,577)

yāṃ yāṃ mudrāṃ tu badhanīyād yasya yasya mahātmanaḥ /(STT 1,305,578)
japaṃs tu hṛdayārthena bhāvayet taṃ svam ātmanā //(STT 1,305,578)

anena jñānayogena siddhiṃ yānti mahātmanām /(STT 1,305,579)
sarvamudrās tu sarveṣāṃ vajrapāṇir vaco yathā //(STT 1,305,579)

tataḥ sarvamudrārahasyaṃ brūyāt //(STT 1,305,580)

vidārya svendriyaṃ gṛhṇed vajramuṣṭigraheṇa tu /(STT 1,306,581)
tena mudrāṃ spṛśed yāṃ tu sā vaśaṃ yāti tat kṣaṇāt //(STT 1,306,581)

tataḥ sarvamudrādharmātāṃ brūyāt //(STT 1,306,582)

sūkṣmavajravidhiṃ yojya jñānamudrāṃ tu bandhayet /(STT 1,306,583)
anena vidhiyogena jñānamudrāṃ vaśaṃ nayet //(STT 1,306,583)

tataḥ sarvamudrākarma brūyāt //:(STT 1,306,584)

gītanṛtyarasāhāravihārādisukhāni tu /(STT 1,306,585)
niryātayaṃs tu buddhebhyaḥ karmamudrā vaśaṃ nayed iti //(STT 1,306,585)

tataḥ sarvamaṇḍalasādhikārahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,307,586)

stabdhaliṅgaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā nipadyet paṭake site /(STT 1,307,587)
liṅgaṃ caityaṃ adhiṣṭhāya vajradhātur ahaṃ svayam //(STT 1,307,587)

vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya madhyamotthasamāṅkurā /(STT 1,307,588)
kanyasāgryā mukhotthānāt samayaḥ samayāgriṇām //(STT 1,307,588)

sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa bhāvayet susamāhitaḥ /(STT 1,307,589)
maṇḍalaṃ sūkṣmavajraṃ tu samādhivaśitāṃ nayet //(STT 1,307,589)

vajramudrādvikaṃ baddhvā gṛhṇed vajraṃ tayor dṛḍham /(STT 1,307,590)
kaniṣṭhāgrā nibandhena vajrakāryāgramaṇḍala iti //(STT 1,307,590)

tato yathāvad vajrasattvamahāmudrābandhacatuṣṭayaṃ śikṣayitvā, yathāvad vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalavidhivisatara iti //(STT 1,308,591)

yathā vajrasiddhicaturmudrāmaṇḍalam evam akṣobhyādīni sarvamaṇḍalāni caturmudrāmaṇḍalayogena likhet //(STT 1,308,592)
svābhiḥ svābhir mudrābhiḥ sarvasiddhayo dadantīti /(STT 1,308,592)

evaṃ paṭakuḍyākāśasarvasthānābhilikhitāni sarvasiddhayo dadantīti //(STT 1,308,593)

maṇḍalakalpanāt prabhṛti keṣāṃ cit tasminn eva maṇḍalapraveśe siddhir yathābhirucitā,(STT 1,308309,594)

keṣāṃ cit tata ārabhya divasena, keṣāṃ cid divasacatuṣṭayena, keṣāṃ ciṭ ṣoḍaśāhāt, (STT 1,309,595)

keṣāṃ cit pañcānantaryakāri.ām api yathākāmaṃ sukhataḥ sarvakāryāṇi kurvatāṃ sarvānurāgasarvarasāhāravihārasukhāny anubhavatāṃ varṣeṇottamā siddhir bhagavatā nirdiṣṭeti // //(STT 1,309,596)

(STT 1,310,597)

atha bhagavān vairocanaḥ punar api sarvatathāgatottamasiddhisamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,310,598)
vajrasattva //(STT 1,310,598)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvo 'śeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvahitasukhasaumanasyānubhavanārthaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatasarvottamasiddhaya idaṃ mahāyānābhisamayamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,310,599)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,310,600)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ vajrasattvam iti smṛtam //(STT 1,310,600)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayed bāhyamaṇḍalam /(STT 1,310,601)
candramaṇḍalamadhye tu vajrasattvaṃ niveśayed iti //(STT 1,310,601)

tato yathāvad ākarṣaṇapraveśādiṃ kṛtvā sarvatathāgatasiddhijñānāny utpādayet //.(STT 1,311,602)

tatra prathamaṃ tāvad vaktavyam /:(STT 1,311,603)
na tvayā kasya cid adṛṣṭasamayasyaiṣāṃ rahasyānām akovidasya vaktavyam /.(STT 1,311,603)

mā te sarvāpāyopapattayo bhaveyur, viṣamāparihāreṇākālamaraṇaṃ vā syād iti //(STT 1,311,604)

tato vajrasattvottamasiddhiniṣpattijñānaṃ śiksayet //:(STT 1,312,605)

pūrṇendumaṇḍalārūḍho mahāmudrāparigrahaḥ //(STT 1,312,606)
vajrasattvaṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan sidhyate laghur iti //(STT 1,312,606)

tataḥ sarvamaṇḍalaguhyasamayajñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,312,607)

virāgasadṛśaṃ pāpam anyan nāsti tridhātuke /(STT 1,312,608)
tasmāt kāmavirāgitvaṃ na kāryaṃ bhavatā punaḥ //(STT 1,312,608)
mahāsamaya hana phaṭ //(STT 1,312,608)

tataḥ śapathahṛdayaṃ dadyād evam /:(STT 1,312,609)
sarvatathāgatakulamaṇḍaleṣu vidhivistareṣu samayasaṃvaraṃ dātavyam //.(STT 1,312,609)

(STT 1,313,610)

tato vajrasattvamahāmudrādibandhacatuṣṭayaṃ śikṣayet /.
tathāiva siddhayaḥ /(STT 1,313,611)
evaṃ paṭādiṣu sarvapratimāsu ca manīṣitavidhānena sarvasiddhayo dadanti //.(STT 1,313,611)
evaṃ yathā vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalavidhivistara iti //(STT 1,313,611)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punar api samājam āgatya, bhagavate sarvatathāgatādhipataye ed. sarvatahāgatādhipataye mahābodhicittāya vajrasattvāya mahāvajrapāṇaye vajratuṣṭyānena hṛdayena sādhukāram adaduḥ //:(STT 1,313,612)

oṃ sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /(STT 1,313,613)
vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe //(STT 1,313,613)

subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /(STT 1,313,614)
sarvatathāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham //(STT 1,313,614)

vajrasattvasya nāmāpi sarvasiddhikaraṃ param /(STT 1,313,615)
sādhyamānas tu śuddhyā vai sukhair buddhatvam ānuyāt //(STT 1,314,615)

vajradharmaprayogeṇa sarvakāmasukhaiḥ sukham /(STT 1,314,616)
sādhayej janmanīhaiva sukham akṣayam avyayam iti // //(STT 1,314,616)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ samāptaḥ // //(STT 1,314,617)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ (STT 1,315,618)
trilokavijayamahāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ (STT 1,315,618)

atha bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya, bhagavantaṃ sarvatathāgatamahācakravartinam anena nāmāṣṭaśatenādhyeṣitavantaḥ //:(STT 1,315,619)

vajrasattva mahāvajra vajranātha susādhaka /(STT 1,315,620)
vajrābhiṣeka vajrābha vajraketu namo 'stu te //(STT 1,315,620)

hāsavajra mahādharma vajrakośa mahāvara /(STT 1,315,621)
sarvamaṇḍala rājāgrya niṣprapañca namo 'tu te //(STT 1,315,621)

vajrakarma mahārakṣa caṇḍayakṣa mahāgraha /(STT 1,315316,622)
vajramuṣṭi mahāmudra sarvamudra namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,622)

bodhicitta mahābodhe buddha sarvatathāgata /(STT 1,316,623)
vajrajñāna mahājñāna mahāyāna namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,623)

sarvārtha sarvatattvārtha mahāsattvārtha sarvavit /(STT 1,316,624)
sarvajña sarvakṛt sarva sarvadarśi namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,624)

vajrātmaka suvajrāgrya vajravīrya suvajradhṛk /(STT 1,316,625)
mahāsamayatattvārtha mahāsatya namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,625)

vajrāṅkuśa mahākāma surate sumahāprabha /(STT 1,316,626)
vajraprabha prabhoddyota buddhaprabha namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,626)

vajrarājāgrya vajrāgrya vidyāgryāgrya narottama /(STT 1,316,627)
vajrottama mahāgryāgrya vidyottama namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,627)

vajradhāto mahāguhya vajraguhya vajraguhya suguhyadhṛk /(STT 1,316,628)
vajrasūkṣma mahādhyāna vajrakārya namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,628)

buddhāgrya buddhavajrāgrya buddhabodhe mahābuddha /(STT 1,316,629)
buddhajñāna mahābuddha buddhabuddha namo 'stu te //(STT 1,316,629)

buddhapūja mahāpūja sattvapūja supūjaka /(STT 1,316317,630)
mahopāya mahāsiddhe vajrasiddhi namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,630)

tathāgatamahākāya tathāgatasarasvate /(STT 1,317,631)
tathāgatamahācitta vajravajra namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,631)

buddhādhipa jinājñākṛd buddhamitra jināgraja /(STT 1,317,632)
mahāvairocana vibho śāstā śānta raudra namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,632)

tathāgata mahātattva bhūtakoṭe mahānaya /(STT 1,317,633)
sarvapāramitājñāna paramārtha namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,633)

samantabhadra caryāgrya māra mārapramardaka /(STT 1,317,634)
sarvāgrya samatājñāna sarvatraga namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,634)

buddhahuṃkāra huṃkāra vajrahuṃkāra dāmaka /(STT 1,317,635)
viśvavajrāṅga vajrogra vajrapāṇe namo 'stu te //(STT 1,317,635)

vandyaḥ pūjyaś ca mānyaś ca satkartavyas tathāgataiḥ /(STT 1,317,636)
yasmād vajradṛḍhaṃ cittaṃ vajrasattvas tvam ucyase //(STT 1,317,636)

tvadadhīnā hi saṃbodhiḥ pitā tvaṃ sarvadarśinām /(STT 1,317,637)
saṃbhūtāḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti tvām āsādya tathāgatāḥ //(STT 1,318,637)

anena stotrarājena stunuyād vai subhaktitaḥ /(STT 1,318,638)
yo gāyan stunuyāt so 'pi bhaved vajradharopamaḥ //(STT 1,318,638)

adhyeṣayāmas tvāṃ nātha sarvabuddhaviśaṃkaram /(STT 1,318,639)
sarvasattvārthakāryārtham utpādya kulaṃ svakam iti // //(STT 1,318,639)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatādhipatiḥ sarvatathāgatādhyeṣaṇavacanam upaśrutya, tad vajraṃ svahṛdi pratiṣṭhāpya, tān sarvatathāgatān āhūyaivam āha //:(STT 1,323324,640)

bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatā na pratipadyāmi //(STT 1,324,641)

sarvatathāgatāḥ prāhuḥ /:(STT 1,324,642)
ko hetuḥ //(STT 1,324,642)

vajradharaḥ prāha /:(STT 1,324,643)

santi, bhagavantaḥ, maheśvarādayo duṣṭasattvā, ye yuṣmābhir api sarvatathāgatair api na neyāḥ, teṣāṃ mayā kathaṃ pratipattavyam iti //(STT 1,324,644)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānena sarvatathāgatamahopāyajñānavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ //.(STT 1,325,645)

samanantasamāpanne cātha tāvad eva sarvatathāgatāḥ sakalākāśadhātuparamāṇurajaḥsamavasaraṇaspharaṇatayā, sumerugirimūrdhni vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgāre punar api samājaṃ āgamya, (STT 1,325,646)

sarvatathāgatasamatām adhyālambya, bhagavato vairocanasya śrīvatsahṛdaye praviṣṭāḥ //.(STT 1,325,647)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatahṛdayam ātmānam adhiṣṭhāya, sarvavajrasamatayāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇasarvahitasukhottamasiddhihetoḥ sarvaduṣṭavinayāya ca /,(STT 1,325,648)

sarvatathāgatamahākaruṇopāyasamādhijñānam adhyālambya /(STT 1,325,649)
sarvatathāgatamahākaruṇopāyakrodhasamayavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ //.(STT 1,325,649)

samanantarasamāpanne cātha tasminn eva kṣaṇe, sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ sarvatathāgatavajrasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ niścacāra //:(STT 1,325326,650)
huṃ //(STT 1,326,650)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre vajrapāṇihṛdayavajrāt sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ samantajvālāgarbhāḥ sabhrukuṭibhrūbhaṅgakuñcitalalāṭavikaṭadaṃṣṭrākarālamukhā (STT 1,326,651)

vajrāṅkuśakośapāśādivajrajvālāgnipradīptapraharaṇavyagrakarā anekavidhavarṇālaṃkāravicitraveṣadharā vajrapāṇivigrahā vinoścaritvā, (STT 1,326,652)

sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvaduṣṭavinayaṃ kṛtvā, bhagavato vairocanasya sarvato vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayinsuḥ //:(STT 1,326,653)

aho hy upāyavinayaṃ mahopāyavatām aham /(STT 1,326,654)
yat sattvopāyavinayāt krodhatvaṃ yānti nirmalā iti //(STT 1,326,654)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatāprapañcadharmatām adhyālambya, sarvatathāgatamahākrodhavajrasamayavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ sarvatathāgatavajrahuṃkāraṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ vidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,328,655)

oṃ śumbha niśumbha huṃ gṛhṇa gṛhṇa huṃ gṛhṇāpaya huṃ ānaya ho bhagavan vajra huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,328,656)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajrapāṇir viniḥsṛtya, sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudrebhyo yāvantaḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ sabodhisattvaparṣanmaṇḍalāḥ samadhiṣṭhāyākṛṣya, vajrasamayamahāmaṇḍale praveśya, samayair baddhvā, (STT 1,328329,657)

punar apy ekaghano mahāvajrakrodhakāyo bhūtvā, bhagavato vairocanasya hṛdaye sthitvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,329,658)

aho hi bodhicittasya sarvato bhadratānaghā /(STT 1,329,659)
yat sarvavinayād yāti krodho 'pi ramaṇīyatām iti //(STT 1,329,659)

atha sa mahāvajrakrodhakāyo bhagavato hṛdayād avatīrya, sarvatathāgatānāṃ purataś candramaṇḍalāśrito bhūtvā, punar apy ājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,329,660)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamayākarṣaṇavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgtasamayāṅkuśaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(STT 1,330,661)

huṃ ṭakki jjaḥ //(STT 1,330,662)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvalokadhātuprasarameghasamudreṣu, yāvantas trailokyādhipatayo maheśvarādayas, te sarve sarvalokasaṃniveśagaṇaparivṛtā aśeṣānava.eṣāḥ sarvatathāgatasamayavajrāṅkuśenākṛṣṭāḥ samānā, (STT 1,330,663)

yena sumerugirimūrdhā, yena ca vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgāras, tenopasaṃkramya, bhagavato vajramaṇiratnaśikharakūṭāgārasya sarvataḥ parivāryāvasthitā abhūvan //(STT 1,330,664)

atha vajrapāṇis tad vajraṃ svahṛdayād gṛhyollālayan sarvāvantaṃ sakalatraidhātukatrilokacakram avalokyaivam āha /:(STT 1,331,665)

pradipadyata, mārṣāḥ, sarvatathāgataśāsane, mama cājñāṃ pālayata //(STT 1,331,666)

atha ta evaṃ āhuḥ //(STT 1,331,667)
kathaṃ pratipadyāmaḥ /(STT 1,331,667)

bhagavān vajrapāṇir āha /:(STT 1,331,668)
buddhaṃ dharmaṃ ca saṃghaṃ ca śaraṇapratipattitaḥ /(STT 1,331,668)
sarvajñajñānalābhāya pratipadyadhvaṃ mārṣā iti //(STT 1,331,668)

atha yo 'smin lokadhātau sakalatrailokyādhipatir mahādevaḥ sarvatrailokyādhipatyagarvito mahākrodhatāṃ darśayann evam āha //:(STT 1,331,669)

ahaṃ, bho yakṣa, trailokyādhipatir īśvaraḥ karttādhikartā sarvabhūteśvaro devātidevo mahādevaḥ, tat katham ahaṃ yakṣājñāṃ kariṣyāmīti //(STT 1,332,670)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar api vajram ullālayann ājñāpayati /:(STT 1,332,671)
bho duṣṭasattva śīghraṃ praviśa maṇḍalam /(STT 1,332,671)
mama ca samaye tiṣṭha //(STT 1,332,671)

atha mahādevo devo bhagavantam idam avocat /:(STT 1,332,672)
ko 'yaṃ, bhagavann, īdṛśah sattvo, yo 'yam īśvarasyaivam ājñāṃ dadāti //(STT 1,332,672)

atha bhagavān sarvāvantaṃ maheśvarāditrailokyagaṇam āhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,332,673)

pratipadyata, mārṣās, triśaraṇagamanasamayasaṃvare māyaṃ vajrapāṇiyakṣaḥ krūraḥ krodhanaś caṇḍo mahābodhisattvaś ca vo dīptena vajreṇa sakalam eva traidhātukaṃ nāśayed iti //(STT 1,332,674)

atha maheśvaraḥ sakalatrailokyādhipatyatayā svajñānavaśitayā ca bhagavato vajrapāṇeḥ saṃdarśanārthaṃ mahācaṇḍakrodhatāṃ mahābhairavarūpatāṃ mahājvālotsṛjanatāṃ mahāraudrāṭṭahāsatāṃ sahagaṇaiḥ saṃdarśayann evam āha /:(STT 1,332,675)

ahaṃ, bhoḥ, sakalatrailokyādhipas, tvāṃ ma mājñāṃ dadāmīti /(STT 1,332,676)

atha vajrapāṇis tad vajraṃ sagarvam ullālayan vihasann evam āha /:(STT 1,332,677)

pratipadyasva bho kaṭapūtana mānuṣamāṃsāhāra citibhasmabhakṣyabhojyaśayyāsanaprāvaraṇa mamājñām iti //(STT 1,332,678)

atha maheśvaro mahādevaḥ sakalaṃ trailokyaṃ mahākrodhāviṣṭam adhiṣṭhāyaivam āha /:(STT 1,332,679)

tvam api mamājñāṃ pālaya samaye ca pratipadyasveti //(STT 1,332,680)

atha vajrapāṇir mahākrodharājo bhagavantam etad avocat /:(STT 1,335,681)

ayaṃ bhagavan, mahādevo devaḥ svajñānabalagarvān mahaiśvaryād ādhipatyāc ca sarvatathāgataśāsane na praṇamati /.(STT 1,335336,682)
tat katham asya kriyata iti //(STT 1,336,682)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatahṛdayasaṃbhūtaṃ mahāvajrasamayaṃ smārayati //:(STT 1,336,683)
oṃ niśumbha vajra huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,336,683)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ svavajrahṛdayam udājahāra //:(STT 1,336,684)
huṃ //(STT 1,336,684)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre sakalatraidhātukasaṃnipatitā mahādevādayaḥ sarvatrailokyādhipatayo 'dhomukhāḥ vajrapāṇeś ca śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ /.(STT 1,336,685)
sa ca mahādevo devo bhūmyāṃ prapatito niśceṣṭībhūto mṛtaḥ //(STT 1,336,685)

atha bhagavāñ jānann eva vajrapāṇim evam āha /:(STT 1,337,686)
pratipadyasva, vajrapāṇe, 'sya sakalatrilokacakrasyābhayāya mā pañcatvam āpādaya //(STT 1,337,686)

atha vajrapāṇir mahākrodharājo bhagavato vacanam upaśrutya, tān sarvadevādīn āhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,337,687)

buddhaṃ dharmaṃ ca saṃghaṃ ca śaraṇaṃ pratipadyata /(STT 1,337,688)
mamājñākāritāyāṃ ca yadīṣṭaṃ vaḥ svajīvitam iti //(STT 1,337338,688)

atha ta evam āhuḥ /:(STT 1,338,689)
saṃbuddhadharmasaṃghasamudrāñ charaṇaṃ gacchāmaḥ /(STT 1,338,689)
tvacchāsanājñāṃ na jānīma iti //(STT 1,338,689)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgatas tān āhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,338,690)

ayaṃ, bho devā, asmākaṃ sarvatathāgatādhipatiḥ sarvatathāgatapitā sarvatathāgatājñākaraḥ sarvatathāgatajyeṣṭhaputro bhagavān samantabhadro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ, sarvasattvavinayanakāryakaraṇatayā mahākrodharājyatāyām adhiṣiktaḥ /.(STT 1,338,691)

tat kasmād dhetoḥ :(STT 1,338,692)
santi yuṣmanmadhye mahādevādayo duṣṭagaṇās, te sarvatathāgatair api na śakyāḥ śānttayā pāpebhyo nivārayitum /,(STT 1,338,692)

teṣāṃ pāpasattvānāṃ nigrahāyādhiṣṭhitas, tad yuṣmābhir asya samaye sthātavyam ity ājñeti //(STT 1,338,693)

ta evam āhur :(STT 1,338,694)
asmākaṃ, bhagavann, asmāj jīvitavipralopāt paritrāyasva /(STT 1,338,694)
yām ājñāṃ dāsyati, tat kariṣyāmaha iti //(STT 1,338,694)

bhagavān āha /:(STT 1,338,695)
haṃ bho mārṣā etam eva śaraṇaṃ gacchatāyam eva vaḥ paritrāsyati, nānya iti //(STT 1,338,695)

atha te trilokasakalatraidhātukasaṃnipatitāḥ tribhuvanapatayo, yena bhagavān vajradharas, tenābhimukhā ekakaṇṭhāmahārtān svarān pramuñcanta evam āhuḥ /:(STT 1,340,696)

paritrāyasva bho bhagavan paritrāyasva bho sugata ato maraṇaduḥkhād iti //(STT 1,340,697)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvas tān devādīn āhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,340,698)

haṃ bho duṣṭāḥ pratipadyata mama śāsane mā vo 'ham anena vajreṇaikajvālīkṛtya sarvān eva bhasmīkuryām iti //(STT 1,340,699)

ta evam āhuḥ /:(STT 1,340,700)
samantabhadras tvaṃ bhagavan sarvatathāgatacittotpādaḥ śāntasuvinītaḥ sarvasattvahitaiṣī sarvasattvābhayapradaḥ /(STT 1,340,700)
tat kathaṃ, bhagavann, asmākaṃ nirdahiṣyaiti //(STT 1,340,700)

atha vajrapāṇir mahākrodharājas tān evam āha /:(STT 1,341,701)

tenaivāhaṃ mārṣāḥ samantabhadro, yena sarvatathāgatājñākāritvād yuṣmadvidhānaṃ duṣṭasattvajātīyānāṃ pāpacittānāṃ saṃśodhanārthāya vināśayāmi, yadi matsamaye na tiṣṭha iti //(STT 1,341,702)

te prāhur evam astv iti //(STT 1,341,703)

atha vajrapāṇir mahākrodharājo maheśvaraṃ muktvā 'nyadevān āśvāsyotthāpanārtham idaṃ vajrottiṣṭhaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,342,704)
vajrottiṣṭha //(STT 1,342,704)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre maheśvaraṃ muktvā, sarve te tridhātukasaṃnipatitās tribhuvanapatayaḥ saparivārāḥ saṃmūrchitāḥ samānāḥ samāśvastahṛdayā abhūvan //(STT 1,342,705)

divyāni sukhāny anubhavato vigatabhayacchambhitaromaharṣā bhagavantaṃ vajrapāṇim avalokayantaḥ samutthitā iti //(STT 1,342,706)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇiṃ bodhisattvam āmantrayām āsa /:(STT 1,343,707)
ayaṃ, mahāsattva, mahādevo devādhipatir notthāpitaḥ. (STT 1,343,707)
tat kim asya jīvitavipraṇāśena kṛtena (STT 1,343,707)
jīvāpayainam satpuruṣo 'yaṃ bhaviṣaytīti //(STT 1,343,707)

atha vajrapāṇir evam astv iti kṛtvedaṃ mṛtasaṃjīvanahṛdayam udājahāra //:(STT 1,343,708)
vajrāyuḥ //(STT 1,343,708)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre mahādevo devo mṛtaḥ saṃjīvyotthātum icchati, na śaknoty utthātum /.(STT 1,343,709)
tato bhagavantam etad avocat /:(STT 1,343,709)
kiṃ ahaṃ bhagavataivaṃ śāsyāmi /(STT 1,343,709)

bhagavān āha /:(STT 1,343,710)
na tvaṃ pratipdyasy asya mahāsatpuruṣasyājñāṃ kartum /.(STT 1,343,710)
ayam eva te 'nuśāsti nāham //(STT 1,343,710)

maheśavraḥ prāha /(STT 1,343,711)
kiṃ na tvaṃ, bhagavañ, chokto 'smād duṣṭasattvāt paritrātum iti //(STT 1,343,711)

bhagavān āha /:(STT 1,343,712)
nāham asmāt samarthaḥ paritrātum //(STT 1,343,712)

maheśvara āha /:(STT 1,343,713)
tat kasmād dhetor (STT 1,343,713)

bhagavān āha :(STT 1,343,714)
sarvatathāgatādhipatitvāt /(STT 1,343,714)

maheśvara āha :(STT 1,344,715)
nāhaṃ, bhagavan, bhagavato bhāṣitasyārtham ājñe. kiṃ tu yatra hi nāma tathāgatānām api sarvatridhātukādhipatīnām anyo 'dhipatis, taṃ na jāne, ko 'yam iti //(STT 1,344,715)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar api mahādevam āhūyaivam āha /:(STT 1,344,716)

na pratipadyasi, duṣṭasattva, mamājñāṃ kartum iti //(STT 1,344,717)

atha mahādevo vajrasattvavacanam upaśrutya, kupitaś caṇḍībhūtas tathāpatita eva punar api mahāraudrarūpatāṃ darśayann evam āha /:(STT 1,345,718)

maraṇam apy utsahāmi, na ca tavājñāṃ kariṣyāmīti //(STT 1,345,719)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvo mahākopatāṃ saṃdarśayan, svakramatalād idaṃ vajrānucaraṃ niścacāra /:(STT 1,345,720)
oṃ ed. om pādākarṣaṇavajra hūṃ //(STT 1,345,720)

atha bhagavantaś caraṇatalāt samantajvālāgarbhaḥ kṛtabhrukuṭidaṃṣṭrākarālamahāvaktro vajrānucaro viniḥsṛtya orviniścaritvā ? vajrapāṇeḥ punataḥ sthitvājñāṃ mārgayām āsa //(STT 1,345,721)

atha vajrapāṇir maheśvarasaṃśodhananimittam evam āha /:(STT 1,345,722)

buddhasya krodhasamayān yathāvat tu likhed buddhaḥ //(STT 1,423,998)

vajravegena niṣkramya vajrapāṇes tu maṇḍalam /(STT 1,424,999)
tatra madhye likhet tiryakśūle vajraṃ pratiṣṭhitam //(STT 1,424,999)

jvālāmadhye likhet tasya yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /(STT 1,424,1000)
vajraṃ vajrāṅkuśaṃ caiva vāṇaṃ  tuṣṭiṃ tathaiva ca //(STT 1,424,1000)

vajravegena cākramya dvitīyaṃ maṇḍalottamam /(STT 1,424,1001)
vajraratnaṃ likhec caiva cakramadhye pratiṣṭhitam //(STT 1,424,1001)

vajraṃ bhṛkuṭimadhye tu vajraṃ sūrye tathā dhvajam /(STT 1,424,1002)
dantapaṅkutiṃ tathā vajre tasya pārśveṣu saṃlikhet //(STT 1,424,1002)

vajravegena cākramya tṛtīyaṃ manḍalottamam /(STT 1,424,1003)
vajrapadmaṃ likhed divyaṃ padmamadhye pratiṣṭḥitam //(STT 1,424,1003)

jvālāmadhye likhet padmaṃ khaḍgaṃ cakraṃ tathaiva ca /(STT 1,424425,1004)
vajrajihvāṃ yathāvat tu tasya pārśveṣu sarvadā //(STT 1,425,1004)

vajravegena cākramya caturthaṃ maṇḍalottamam /(STT 1,425,1005)
triyagvajre likhed vajraṃ vṛtaṃ vajrair mahāprabhaiḥ //(STT 1,425,1005)

tasyāḥ pārśveṣu sarveṣu sarvajvālākulaprabhāḥ /(STT 1,425,1006)
sarvavajraṃ sukavacaṃ vajradaṃṣṭrāṃ sumuṣṭi ceti //(STT 1,425,1006)

koṇeṣu bāhyasaṃstheṣu yathāvat tu likhen nayam /(STT 1,425,1007)
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mudrāvidyāḥ samāsataḥ //(STT 1,425,1007)

jhiḥ //(STT 1,426,1008)
oṃ vajrakrodhasamaye jhiḥ //(STT 1,426,1008)
oṃ vajraroṣāṅkuśy ānaya sarvaṃ jhiḥ //(STT 1,426,1008)
oṃ vajraroṣe kāmavajriṇi vaśaṃ ma ānaya jhiḥ //(STT 1,426,1008)
oṃ vajratuṣṭikrodhe toṣaya sarvān jhiḥ //(STT 1,426,1008)

vajrajhiḥkāramaṇḍale //(STT 1,426,1009)

jiḥ //(STT 1,426,1010)
oṃ vajrabhṛkuṭikrodhe hara sarvārthān jiḥ //(STT 1,426,1010)

oṃ vajradhvajāgrakeyūramahākrodhe dehi me sarvārthaṃ jiḥ //(STT 1,426,1011)
oṃ vajrāṭṭahāsini hasa hasāṭṭāṭṭahāsena māraya jiḥ //(STT 1,426,1011)

vajrajiḥkāramaṇḍale //(STT 1,426,1012)

diḥ //(STT 1,426,1013)

vajradiḥkāramaṇḍale //(STT 1,426,1015)

oṃ vajrakrodhamuṣṭi bandha hniḥ //(STT 1,427,1017)

vajrahniḥkāramaṇḍale //(STT 1,427,1018)

athāsmin vajrakulaguhyamaṇḍale praveśavidhivistaro bhavati //:(STT 1,430,1022)

tatrādita eva tāvat trilokavijayamahāmaṇḍalapraveśavidhinā praviśya, vajraṃ gṛhya, vajrakulasamayamudrāpratimudropamudrājñānamudrābhiḥ vajradharapūjārthaṃ nṛtyopahāraḥ kartavya iti //(STT 1,430,1023)

tatredaṃ nṛtyapratinṛtyopanṛtyajñānanṛtyopahāramudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:(STT 1,430,1024)

tatrādita eva vajradhātusaṃgrahahṛdayaṃ vajragītena gāyan, sarvatathāgatānāṃ sotropahāraṃ kṛtvā, vajrācāryeṇa sattvavajrimudrā sphoṭayitavyā /(STT 1,430,1025)
tato yathā praviṣṭān mudrābhiḥ samāviśanti //(STT 1,430,1025)

vajranṛtyaprayogeṇa vajrakrodhāṅgulidvayam /(STT 1,431,1026)

parivartya tathā caiva vāmavajrapratiṣṭhiteti //(STT 1,438,1051)

vajrabandhaṃ tale kṛtvā cchādayet kruddhamānasaḥ /(STT 1,438,1052)

atha vajrakulaguhyasamayamudrābandho bhavati //:(STT 1,439,1057)

(vajrakuladharmajñānasamayamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ)(STT 1,444,1067)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatavajrakulasamādhijñānamudrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,444,1068)

oṃ sūkṣmavajrakrodhākrama hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,444,1069)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imaṃ trilokavijayasūkṣmavajravidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,444,1070)
oṃ sūkṣmavajrakrodhākrama hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,444,1070)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva imaṃ trilokavijayasūkṣmavajravidyottamam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,444,1072)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar api svakulam utpādya, vajradhātumahāmaṇdalayogena saṃniveśyaitāni svahṛdayāny abhāṣat //:(STT 1,445,1073)

oṃ vajrasattvasūkṣmajñānakrodha hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,445,1074)

oṃ sūkṣmavajrakrodhamahācakra cchinda pātaya śiraḥ praviśya hṛdayaṃ bhinda hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,446,1079)

oṃ sūkṣmavajrayakṣakrodha hana bhakṣaya sarvaduṣṭān cintitamātreṇa vajradaṃṣṭra hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,447,1081)
oṃ sūkṣmavajramuṣṭikrodha bandha bandha hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,447,1081)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar apīdaṃ vajrakulasūkṣmajñānasamayamaṇḍalam udājahāra //:(STT 1,448,1082)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dharmamaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,448,1083)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ krodhajñānam iti smṛtam //(STT 1,448,1083)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /(STT 1,448,1084)
tasya madhye likhed buddhaṃ jñānavajrasya madhyagam //(STT 1,448,1084)

buddhasya sarvapārśveṣu mudrās tā eva saṃlikhet /(STT 1,448,1085)

trilokavijayādyāṃs tu yathāvat tu niveśayet /(STT 1,448,1086)

tatrādita eva tāvat praveśya brūyād :(STT 1,449,1087)

adya tvaṃ sarvatathāgatavajrakrodhatāyāṃ vajrapāṇinā bhagavatā niṣicyase /.(STT 1,449,1088)
tat sādhu pratipadyasvāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuparitrāṇaṃ yāvat sarvatathāgatahitasukhottamasiddhyavāptiphalahetor vajrakrodhaḥ sarvasattvān api saṃśodhananimittaṃ mārayituṃ kaḥ punar vādaḥ sarvaduṣṭān iti //(STT 1,449,1088)

idam uktvā mukhabandhaṃ muñcet //(STT 1,449,1089)
tataḥ sarvamaṇḍalaṃ darśayitvā, vajraṃ or tad vajraṃ yathāvat pāṇau dattvā, (STT 1,449,1089)

tato vajrakrodhasūkṣmajñānāni śikṣayet //:(STT 1,450,1090)
sūkṣmavajraṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya vajrahuṃkārayogataḥ /(STT 1,450,1090)
huṃkāraṃ yojayed yasya tasya naśyati jīvitam //(STT 1,450,1090)

sūkṣmavajraṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya spharayeta yathāvidhi /(STT 1,450,1091)
yāvantaṃ spharate taṃ tu tāvan naśyaty asau ripuḥ //(STT 1,450,1091)

sūkṣmavajravidhiṃ yojya vajrahuṃkārayogataḥ /(STT 1,450,1092)
spharayet krodhavān yāvat tāvat sarvān vināśayet //(STT 1,450,1092)

tathaiva saṃharet saṃ tu yāvad iccheta yogavān /(STT 1,450,1093)
sarvaṃ vāpi hi niḥśeṣaṃ punar dadyāt tu jīvitam iti //(STT 1,450,1093)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,450,1094)
huṃ //(STT 1,450,1094)
huṃ nāśaya vajra //(STT 1,450,1094)
huṃ vināśaya sarvān vajra //(STT 1,450,1094)
oṃ sūkṣmavajra pratyānaya śīghraṃ huṃ //(STT 1,451,1094)

vairaṃ tu yasya sattvasya sahabhūtvā mahādṛḍham /(STT 1,451,1095)
maitrīspharaṇatāyogāt spharan vaireṇa nāśayet //(STT 1,451452,1095)

vajraspharaṇatāyogāt kāruṇyaṃ yasya kasya cit /(STT 1,452,1096)
tena kāruṇyayogena sarvaduṣṭān sa nāśayet //(STT 1,452,1096)

adharmā yadi vā dharmā prakṛtyā tu prabhāsvarāḥ /(STT 1,452,1097)
evaṃ tu bhāvayan sattvān hūṃkāreṇa tu nāśayet //(STT 1,452,1097)

durdurūṭā hi ye sattvā buddhabodhāv abhājanāḥ /(STT 1,452,1098)
teṣāṃ tu śodhanārthāya hūṃkāreṇa tu nāśayet //(STT 1,452,1098)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,452,1099)
vairavajrakordha huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,452,1099)
karuṇāvajrakrodha huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,452,1099)
huṃ viśuddhakrodhavajra huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,452,1099)
huṃ viśodhanavajrakrodhā huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,451,1099)

vajrabimbaṃ samālikhya manasā yasya kasya cit /(STT 1,453,1100)
pātayed gṛhamadhye tu tasya tan naśyate kulam //(STT 1,453,1100)

tathaiva sūkṣmavidhānena hṛdvajraṃ paribhāvayet /(STT 1,453,1101)
bodhisattvamahābimbaṃ pātayan nāśayet kulam //(STT 1,453,1101)

vajrapāṇimahābimbaṃ sādhayan yatra pātayet /(STT 1,453,1102)
tad rājyaṃ vividhair doṣai rājñaiva saha naśyati //(STT 1,453,1102)

sarvākāravaropetaṃ buddhabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /(STT 1,453,1103)
pātayed yatra rājye tu tad rājyaṃ naśyate dhruvam iti //(STT 1,453,1103)

tatraitāni hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,454,1104)
hūṃ vajraprapāta //(STT 1,454,1104)
hūṃ bodhisattvaprapāta //(STT 1,454,1104)
hūṃ vajradharaprapāta //(STT 1,454,1104)
hūṃ buddhaprapāta //(STT 1,454,1104)

sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa candrabimbaṃ svam ātmanā /(STT 1,454,1105)
bhāvayan svayam ātmānaṃ pated yatra patet sa tu //(STT 1,454,1105)

candre vajraṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /(STT 1,454,1106)
pated yatra susaṃkruddhas tat kulaṃ patati kṣaṇāt //(STT 1,454,1106)

vajrapāṇiṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /(STT 1,454,1107)
pated yatra hi taṃ deśam acirād vipraṇaṅkṣayate //(STT 1,454455,1107)

buddhabimbaṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /(STT 1,455,1108)
pated yatra tu tad rājyam acireṇaiva naśyatīti //(STT 1,455,1108)

tatraitāni hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,455,1109)
bodhyagra prapātaya huṃ (STT 1,455,1109)
sattvavajraprapātaya huṃ //(STT 1,455,1109)
vajrasattva prapātaya huṃ //(STT 1,455,1109)
buddha prapātaya huṃ //(STT 1,455,1109)

tato vajrakuladharmarahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,455,1110)
vajrakrodhasamāpattyā svakāyaṃ pariveṣṭayet /(STT 1,455,1110)
yasya nāmnā sa mriyate saṃveṣṭan vajrahuṃkṛtaḥ //(STT 1,455,1110)

sūkṣmavajraṃ samāpadya sūkṣmanāsikayā sakṛt /(STT 1,455,1111)
śvāsahuṃkārayogena trailokyam api pātayet //(STT 1,456,1111)

sūkṣmavajravidhiṃ yojya kruddhaḥ san vajradṛṣṭitaḥ /(STT 1,456,1112)
nirīkṣann andhatām yāti maraṇaṃ vā nigacchati //(STT 1,456,1112)

bhagena tu praviṣṭo vai manasā yasya kasya cit /(STT 1,456,1113)
hṛdayākarṣaṇād yāti vaśaṃ svaṃ vā yam asya veti //(STT 1,456,1113)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,456,1114)
huṃ vajravalitakrodha māraya huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,456,1114)
oṃ vajrasūkṣmavajraśvāsa viṣaṃ pātaya huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,456,1114)
oṃ vajradṛṣṭi viṣaṃ nāśaya huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,456,1114)
huṃ hṛdayākarṣaṇakrodha praviśa kāyaṃ hṛdayaṃ chinda bhindākaḍḍhākaḍḍha phaṭ //(STT 1,456,1114)

tato vajrakuladharmamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,459,1115)
tatra tāvan mahāmudrābandho bhavati //:(STT 1,459,1115)

vajrajñānaprayogeṇa jvālāmālākulaprabhān /(STT 1,459,1116)
vajrakrodhān svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan sidhyati kṣaṇād iti //(STT 1,459,1116)

tato vajrakuladharmasamayamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,459,1117)
samādhijñānasamayād dvihuṃkārasamānvitā /(STT 1,459,1117)
yathā sthāneṣu saṃstheyā sarvasiddhipradā vareti //(STT 1,459,1117)

tato vajrakuladharmasamayadharmamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //(STT 1,459,1118)
phaṭ śaṭ maṭ saṭ raṭ raṭ dhṛt haṭ paṭ traṭ kaṭ bhaṭ kṛṭ riṭ khaṭ vaṭ cieti/(STT 1,459,1118)
prokotā dharmamudrāḥ samāsata iti //(STT 1,459,1118)

tato vajrakuldadharmasamayakarmamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,460,1119)
dharmamuṣṭiṃ dvidhīkṛtya yathāsthānaprayogataḥ /(STT 1,460,1119)
karmamudrāḥ samāsena siddhiṃ yānti yathāvidhīti // //(STT 1,460,1119)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājād vajrakuladharmajñānasamayamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ // //(STT 1,461,1120)

(vajrakulakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ)(STT 1,462,1121)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatavajrakarmasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,462,1122)
oṃ sarvatathāgatakarmeśvari hūṃ //(STT 1,462,1122)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar apīmāṃ svavidhyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,462,1123)
oṃ sarvatathāgatadharmadhātuspharaṇamahāpūjākarmavidhivistarasamaye trilokavijayaṃkari sarvaduṣṭān dāmaya vajriṇi hūṃ //(STT 1,462,1123)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvaḥ punar apīmāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,462,1124)
oṃ sarvatathāgatākāśadhātusamavasaraṇamahāpūjākarmavidhivistarasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,462,1124)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvaḥ punar apīmāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:
oṃ sarvatathāgatadharmadhātuspharaṇamahāpūjākarmavidhivistarasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,462,1125)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvaḥ punar apīmāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:
oṃ sarvatathāgatasarvalokadhātuvividhamahāpūjākarmavidhivistarasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,462,1126)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar api svakulapūjāvidhivistaradevatāḥ svahṛdayād utpādya, sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvatathāgatākarṣaṇa, vaśīkaraṇānurāgaṇa, sarvakarmasiddhikāryakaraṇatāsaṃniyojanādīni (STT 1,462463,1127)

sarvatathāgatarddhivikurvitāni kṛtvā, punar api bhagavato vairocanasya, vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena candramaṇḍalāny āśrityāvasthitā iti //(STT 1,463,1128)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva idaṃ vajrakarmasamayavidhivistarakarmamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,463,1129)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi karmamaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,463,1130)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ karmavajram iti smṛtam //(STT 1,464,1130)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /(STT 1,464,11301)
madhyamaṇḍalasaṃstheṣu buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet //(STT 1,464,1131)

buddhasya sarvapārśveṣu samayāgryo niveśayet /(STT 1,464,1132)
vajravegaiḥ samākramya maṇḍalānāṃ catuṣṭaye //(STT 1,464,1132)

catvāro vajranāthādyā yathāvat tu niveśayet /(STT 1,464,1133)
teṣāṃ sarveṣu pārśveṣu mahāsattvā niveśayed iti //(STT 1,464,1133)

athātra karmamaṇḍale vajrakarmamudrā bhavanti //:(STT 1,464,1134)
oṃ vajrasattvasiddhijñānasamaye huṃ jjaḥ //(STT 1,464465,1134)
oṃ vajrākarṣaṇakarmajñānasamaye huṃ jjaḥ //(STT 1,465,1134)
oṃ vajrarati rāgakarmajñānasamaye huṃ jjaḥ //(STT 1,465,1134)
oṃ vajrasādhukarmajñānasamaye huṃ jjaḥ //(STT 1,465,1134)

oṃ vajrabhṛkuṭi vaśīkuru huṃ //(STT 1,465,1135)
oṃ vajrasūryamaṇḍale vaśīkuru huṃ //(STT 1,465,1135)
oṃ vajradhvajāgrakeyūre vaśīkuru huṃ //(STT 1,465,1135)
oṃ vajrāṭṭahāse vaśīkuru huṃ //(STT 1,465,1135)

oṃ vajrapadmarāge rāgaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1136)
oṃ vajratīkṣṇarāge rāgaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1136)
oṃ vajramaṇḍalarāge rāgaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1136)
oṃ vajravāgrāge rāgaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1136)

oṃ vajrakarmasamaye pūjaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1137)
oṃ vajrakavacabandhe rakṣaya huṃ //(STT 1,465,1137)
oṃ vajrayakṣiṇi māraya vajradaṃṣṭrayā bhinda hṛdayam amukasya huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,465,1137)
oṃ vajrakarmamuṣṭi sidhya sidhya huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,465,1137)

athātra karmamaṇḍale yathāvad vidhivistaraṃ kṛtvā, vajrakulakarmajñānāny utpādayet //:(STT 1,466,1138)

tatrādita eva śāntikarmādijñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,466,1139)

samidbhir madhurair agniṃ prajvālya susamāhitaḥ /(STT 1,466,1140)
vajrakrodhasamāpattyā tilāṃ hutvā aghān dahet //(STT 1,466,1140)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālya tu hutāśanam /(STT 1,466,1141)
taṇḍulāṃs tu juhvan nityaṃ gṛhapuṣṭir bhaved dhruvam //(STT 1,466,1141)

samidbhir madhuraiś cāpi vahniṃ prajvālya paṇḍitaḥ /(STT 1,466,1142)
dūrvāpravālān saghṛtān juhvann āyuḥ pravardhate //(STT 1,466,1142)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālya tu hutāśanam /(STT 1,466,1143)
kuśapravālāṃs teilena juhvan rakṣā tu śāśvatam iti //(STT 1,466,1143)

athaiśāṃ hṛdayamantrāṇi bhavanti //:(STT 1,466,1144)
oṃ sarvapāpadahanavajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,467,1144)
oṃ vajrapuṣṭaye svāhā //(STT 1,467,1144)
oṃ vajrāyuṣe svāhā //(STT 1,467,1144)
oṃ apratihatavajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,467,1144)

samidbhiḥ kaṭukaiḥ pūrvaṃ vajrakrodhasamādhinā /(STT 1,467468,1145)
agniṃ prajvālya kuñjais tu kaṇṭakair eti karṣitaḥ //(STT 1,468,1145)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ suroṣavān /(STT 1,468,1146)
raktapuṣpān phalān vāpi juhvan rāgayate jagat //(STT 1,468,1146)

samidbhis tais tu saṃkruddho hy agniṃ prajvālya yogavān /(STT 1,468,1147)
ayorajāṃsi juhvan hi vajrabandho bhaviṣyati //(STT 1,468,1147)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ /(STT 1,468,1147)
juhet tiktaphalaṃ krodhān mārim utpādayet kṣaṇāt //(STT 1,468,1147)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,468,1149)
huṃ vajrākarṣaya svāhā //(STT 1,468,1149)
huṃ vajra rāgaya svāhā //(STT 1,468,1149)
huṃ vajrabandhāya svāhā //(STT 1,468,1149)
huṃ vajramāraṇāya svāhā //(STT 1,468,1149)

samidbhir amlaiḥ prajvālya kruddho hutabhujaṃ budhaḥ /(STT 1,471,1150)
homam āmlaphalaiḥ puṣpair vaśīkaraṇam uttamam //(STT 1,471,1150)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ /(STT 1,471,1151)
juhuyāt kāmaphalān kruddhaḥ kāmarūpitvam āpnuyāt //(STT 1,471,1151)

samidbhis tādṛśair eva prajvālya tu hutāśanam /(STT 1,471,1152)
kāṇḍāny adṛśyapuṣpānāṃ juhvan rucyā na dṛśyate //(STT 1,471,1152)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ /(STT 1,472,1153)
ākāśavallipuṣpāni juhvann ākāśago bhaved iti //(STT 1,472,1153)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,472,1154)
oṃ vajravaśaṃkarāya svāhā //(STT 1,472,1154)
oṃ kāmarūpavajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,472,1154)
oṃ adṛśyavajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,472,1154)
oṃ vajrakhacāriṇe svāhā //(STT 1,472,1154)

samidbhis tiktavīryais tu prajvālyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ /(STT 1,473,1155)
vajripuṣpāñ juhet kruddho vajram ājñākaraṃ bhavet //(STT 1,473,1155)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ suroṣavān /(STT 1,473,1156)
yasya śaure juhen mālyaṃ so 'py ājñākaratāṃ vrajet //(STT 1,473,1156)

samidbhis tais tu saṃkruddhaḥ prajvālyāgniṃ samāhitaḥ /(STT 1,473,1157)
vajrapāṇer juhen mālyaṃ so 'py ājñākaratāṃ jvajet //(STT 1,473,1157)

tair eva tu samidbhis tu prajvālyāgniṃ suroṣitaḥ /(STT 1,473,1158)
cīvarāṇi juhed buddho yāty ājñākaratāṃ kṣaṇāt //(STT 1,473,1158)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,473,1159)
huṃ vajravaśaṃkarāya svāhā //(STT 1,473,1159)
huṃ śaurivaśaṃkaravajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,473,1159)
huṃ vajrapāṇivaśaṃkarāya svāhā //(STT 1,473,1159)
huṃ buddhavaśaṃkaravajrāya svāhā //(STT 1,473,1159)

tato rahasyakarmamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,474,1160)
priyayā tu striyā sārdhaṃ saṃvasaṃs tu bhage 'ñjanam /(STT 1,474,1160)
prakṣipya ghaṭṭayet tatra tenāñjyākṣi vaśaṃ nayet //(STT 1,474,1160)

manaḥśilāṃ bhage viddhvā vajrabandhena tāṃ pidhet /(STT 1,474,1161)
caturvidhair nimittais tu siddhiś cāpi caturvidhā //(STT 1,474,1161)

rocanāṃ tu bhage sthāpya guhyamuṣṭyā nipīḍayet //(STT 1,474,1162)
sthāpitaṃ jvalate tatra bhaved vajradharopamaḥ //(STT 1,474,1162)

kuṅkumaṃ tu bhage viddhvā tad bhagaṃ satavvajrayā /(STT 1,474,1163)
chāditaṃ jvalate tat tu bhaved vajradharopama iti //(STT 1,474,1163)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(STT 1,474,1164)
oṃ vajraguhyarati vaśaṃkara sidhya huṃ //(STT 1,474,1164)
oṃ vajraguhya sidhya huṃ //(STT 1,474,1164)
oṃ guhyavajra sidhya huṃ //(STT 1,474,1164)
oṃ vajradharaguhya sidhya huṃ //(STT 1,474,1164)

tato vajrakulakarmamahāmudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,478,1165)
vajrakāryaprayogeṇa mahāmudrāḥ samāsataḥ /(STT 1,478,1165)
vajrakrodhasamāpattyā vajramuṣṭiprayogataḥ //(STT 1,478,1165)

samayāgryas tathaiveha huṃkārāṅguliyogataḥ /(STT 1,478,1166)
dharmamudrās tathaiveha oṃkārādyair ākṣaraiḥ //(STT 1,478,1166)

karmamudrāḥ samāsena karmamuṣṭidvidhīkṛtāḥ /(STT 1,478,1167)
sarvasiddhikarā śuddhā vajrakarmaprayogataḥ //(STT 1,478,1167)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājād vajrakulakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ //(STT 1,479,1168)

(mahākalpavidhivistara)(=mahāvajrakalpavidhivistara ?)(STT 1,480,1169)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatavajrasamayamudrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,480,1170)
oṃ sarvatathāgatavajrasamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,480,1170)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva imāṃ svavajrasamayamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,480,1171)
huṃ vajri maṭ //(STT 1,480,1171)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imāṃ svaratnasamayamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,480,1172)
huṃ bhṛkuṭivajri raṭ //(STT 1,480,1172)

huṃ padmavajri triṭ //(STT 1,480,1173)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svakarmasamayamudrām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,480,1174)
huṃ vajrakarmāgri kṛṭ //(STT 1,480,1174)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar apīdaṃ trilokavijayacaturmudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,481,1175)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mudrāmaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,481,1176)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ krodhavajram iti smṛtam //(STT 1,481,1176)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam //(STT 1,481,1177)
trilokavijayādyās tu likhed buddhasya sarvata iti //(STT 1,481,1177)

athātra caturmudrāmaṇḍale mahāmaṇḍalayogenākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā praveśya,(STT 1,481,1178)

caturmudrāmaṇḍalaguhyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //(STT 1,481482,11782)

svayaṃ likhya caturmudrāmaṇḍalaṃ śuddhadharmatām /(STT 1,482,1179)
uccārayan striyā sārdhaṃ saṃvasan siddhir āpyate //(STT 1,482,1179)

svayaṃ likhya caturmudrāmaṇḍalaṃ śuddhadharmatām /(STT 1,482,1180)
uccārayan rāgeṇa nirīkṣan siddhir āpyate //(STT 1,482,1180)

svayaṃ likhya caturmudrāmaṇḍalaṃ śuddhadharmatām /(STT 1,482,1181)
pravartayan striyaṃ kāntāṃ paricumbaṃs tu sidhyati //(STT 1,482,1181)

svayaṃ likhyacaturmudrāmaṇḍalaṃ śuddhadharmatām /(STT 1,482,1182)
uccārayan samāliṅget sarvasiddhir avāpyate //(STT 1,482,1182)

tatraitāḥ śuddhadharmatāmudrā bhavanti //:(STT 1,482,1183)
oṃ sarvatathāgataviśuddhadharmate hoḥ //(STT 1,482,1183)
oṃ vajraviśuddhadṛṣṭi jjaḥ //(STT 1,482,1183)
oṃ svabhāvaviśuddhamukhe huṃ //(STT 1,482,1183)
oṃ sarvaviśuddhakāyavāṅmanaḥkarmavajri phaṭ //(STT 1,482,1183)

tataś caturmudrāmaṇḍalaguhyarahasyamudrāṃ śiksa.yet //:(STT 1,483,1184)
praviśya maṇḍalam idaṃ pañcabhiḥ kāmasadguṇaiḥ /(STT 1,483,1184)
ramayan paradārāṇi sutarāṃ siddhim āpunute //(STT 1,483,1184)

athāsyā hḍayaṃ bhavati //(STT 1,483,1185)
ho vajrakāma //(STT 1,483,1185)

tato yathāvad vajrakrāntitriśūlamudrādyāḥ catasraḥ samayamudrāḥ savidhivistarāḥ śikṣayitvānena caturmudrāprayogeṇa vajravādyatūryatālān niryātya, vajrasattvasaṃgrahahṛdayagītiṃ gāyatā mudrāpratimudropamudrājñānamudrābhir nṛtyopahārāpūjā kāryeti //(STT 1,484,1186)

tatreyaṃ nṛtyopahārapūjā bhavati //:(STT 1,484,1187)
vajranṛtyaprayogeṇa vajrakrodhāṅgulidvayam /(STT 1,484,1187)
vajrahuṃkāramudrāṃ tu hṛdaye tu nibandhayet //(STT 1,484,1187)

tathaiva nṛtyan vāmāṃ tu gṛhya dakṣiṇamuṣṭinā /(STT 1,484,1188)
parivartya lalāṭe tu niveśyāgryāmukhena tu //(STT 1,484,1188)

tathaiva nṛtyaṃ muktvā tu samakuḍmalasaṃdhite /(STT 1,484,1189)
agrāṅguliṃ hṛdi sthāpya named āśayakampitaiḥ //(STT 1,484485,1189)

vajrakrodhāṅgulī samyag uttānamukhasaṃdhite /(STT 1,485,1190)
parivartya tathoṣ.īṣe tarjanīmukhasaṃsthiteti //(STT 1,485,1190)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar apīmaṃ svavajrasamayakrodham abhāṣat //:(STT 1,486,1191)
huṃ //(STT 1,486,1191)

athāsya maṇḍalaṃ bhavati //:(STT 1,486,1192)
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi guhyamaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,486,1192)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ vajrahuṃkārasaṃjñitam //(STT 1,486,1192)

mahāmaṇḍalayogena bāhyamaṇḍalam ālikhet /(STT 1,486,1193)
tasya madhye likhet samyag vajriṇaṃ candramaṇḍalam //(STT 1,486,1193)

savajravajrahuṃkāramahāmudrākaragraham /(STT 1,486,1194)
pratyālīḍhasusaṃsthānaṃ yathāvad varṇarūpiṇam iti //(STT 1,486,1194)

athātra guhyamaṇḍale sarvasiddhividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā,(STT 1,487,1195)

vajrahuṃkāraguhyamudrājñānam udīrayet //:(STT 1,487,1196)
praviśya maṇḍalam idaṃ trilokavijayāṅgulīm /(STT 1,487,1196)
sādhayet tu bhage viddhvā sarvakarmasu sidhyati (STT 1,487,1196)

athāsyāḥ sādhanahṛdayaṃ bhavati //:(STT 1,487,1197)
huṃ vajrasamaya kṛt //(STT 1,487,1197)

tato vajrahuṃkārārahasyasādhanamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(STT 1,488,1198)
praviṣṭvā maṇḍalaṃ samyaṅ mahāmudrāgrasaṃsthitaḥ /(STT 1,488,1198)
saṃvasan vajrahuṃkāraḥ sarvakarmakaro bhaved iti //(STT 1,488,1198)

tatrāsyāḥ sādhanahṛdayaṃ bhavati //:(STT 1,488,1199)
huṃ vajrasamaya huṃ //(STT 1,488,1199)

tato yathāvan mudrābandhacatuṣṭayaṃ śikṣayet //(STT 1,488,1200)
tathaiva siddhayaḥ saṃbhāntīti //(STT 1,488,1200)

yathā maṇḍala evaṃ paṭādiṣu likhitānāṃ sarvapratimāsv api sāmānyā siddhir iti //(STT 1,488,1201)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ sarvatathāgatān āhūyaivam āha //:(STT 1,489,1202)
adhitiṣṭhata, bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatā mamedaṃ kulaṃ, yena sarvasattvā yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā sarvasiddhīḥ prāpnuyur iti //(STT 1,489,1202)

atha bhagavataḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamyāsya trilokavijayakalpasyādhiṣṭhānāyedam ūcuḥ //(STT 1,489490,1203)

sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratyāna sādhu te /(STT 1,490,1204)
vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe //(STT 1,490,1204)
subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /(STT 1,490,1204)
sarvatathāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham iti //(STT 1,490,1204)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājān mahāvajrakalpavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ //(STT 1,490,1205)

trilokacakramahāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ (STT 1,491,1206)
atha bhagavantḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ punar api samājam āpadya jānann eva vajrapāṇiṃ mahābodhisattvam evam āhuḥ /(STT 1,491,1206)

pratiapdyasva, vatsa, sarvatathāgatājñākāritāyā imaṃ maheśvarakāyam ataḥ svapādatalād moktum iti //(STT 1,491,1207)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇis tāṃs tathāgatān evam āha //:(STT 1,491,1208)
ahaṃ bhagavadbhiḥ sarvaduṣṭadamakaḥ krodha ity abhiṣiktaḥ /(STT 1,491,1208)
tan mayāyaṃ vyāpāditaḥ. tat katham asya mokṣyāmīti //(STT 1,491,1208)

atha sarvatathāgatā maheśvarasya sarvatrilokādhipateḥ śarīrasya jīvitasaṃjananahetor idaṃ mṛtavijñānākarṣaṇahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayebhyo niśceruḥ //:(STT 1,492,1209)
oṃ vajrasattva hūṃ jjaḥ //(STT 1,492,1209)

athāsya mudrābandho bhavati //:(STT 1,492,1210)
guhyāṅkuśīṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya samāntyasuprasāritā /(STT 1,492,1210)
mṛtasya mūurdhni saṃdhāya ratijīvanam āpnuyāt //(STT 1,492,1210)

athāsmin āptamātre bhagavān bhasmeśvaranirghoṣatathāgato bhasmacchannalokadhātor āgatvā maheśvarakāyaṃ praviṣṭvedam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,492,1211)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ buddhajñānam anuttaram /(STT 1,492,1212)
yo mṛto 'pi hi kāyo 'yaṃ jīvadhūtatvam āgata iti //(STT 1,492,1212)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva idaṃ pādotkṣepaṇaṃ nāma hṛdayam udājahāra //:(STT 1,496,1213)
oṃ vajra muḥ //(STT 1,496,1213)

athāsya mudrābandho bhavati //:(STT 1,496,1214)
vajrakrodhāṅgulīsamayaṅ mukhāsaṅgaṃ tu harṣite /(STT 1,496497,1214)
parivartya tayor vajraṃ tam adhogāt samuddhared iti //(STT 1,497,1214)
vajrakrodhāṅgulī samayaṅ mukhāsaṅgaṃ samādhayan /(STT 1,497,1214)
harṣite parivartā tu (or haste paribhraman vajre) vajrādhonayam uddhared iti // (or 'dho mūrdhe gāṃ samuddhared iti //(STT 1,497,1214)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre mahāvajradharapādamūlān mahādevo muktaḥ svayam ajānāt // tato 'yaṃ maheśvarakāyo 'nena tatathāgatena pratijīvam (or sañīvam) adhitiṣṭhāya, (STT 1,504,1215)

svayauva (or yuva)rājyatāyām atraiva lokadhātau sarvasattvārthaṃ sarvaduṣṭavinayārthaṃ ca pratiṣṭhāpitavān iti //(STT 1,504,1216)

atha tato vajrapāṇicaraṇatalād imāṃ cajdrapādāṃ nāma sarvatathāgatabodhicittamudrāṃ niścacāra //:(STT 1,505,1217)
oṃ candrottare samantabhadrakiraṇe mahāvajriṇi hūṃ //(STT 1,505,1217)

athāsyā mudrābandho bhavati //(STT 1,505,1218)
vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhasamayoḥ /(STT 1,505,1218)
prasāritā tu saṃdhāya candrapādeti saṃjñitā //(STT 1,505,1218)

athāsyāṃ viniḥsṛtamātrāyāṃ tata eva pādatālāc candrottara eva tathāgato viniḥsṛtya maheśvaramūrdhavajrapāṇicaraṇākrānta pādena candrārdhikakrānto bhūtvā vāmapārśve saṃsthitaḥ //(STT 1,505,1219)

atha sarvatathāgatair vajrapāṇimitratve pāṇau (or pāṇibhyāṃ) vajrajñānaṃ vadhvā (or vajraśūlaṃ dattvā) vajravidyottamo vajravidyottama iti vajranāmābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ //(STT 1,511,1220)

atha vajravidyottamo bodhisattvo mahāsattvas tena vajraśūlenālātacakraparivartanatayā nṛtyopahārapūjāṃ kurvann idam udānam udānayām āsa //:(STT 1,511,1221)

aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ bodhicittam anuttaram /(STT 1,511,1222)
yat pādāgraspṛśenāpi buddhatvaṃ prāpyate mayeti //(STT 1,511,1222)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvas tato vajrakrodhasamādher vyutthāya bhagavantam etad avocad //:(STT 1,512,1223)

ahaṃ, bhagavan, sarvatathāgatair vajraṃ pāṇibhyāṃ dattvā vajrapāṇitvenābhiṣiktaḥ //.(STT 1,512,1224)
tad eṣāṃ devādīnāṃ bāhyavajrakulānām asmin trilokavijayamahāmaṇḍale sthānaviniyogaṃ kariṣyāmi, yena te sattvā avaivartikā bhaviṣyanty anuttarāyāṃ samyaksambodhāv iti //(STT 1,512,1224)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgato 'rhan samyaksambuddha idaṃ tathāgatoṣṇīṣam udājahāra //:(STT 1,512513,1225)
oṃ vajrasattvoṣṇīṣa huṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,513,1225)

athātra trilokacakramahāmaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādikarma kṛtvā, svayaṃ vajrācāryo vajrakrodhaterittirimudrāṃ baddhvaivaṃ brūyād (STT 1,537,1291)

vajraceṭasamayamudrāḥ //(STT 1,559,1348)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vajramaṇḍalam uttamam /(STT 1,560,1350)
caturasram (ed. aśram) uttaradvāraṃ sūtrayed bāhyamaṇḍalam //(STT 1,560,1350)

tasyābhyantaratas tatra pūrvadvāraṃ tathaiva ca /(STT 1,560,1351)
tasya madhye yathānyāyaṃ buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet //(STT 1,560,1351)

trilokavijayādyās tu catasras tasya sarvataḥ /(STT 1,560,1352)
maṇḍalasya tathā 'greṣu vajramudrāḥ samālikhet //(STT 1,560,1352)

tesāṃ sarveṣu pārśveṣu kulamudrāḥ samālikhet /(STT 1,560,1353)
vajraśuauṇḍādayaś caiva catvāro dvārarakṣakāḥ //(STT 1,560,1353)

bhīmāṃ śriyaṃ sarasvatīṃ durgāṃ koṇeṣu vāmataḥ /(STT 1,560,1354)
bāhyakoṇeṣu mudrā vā āsām eva tu saṃlikhet //(STT 1,560,1354)

bāhyamaṇḍalasaṃstheṣu sarvadevīḥ samālikhet /(STT 1,560,1355)
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvad vidhivistaram iti //(STT 1,560,1355)

athātra vajramaṇḍale yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā vajrāṅkuśādibhiḥ samayakarma kṛtvā, vajradhārimudrāṃ yathāvad baddhvā brūyān:(STT 1,561,1356)

na kasya cit tvayādṛṣṭasamayasyaitāḥ samayamudrāḥ purato vaktavyāḥ /(STT 1,561,1357)
na ca rahasyabhedaḥ kartavyaḥ //(STT 1,561,1357)

tatas tat karmavajraṃ vajradhārimudrāyā upari sthāpya yathāvat praveśayet //.(STT 1,561,1358)

praveśya tad vajraṃ tathaiva kṣipet/.(STT 1,561,1359)
yatra patati sāsya samayamudrā vaśyā bhavati //(STT 1,561,1359)
tayā sarvakarmāṇi karoti //(STT 1,561,1359)

tato mukhabandhaṃ muktvā maṇḍalaṃ yathāvad darśayitvā, samayamudrārahasyaṃ brūyāt //:(STT 1,563,1360)

etāḥ samayamudrās te sarvakarmakarāḥ sadā /(STT 1,563,1361)
mātaraś ca bhaginyaś ca bhāryā duhitaro 'nugā iti //(STT 1,563,1361)

tatrāsyā hṛdayaṃ bhavati //:(STT 1,563,1362)
oṃ sarvavajragāmini sarvabhakṣe sādhaya guhyavajriṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,563,1362)

anayā sakṛjjaptayā sarvastriyo vaśīkṛtyopabhoktavyāḥ /(STT 1,563,1363)
adharmo na bhavati //(STT 1,563,1363)
yathābhirucitaś ca sarvaṃ bhuktvā sādhyāḥ /(STT 1,563,1363)
tataḥ sarvaśuddhicittatām avetya, sarvamudrā manasttamāny api sarvakarmāṇi kurvantīty āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ //(STT 1,563,1363)

ataḥ samayamudrāḥ śikṣayitavyāḥ //(STT 1,564,1364)
samayakrodhāṅgulī mūrdhni hṛdaye ca dṛḍhīkṛtā /(STT 1,564,1364)
mukhorṇā ca mukhodvāntā mūrdhni sthāpya dvidhīkṛteti //(STT 1,564,1364)

vāmavajrāgrabandhena triśūlāṅkaṃ tu pīḍayet /(STT 1,564,1365)
anayā baddhayā samyak sidhyed vidyottamaḥ svayam //(STT 1,564,1365)

sarvavajrakulānāṃ tu vāmavajrāgrasaṃgraham /(STT 1,564,1366)
mudrābandhaṃ pravakṣyāmi samayānāṃ yathāvidhi //(STT 1,564,1366)

cakrā sarvāṅgasaṃpīḍā ghaṇṭāmudrā tathaiva ca /(STT 1,564,1367)
tathaiv' oṃkāramudrā tu siṃhakarṇaparigrahā //(STT 1,564,1367)
vidyārājanakāḥ //(STT 1,564,1367)

jvālāparigrahā caiva prabhāsaṃgraham eva ca /(STT 1,564,1368)
daṇḍamuṣṭigrahā caiva mukhataḥ parivartitā //(STT 1,564,1368)
krodhasamayāḥ //(STT 1,565,1368)

pānamudrā ca mālā ca vajrāvaṣṭambhanāmitā /(STT 1,565,1369)
mūrdhasthā caiva gaṇikā maṇḍaladvārapālikāḥ //(STT 1,565,1369)
gaṇapatisamayāḥ //(STT 1,565,1369)

bāhusaṃkocavakrā tu pṛṣṭhataḥ parivartitā /(STT 1,565,1370)

jvālāsphuliṅgamokṣā ca vidāritamukhasthitā //(STT 1,565,1371)
dūtasamayāḥ //(STT 1,565,1371)

dvyantapraveśitamukhīpīḍya caiva prapātanī /(STT 1,565,1372)
bāhuveṣṭanaveṣṭā ca sahasā hāriṇī tatheti //(STT 1,565,1372)
ceṭasamayāḥ //(STT 1,565,1372)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājāt sarvavajrakulavajramaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // //(STT 1,568,1373)

sarvavajrakuladharmasamayamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ(STT 1,569,1374)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatadharmasamayasaṃbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,569,1375)
oṃ vajravit //(STT 1,569,1375)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar apīmaṃ svadharmasamayam abhāṣat //:(STT 1,569,1376)

atha māyāvajra uvāca //:(STT 1,570,1381)

athātra dharmasamayamaṇḍale yathāvat karma kṛtvā, vajradhārimudrāṃ savajraghaṇṭāṃ baddhvā praveśyaivaṃ brūyāt /:(STT 1,574,1389)

na tvayā kasya cid asamayadṛṣṭasyādṛṣṭadevakulasya vaktavyam iti //(STT 1,574,1390)

uktvā tāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ raṇāpayet //,(STT 1,574,1391)
evaṃ ca brūyāt śapathahṛdayaṃ dattvā //(STT 1,574,1391)

yathā raṇāpyate ghaṇṭā śabdaś cāsya yathā dhruvam /(STT 1,574,1392)
tatredaṃ karmavajraṃ te nāśaṃ kuryāt tathā dhruvam //(STT 1,574,1392)

vajrācāryaṃ na gauravyaṃ vajrabhrātṛṣv amitratā /(STT 1,574,1393)
duṣṭamaitrī virāgaś ca yadi kuryād bhavān kadeti //(STT 1,574,1393)

tato mukhabandhaṃ muktvā maṇḍalaṃ darśya, dharmasamayamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //(STT 1,578,1394)

buddhavajradharādīnāṃ yathāvad dharmamaṇḍale /(STT 1,578,1395)
dhyānaṃ sarvasamatvaṃ hi vajravidyottamasya tu //(STT 1,578,1395)

māyopamaṃ jagad idaṃ duḥkhaṃ ghaṇṭopamaṃ tathā /(STT 1,578,1396)
nirvāṇaṃ sarvaduḥkhānāṃ vajraṃ bhediṣv anuttamam iti //(STT 1,578,1396)
vidyārājanakasamādhayaḥ //(STT 1,578,1396)

krodho 'gryaḥ sattvavinaye saumyatvaṃ māraṇaṃ dhruvam /(STT 1,578,1397)

vajrakrodhasamādhayaḥ //(STT 1,578,1397)

madāt tulyo na dhairyo 'sti mālātulyaṃ na bandhanam /(STT 1,578,1398)

gaṇasamādhayaḥ (gaṇapatisamādhayaḥ ?)//(STT 1,578,1398)

prahāro nigrahāgryo hi saparśānāṃ tu samīraṇāḥ /(STT 1,578579,1399)
tejasāṃ hutabhug jyeṣṭhaḥ bhojanānāṃ tu lohitam iti //(STT 1,579,1399)
dhūtasamādhayaḥ //(STT 1,579,1399)

daṃṣṭrāśuddhaḥ praviṣṭas tu mṛtyuḥ sarvapade sthitaḥ /(STT 1,579,1400)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājāt sarvavajrakuladharmasamayamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ //STT 1,580,1401)

sarvavajrakulakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ (STT 1,581,1402)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatakarmasamayodbhavavajrādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //(STT 1,581,14031405)
oṃ vajrakarmapravartanisamaye hūṃ //(STT 1,581,1405)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar api svakarmottamām abhāṣat //(STT 1,581,1406)
oṃ vajravilāse pūjaya hūṃ //(STT 1,581,1406)

atha vajragarbhaḥ svakarmottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,581,1407)
oṃ vajrābhiṣeke 'bhiṣiñca hūṃ //(STT 1,581,1407)

atha vajranetraḥ svakarmottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,581,1408)
oṃ vajragīte gāhi hūṃ //(STT 1,582,1408)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvaḥ svakarmavidyottamām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,582,1409)
oṃ vajranṛtye nṛtya hūṃ //(STT 1,582,1409)

atha vajravidyottamaḥ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //(STT 1,582,1410)
oṃ vajravidyottame nṛtya nṛtya vikurva vikurva hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,582,1410)

atha vajrakrodhavajrāgnimahādevīmāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,586,1411)

oṃ vajrakrodhavajrāgni jvālaya triśūlaṃ bhinda hṛdayaṃ vajreṇa hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,586,1412)

atha vajrahemāmahādevīmāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,586,1413)
oṃ vajraheme chinda cakreṇa vajriṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,586,1413)

atha vajrakaumārīmāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,586,1414)
oṃ vajrakaumārī śīghram āveśaya ghaṇṭāśabdena vajrapāṇipriye vajrasamayam anusmara raṇa raṇa hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,586587,1414)

atha vajraśāntir mahādevīmāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //(STT 1,587,1415)
oṃ vajraśānti japa japākṣamālayā sarvān māraya śāntadṛṣṭyā hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,587,1415)

atha vajramuṣṭi hana hana vajreṇa bhinda bhinda pīḍaya pīḍaya sarvaduṣṭahṛdayāni, oṃ śumbha niśumbha hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,587,1416)
vidyārājanikāḥ //(STT 1,587,1416)

atha vajrāmṛtā krodhinī svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,588,1417)

oṃ vajrāmṛte sarvaduṣṭān gṛhṇa bandha hana paca vidhvaṃsaya vināśaya bhinda chinda bhasmīkuru mūrdhānaṃ tāḍaya vajreṇa ye kecid mam amukasya vighnavināyakās tān dāmaya dīptakrodhavajriṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,588589,1418)

atha vajrakāṇṭiḥ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(STT 1,589,1419)
oṃ vajrakāṇṭi māraya saumye rūpe pradīptarāgeṇa śīghraṃ sphoṭaya hṛdayaṃ vajradharasatyena mahājyotsnākarāle śītaraśmivajriṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(STT 1,589,1419)

atha vajradaṇḍāgrā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1,1420)
oṃ vajradaṇḍāgre ghātaya huṃ (or hūṃ) phaṭ //(1, 1420)

atha vajramekhalā mahākrodhinīmām svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1421)
oṃ vajramekhale khana khana śabdena vaśīkuru māraya bhīṣaṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(1, 1421)
krodhavidyāḥ //(1, 1421)

atha vajravilayā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1422)
oṃ vajravilaye chinda sina bhinda vajreṇa mādayonmādaya piba piba hūṃ (ed. hūm) phaṭ //(1, 1422)

atha vajrāśanā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1423)
oṃ vajrāśane bhakṣa duṣṭān vajradarśane śantidhāriṇi mānuṣamāṃsāhāre nararudhirasavapriye majja(1, 1423)

vāsānulepenaviliptagātra ānaya sarvadhanadhānyahiraṇyasuvarṇādīni saṃgrahamayavarade bhakṣiṇi hūṃ phaṭ //(1, 1424)

atha vajravasana ānaya sarvavastrānnapānādyupakāraṇāṇi śīghraṃ vaśīkurv idaṃ me prayacchāviśāviśa satyaṃ kathaya vajrakośadhāriṇi huṃ (or hūṃ) phaṭ //(1, 1425)

atha vajravaśī svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1426)

oṃ vajravaśy ānaya vaśīkuru sarvastriyaḥ sarvapuruṣān dāsīkuru kruddhān prasādaya vyavahārebhyo vyutāraya vijayaṃkari vajrapatākādhāriṇi huṃ (or hūṃ) phaṭ //(1, 1428)
vajragaṇikāḥ //(1, 1428)

atha vajramusalā vajradhūtīmāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1429)
oṃ vajradūty ānaya sarvān maṇḍalaṃ praveśaya bandhaya sarvakarmāṇi me kuru śīghraṃ laghu laghu trāsaya māraya māraya rāveṇa vajrakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇi huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1429)

atha vegavajriṇī svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1430)
oṃ vegavajriṇi ghu ghu ghu ghu śabdena māraya vikira vidhvaṃsaya vajrapaṭadhāriṇi huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1430)

atha vajrajvālā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1431)
oṃ vajrajvāle jvālaya sarvaṃ vajrajvālayā daha daha bhasmīkuru huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1431)

atha vajravikaṭā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1432)
oṃ vajravikaṭe pravikaṭadaṃṣṭrākarālabhīṣanavaktre śīghraṃ gṛhṇāveśaya bhakṣaya rudhiraṃ piba mahāyakṣiṇi vajrapāśadhāriṇi huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1432)
vajradhūtyaḥ //(1, 1432)

atha vajramukhī vajraceṭī svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1433)
oṃ vajramukhy ānaya vajradaṃṣṭre bhayānike pātālanivāsini khana khana khāhi khāhi sarvaṃ mukhe praveśaya sphoṭaya marmāṇi sarvaduṣṭānāṃ vajraniśitāsidhāriṇi huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1433)

atha vajrakālī svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1434)
oṃ vajrakāli mahāpretarūpiṇi mānuṣamāṃsarudhirapriya ehy ehi gṛhṇa gṛhṇa bhakṣaya vajraḍākini vajraśaṅkale sarvadevagaṇamātṛbhūte hara hara prāṇān amukasya (1, 1434)

kapālamālālaṃkṛtasarvakāye kiṃ cirāsi vajrakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇīpretamānuṣaśarīre śīghram āveśaya praveśaya bandhaya māraya vajrarākṣasi huṃ huṃ huṃ huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1435)

atha vajrapūtanā svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1436)
oṃ vajrapūtane mānuṣamāṃsavāsarudhiramūtrapurīṣaśleśmasiṃghāṇakaretogarbhāhāriṇy āyāhi śīghram idam asya kuru vajraśodhanikādhāriṇi sarvakarmāṇi me kuru huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1436)

atha vajramakaremāṃ svakarmasamayām abhāṣat //:(1, 1437)
oṃ vajramakare grasa grasa śīghraṃ śīghraṃ praveśaya pātālaṃ bhakṣaya vajramarakadhāriṇi huṃ phaṭ //(1, 1437)
vajraceṭayaḥ //(1, 1437)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ punar apīdaṃ sarvavajrakulakarmamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(1, 1438)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi karmamaṇḍalam uttamam /(1, 1439)
vajramaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam //(1, 1439)

maṇḍalāgrāṇi sarvāṇi buddhamadhyasthitāni /(1, 1440)
teṣāṃ pārśveṣu paṅktyā vai mahāsattvān niveśayet //(1, 1440)

tasya madhye sapatnīkaṃ vajravidyottāma. svayam /(1, 1441)
vajralāsyādighir guhyanṛtyapūjābhir arcayet //(1, 1441)

atra devyo 'nupūrvaṃ tu cakramaṇḍalayogataḥ /(1, 14421443)
svamudrāpratimudrābhir nṛtyamānās tu saṃlikhet //(1, 1443)

pūjārthaṃ buddhavajribhyāṃ vajranṛtyaprayogataḥ /(1, 1444)
koṇeṣu dvārabhāgeṣu hy anupūrvaṃ dhūpādikam iti //(1, 1444)

athātra karmamaṇḍale samākarṣaṇādikarma kṛtvā yathāvad vajradhārikarmasamayamudrāṃ baddhvaivaṃ vadet /(1, 1445)

na tvayā kasya cid adṛṣṭadevatākramavijñātakarmasyedaṃ guhyakarma vaktavyam /.(1, 1446)
mā te samayo vyathed (1, 1446)
ity uktvā svakarmavajradhārisamayamudrāṃ bandhayet //(1, 1446)
krodhadṛṣṭyā ca nirīkṣann idam uccārayet //(1, 14461447)

oṃ vajradhāry āveśaya praveśaya nṛtyāpaya sarvakarmasiddhiṃ me prayaccha hūṃ aḥ hūṃ a la la la la vajri //(1, 1448)

tataḥ svayam āviśya praviśati //(1, 1449)
mudrāpratimudrābhir nṛtyopahārapūjāṃ karoti /.(1, 1449)
tataḥ prabhṛti sarvakarmāṇi kāyavāgdṛṣṭimanovajra^mudrābhir (or mudrādibhir) īpsitena karoti //(1, 1449)

tato mukhabandhaṃ muktvā, nṛtyopahāramudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:(1, 1450)

buddhavajradharādīnāṃ samayāgryo dvidhīkṛtaḥ /(1, 1451)
vajralāsyādipūjāṃ tu vajravidyottamasya vai // (1, 1451)

sarvāsāṃ caiva vidyānāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /(1, 1452)
nṛtyopahārapūjābhiḥ pūjayet karmamaṇḍalam // (1, 1452)


vajranṛtyaprayogeṇa mahāmudrās tu saṃkṣipet /(1, 1453)
samayāgryo dvidhīkṛtya pratimudrābhimokṣayet //(1, 1453)

ābhir nṛtyopahāreṇa pūjayan sarvanāyakān /(1, 1454)
mahāvajradharādīṃś ca karmasiddhir bhaved dhruvam iti //(1, 1454)

sarvatathāgatavajrasamayān mahākalparājāt sarvavajrakulakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // //(1, 1455)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ sarvavajrakulān sarvasattvārthatāyāṃ yāvat saṃniyojyāvaivartikabhūmau pratiṣṭhāpya jānann eva bhagavantam etad avocat //:(1, 1456)

ahaṃ bhagavadbhiḥ sarvatathāgataiḥ sarvaguhyadhāritve 'bhiṣiktaḥ /(1, 1457)
tad ajñāpayasva kiṃ tat tathāgataguhyam iti //(1, 1457)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgataguhyavajraṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgataguhyam abhāṣat //:(1, 1458)

yathā yathā hi vineyāḥ sarvasattvāḥ svajātataḥ /(1, 1459)
tathā tathā hi sattvārthaṃ kuryād rāgādibhiḥ śuciḥ //(1, 1459)

atha vajrapāṇir idaṃ svaguhyatām abhāṣat //:(1, 1460)
sarvasattvahitārthāya buddhaśāsanahetutaḥ /(1, 1460)
mārayet sarvasattvāṃs tu na sa pāpena lipyate //(1, 1460)
% quoted in Nāmamantrārthāvalokinī  \Ted p.226
% pāda c reads mārayan sarvasattvāṃs tu

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva idaṃ svamaṇiguhyam abhāṣat //:(1, 1461)
sarvasattvahitārthāya saṃbuddhārthaprayogataḥ /(1, 1461)
haraṃs tu sarvavittāni na sa pāpena lipyate //(1, 1461)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva idaṃ sarvadharmaguhyam abhāṣat //:(1, 1462)
rāgatulyasukhaṃ nāsti jinebhyas taṃ tu saṃdadan /(1, 1462)
sattvārthaṃ paradārāṇi sevayan puṇyam āpnute //(1, 1462)
% quoted in Nāmamantrārthāvalokinī. pādas ab read rāgatulyaṃ sukhaṃ nāsti taj jinebhyaḥ samādadat.

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva idaṃ svakarmaguhyam abhāṣat //:(1, 1463)
sarvasattvahitarthāya buddhaśāsanahetutaḥ /(1, 1463)
sarvakarmāṇi kuryāt vai sa bahupuṇyam āpnuta iti //(1, 1463)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgato bhagavate guhyadhāriṇe vajradharāya sādhukārair abhiṣṭavat //:(1, 1464)

sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /(1, 1465)
vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe /(1, 1465)

subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /(1, 1466)
sarvatathāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham iti //(1, 1466)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvatathāgatavajrasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ parisamāptaḥ // (1, 1467)

sarvatathāgatadharmasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ (2, 1468)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya, tam eva vajrapāṇiṃ bhagavantaṃ sarvadharmeśvaram avalokiteśvaram anena nāmāṣṭaśatenādhyeṣitavantaḥ //:(2, 1469)

padmasattva mahāpadma lokeśvara maheśvara /(2, 1470)
avalokiteśvara dhīrāgrya vajradharma namo 'stu te //(2, 1470)

dharmarāja mahāśuddha sattvarāja mahāmate /(2, 1471)
padmātmaka mahāpadma padmanātha namo 'stu te //(2, 1471)

padmodbhava supadmābha padmaśuddha suśodhaka /(2, 1472)
padmavajra supadmāṅga padmapadma namo 'stu te //(2, 1472)

mahāviśva mahāloka mahākārya mahopama /(2, 1473)
mahādhīra mahāvīra mahāśaure namo 'stu te // (2, 1473)

sattvāśaya mahāyāna mahāyoga pitāmaha /(2, 1474)
sanso śaṃkara śudhārtha buddhapadma namo 'stu te //(2, 1474)

dharmatattvārtha saddharma śuddhadharma sudharmakṛt /(2, 1475)
mahādharma sudharmāgrya dharmacakra namo 'stu te //(2, 1475)

buddhasattva susattvāgrya dharmasattva susattvadhṛk /(2, 1476)
sattvottama susattvajña sattvasattva namo 'stu te //(2, 1476)

avalokiteśa nāthāgrya mahānātha vilokita /(2, 1477)
ālokaloka lokārtha lokanātha namo 'stu te //(2, 1477)

lokākṣarākṣaramahān akṣarāgryākṣaropama /(2, 1478)
akṣarākṣara sarvākṣa cakrākṣara namo 'stu te //(2, 1478)

padmahasta mahāhasta samāśvāsaka dāyaka /(2, 1479)
buddhadharma mahābuddha buddhātmaka namo 'stu te //(2, 1479)

buddharūpa mahārūpa vajrarūpa surūpavit /(2, 1480)
dharmāloka sutejāgrya lokāloka namo 'stu te //(2, 1480)

padmaśrīnātha nāthāgra dharmaśrīnātha nāthavān /(2, 1481)
brahmanātha mahābrahma brahmaputra namo 'stu te //(2, 1481)

dīpa dīpāgrya dīpāgrya dīpāloka sudīpaka /(2, 1482)
dīpanātha mahādīpa buddhadīpa namo 'stu te //(2, 1482)

buddhābhiṣikta buddhāgrya buddhaputra mahābuddha /(2, 1483)
buddhābhiṣeka mūrdhāgrya buddhabuddha namo 'stu te //(2, 1483)

buddhacakṣo mahācakṣo dharmacakṣo mahekṣaṇa /(2, 1484)
samādhijñāna sarvasva vajranetra namo 'stu te //(2, 1484)

yainaṃ sarvātmanā gauṇaṃ nāmnām aṣṭaśataṃ tava /(2, 1485)
bhāvayet stunuyād vāpi lokaiśvaryam avāpnuyāt //(2, 1485)

adhyeṣayāma tvāṃ vīra prakāśaya mahāmune /(2, 1486)
svakaṃ tu kulam utpādya dharma-maṇḍalam uttamam iti //(2, 1486)

atha āryāvalokiteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvatathāgatādhyeṣaṇavacanam upaśrutya, yena bhagavāñ chākyamunis tathāgataḥ, tenābhimukhaṃ sthitvā, tad vajrapadmaṃ svahṛdi pratiṣṭhāpyedam udānam udānayām āsa //(2, 1487)

aho hi paramaṃ śuddhaṃ vajrapadmam idaṃ mama /(2, 1488)
pitāham asya ca suto 'dhiṣṭhasva kulaṃ tv idam iti //(2, 1488)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgataḥ sarvatathāgatavajradharmasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhānpadmaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvatathāgatadharmasamayaṃ nāma sarvatathāgatahṛdayaṃ svahṛdayān niścacāra //:(2, 1489)

hrīḥ //(2, 1490)

athāsmin viniḥsṛtamātre sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyaḥ padmākārāḥ anekavarṇarūpaliṅeryāpatharaśmayo viniḥsṛtya, (2, 1491)

sarvalokadhātuṣu rāgādīni saṃbuddhadharmatājñānāni saṃśodhya, punar apy āgatyāryāvalokiteśvarasya hṛdaye praviṣṭā iti //(2, 1492)

atha bhagavān sarvatathāgatadharmasamayaṃ nāma vidyottamam abhāṣat //:(2, 1493)
oṃ vajrapadmottama hrīḥ //(2, 1493)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva idaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(2, 1494)
oṃ vajra huṃ phaṭ //(2, 1494)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva idaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //(2, 1495)
oṃ vajraratnottama traḥ //(2, 1495)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva idaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //(2, 1496)
oṃ vajravidyottama hrīḥ //(2, 1496)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva idaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:(2, 1497)
oṃ vajraviśvottama aḥ //(2, 1497)

atha khalv avalokiteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvarūpasaṃdarśanaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ sarvajagadvinayasamayaṃ nāma svahṛdayam abhāṣat //:(2, 1498)
oṃ huṃ hrīḥ hoḥ //(2, 1498)

athāsmin bhāṣitamātre āryāvalokiteśvarahṛdayāt sa eva bhagavān vajradharaḥ āryāvalokiteśvararūpadhāriṇaḥ padmapratiṣṭhāḥ padmamudrācihnadhārivicitravarṇarūpaveśālaṃkārāḥ tathāgatādisarvasattvamūrtidharā mahābodhisattvavigrahā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, (2, 1499)

sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvasattvānāṃ yathāvaineyatayā svarūpāṇi saṃdarśyāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvadhātuvinayaṃ kṛtvā, punar apy āgatya, vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena bhagavataḥ śākyamunes tathāgatasya sarvataś candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayinsuḥ //(2, 1500)

aho hi sarvabuddhānām upāyaḥ karuṇātmanām /(2, 1501)
yatra hy upāyavināyād devā api bhavanti hi //(2, 1501)

atha bhagavān avalokiteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ svakulam utpādya, sarvatathāgatebhyaḥ sarvasattvābhayārthaprāptyuttamasiddhivajradharmatājñānābhijñāvāptiphalahetor niryātya, sarvajagadvinayaṃ nāma mahāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //:(2, 1502)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam /(2, 1503)
vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ jagadvinayasaṃjñitam //(2, 1503)

caturaśraṃ caturdvāraṃ catustoraṇaśobhitam /(2, 1504)
catuḥsūtrasamāyuktaṃ paṭṭasragdāmabhūṣitam //(2, 1504)

sarvamaṇḍalakoṇeṣu dvāraniryūhasaṃdhiṣu /(2, 1505)
khacitaṃ vajraratnais tu sūtrayed bāhyamaṇḍalam //(2, 1505)

tasyābhyantarataḥ sūtraṃ caturaśraṃ parikṣipet /(2, 1506)
dvitīyaṃ dvārakoṇaṃ tu padmākāraṃ prakalpayet //(2, 1506)

aṣṭastambhaprayogeṇa padmam aṣṭadalaṃ likeht /(2, 1507)
tasya keśaramadhye tu buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet //(2, 1507)

tatredaṃ buddhapraveśahṛdayaṃ bhavati //:(2, 1508)
buddha huṃ //(2, 1508)

buddhasya sarvato lekhyāḥ padmamadhyapratiṣṭhitāḥ /(2, 1509)
vajraṃ ratnāṃ tathā padmaṃ viśvapadmaṃ tathaiva ca //(2, 1509)

tatraiṣāṃ hrḍayāni bhavanti //:(2, 1510)
oṃ /(2, 1510)
huṃ /(2, 1510)
dhiḥ /(2, 1510)
kṛḥ //(2, 1510)

vajravegena niṣkramya jagadvinayamaṇḍalam /(2, 1511)
tatra lokeśvaraḥ kāryaḥ sarvarūpān samutsṛjan //(2, 1511)

tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu vajragarvādiyogataḥ /(2, 1512)
buddhādayo mahāsattvān padmacihnadharān likhet //(2, 1512)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(2, 1513)
āḥ //(2, 1513)
oṃ tathāgatadharma hūṃ //(2, 1513)
oṃ vajrapadmāṅkuśakośadhara vajrasattva hūṃ phaṭ //(2, 1513)

oṃ māraya māraya padmakusumāyudhadharāmoghaśara hoḥ //(2, 1514)
oṃ padmasaṃbhavapadmahasta sādhu hūṃ //(2, 1514)

vajravegena cākramya dvitīyamaṇḍalaṃ tathā /(2, 1515)
tatra madhye samālekhyaṃ jaṭāmadhye tathāgatam //(2, 1515)

tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu bhṛkuṭyādiprayogataḥ /(2, 1516)
padmacihnadharā lekhyā yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ //(2, 1516)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //(2, 1517)
hūṃ //(2, 1517)
oṃ padmabhṛkuṭi taṭi tra //(2, 1517)
oṃ padmasūryajvāla hūṃ //(2, 1517)

oṃ padmamaṇiketudhara candraprahlādayāvalokiteśvara dehi me sattvārthān śīghraṃ samaya hūṃ //(2, 1518)
oṃ padmāṭṭahāsaikādaśamukha haḥ haḥ haḥ hūṃ //(2, 1518)

vajravegena cākramya tṛtīyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tathā /(2, 1519)
samāpannaṃ mahāsattvaṃ likhet padmapratiṣṭhitam //(2, 1519)

tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /(2, 1520)
padmālokādiyogena mahāsattvān niveśayet //(2, 1520)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(2, 1521)
dha //(2, 1521)
oṃ tārāpadmāvalokaya māṃ samayasattva hūṃ //(2, 1521)
oṃ padmakumāra padmaśaktidhara khaḍgena cchinda cchinda hūṃ phaṭ //(2, 1521)

oṃ padmalīlakaṇṭhāśaṃkhacakragadāpadmapāṇi vyāghracarmanivasana kṛṣṇasarpakṛtayajñopvītājinacarmavāmaskandhottarīya nārāyaṇarūpadhara trinetra muñcāṭṭahāsaṃ praveśaya samayān dehi me siddhim avalokiteśvara hūṃ //(2, 1522)
oṃ brahmapadmasaṃbhava japa japa padmabhāṣa hūṃ //(2, 1523)

vajravegena cākramya caturthamaṇḍalaṃ tathā /(2, 1524)
tatra padmaṃ caturvakraṃ padmaśūladharaṃ likhet //(2, 1524)

tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu vajranṛtyādiyogataḥ /(2, 1525)
padmacihnadharā lekhyā mahāsattvā yathāvidhi //(2, 1525)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(2, 1526)
trīḥ //(2, 1526)
oṃ padmanarteśvara naṭa naṭa pūjaya sarvatathāgatān vajrakarmasamayākarṣaya praveśaya bandhayāveśaya sarvakarmasiddhiṃ me prayacchāvalokiteśvara hūṃ //(2, 1526)

oṃ abhayaṃdadāvalokite.vara rakṣa bandha padmakavacaṃ samaya haṃ //(2, 1527)
oṃ mahāpracaṇḍaviśvarūpavikaṭapadmadaṃṣṭrākarālabhīṣaṇavaktra trāsaya sarvān padmayakṣa khāda khāda dhik dhik dhik //(2, 1527)
oṃ padmamuṣṭisamayas tvaṃ bandha hūṃ phaṭ //(2, 1527)

vajravegena cākramya sarvakoṇeṣu saṃlikhet /(2, 1528)
vajralāsyādiyogena padmalāsyādidevatāḥ //(2, 1528)

tatraitā mudrā bhavanti //:(2, 1529)
oṃ padmalāsye rāgaya mahādevi rāgapūjāsamaye hūṃ //(2, 1529)
oṃ padmamāle 'bhiṣiñcābhiṣekapūjāsamaye hūṃ //(2, 1529)

oṃ padmagīte gāda gītapūjāsamaye hūṃ //(2, 1530)
oṃ padmanṛtye nṛtya sarvapūjāpravartanasamaye hūṃ //(2, 1530)

vajravegena niṣkramya bāhyamaṇḍalasaṃnidhau /(2, 1531)
catasraḥ padmadhūpādyāḥ pūjādevyaḥ samālikhet //(2, 1531)

tatraitāḥ pūjāmudrā bhavanti //(2, 1532)
oṃ padmadhūpapūjāsamaye prahlādaya padmakuladayite mahāgaṇi padmarati hūṃ //(2, 1532)
oṃ padmapuṣpapūjāsamaye padmavāsini mahāśriye padmakulapratīhāri sarvārthān sādhaya hūṃ //(2, 1532)

oṃ dīpapūjāsamaye padmakulasundari mahādūty ālokaṃ saṃjanaya padmasarasvati hūṃ //(2, 1533)
oṃ gandhapūjāsamaye mahāpadmakulaceṭi kuru sarvakarmāṇi me padmasiddhi hūṃ //(2, 1533)

tato gaṇādayaḥ sarve padmadvāracatuṣṭaye /(2, 1534)
samālekhyā yathāvat tu teeṣāṃ ca hṛdayārthata iti //(2, 1534)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:(2, 1535)
oṃ hayagrīvamahāpadmāṅkuśākarṣaya śīghraṃ sarvapadmakulasamayān padmāṅkuśadhara hūṃ jjaḥ //(2, 1535)

oṃ amoghapadmapāśakrodhākarṣaya praveśaya mahāpaśupatiyamavaruṇakuberabrahmaveśadhara padmakulasamayān huṃ huṃ //(2,1536)
oṃ padmasphoṭa bandha sarvapadmakulasamayān śīghraṃ hūṃ vaṃ //(2, 1536)
oṃ ṣaṃmukhasanatkumāraveśadhara padmaghaṇṭayāveśaya sarvapadmakulasamayān sarvamudrāṃ bandhaya sarvasiddhayo me prayaccha padmāveśa aḥ aḥ aḥ aḥ //(2, 1537)

athātra sarvajagadvinayapadmamaṇḍale vidhivistaro bhavati //(2, 1538)

tatrādita eva padmācāryo vajrapadmasamayamudrāṃ baddhvā, yathāvat praviśya, vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena karma kuryād ebhir hṛdayaiḥ //(2, 1539)
oṃ padmasphoṭādhitiṣṭha aḥ //(2, 1539)

tatas tathaivājñāṃ mārgya, tathaiva samayamudrayā svayam abhiṣicya, padmavigrahaṃ gṛhya, svapadmanāmoccārya, padmāṅkuśādibhiś ca karma kṛtvā, tatas tābhir eva dharmamudrābhir mahāsattvān sādhayet //(2, 1540)
tatas tathaiva siddhir iti //(2, 1540)

tataḥ padmaśiṣyān praveśayet //(2, 1541)

tatrāditaḥ padmaśiṣyāya śapathahṛdayaṃ dadyāt //:(2, 1542)
padmasattvaḥ svayaṃ te 'dya hṛdaye samavasthitaḥ /(2, 1542)
nirbhidya tat kṣaṇam yāyād yadi brūyād imaṃ nayam //(2, 1542)
iti kartavyam /.(2, 1542)

tato brūyāt /:(2, 1543)
na kasya cit tvayedaṃ guhyavidhivistaram ākhyeyam /(2, 1543)
mā te narakapatanaṃ bhavet /(2, 1543)
viṣamāparihāreṇa ca kālakriyāṃ kṛtvā narakapatanaṃ syād iti //(2, 1543)

tataḥ samayamudrāṃ bandhayed anena hṛdayena //(2, 1544)
oṃ vajrapadmasamayas tvam //(2, 1544)

tataḥ śvetavastrottarīyaḥ śvetanaktakena mukhaṃ baddhvā praveśayed anena hṛdayena //(2, 1545)
oṃ padmasamaya hūṃ //(2, 1545)

tato yathāvat karma kṛtvā, padmavigrahaṃ pāṇau dātavyam //(2, 1546)
oṃ padmahasta vajradharmatāṃ pālaya //(2, 1546)

tena vaktavyaṃ kīdṛśī sā vajradharmateti //(2, 1547)

tato vaktavyam /:(2, 1548)
yathā raktam idaṃ padmaṃ gotradoṣair na lipyate /(2, 1548)
bhāvayet sarvaśuddhiṃ tu tathā pāpair na lipyate //(2, 1548)
iyam atra dharmatā //(2, 15489

tataḥ padmakulamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //(2, 1549)
padmaṃ tu hṛdaye likhya padmabhāvanayā hṛdi /(2, 1549)
padmaśriyaṃ vaśīkuryāt kiṃ punaḥ strījano 'dharaḥ //(2, 1549)

buddhabimbaṃ lalāṭe tu likhyābhīkṣṇaṃ tu bhāvayet / (2,1550)
tayā bhāvanayā śīghram abhiṣekam svāpnute //(2, 1550)

buddhabimbaṃ mukhe viddhvā jihvāyāṃ tu prabhāvayet |
svayaṃ sarasvatīdevī mukhe tiṣṭhaty abhīkṣṇaśaḥ || (1551)

padmam uṣṇīṣamadhye tu sthāpayitvā samāhitaḥ /(2, 1552)
bhāvayan padmam uṣṇīṣe khegāmī sa vaśaṃ nayed iti //(2,1552)

tatraitāni hṛdayāni bhavanti //(2,1553)
padmaśriyaṃ vaśam ānaya hoḥ //(2,1553)
padmābhiṣekaṃ prayaccha vaṃ //(2,1553)
padmasarsvati śodhaya hūṃ //(2,1553)
padmordhvagān vaśīkuru jjaḥ //(2,1553)

kuḍye vāpy atha vākāśe bhāvayan padmam uttamam /(2,1554)
anayā sarvasattvānāṃ vaśīkaraṇam uttamam //(2,1554)

ākāśe vānyadeśe vā bhāvayan padmam uttamam /(2,1555)
yadā paśyet tadā gṛhṇa kāmyād adreśyatāṃ vrajet //(2,1555)

kuḍye vāpy atha vākāśe viśvapadmaṃ samādhayet /(2,1556)
paśyan gṛhṇa pradānaṃ viśvarūpī tadā bhavet //(2,1556)

ākāśe vānyadeśe vā vajrapadmaṃ tu bhāvayet /(2,1557)
taṃ tu gṛhṇan kṣaṇāc caiva padmavidyādharo bhavet //(2,1557)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //(2,1558)
oṃ sarvajagadvaśitājñānapadmāviśa aḥ //(2,1558)
oṃ jñānapadma tiṣṭhādreśyaṃ kuru vaṃ //(2,1558)
oṃ samādhiviśvapadma tiṣṭha viśvarūpyaṃ darśa bhagavan dhaḥ //(2,1558)
oṃ samādhivajrapadmaṃ tiṣṭhottiṣṭha śīghraṃ hrīḥ // (2,1558)

loke.varaṃ samīlikhya maṇḍalādiṣu sarvataḥ /
puras tasya samākarṣet hayagrīvāgryamudrayā //
lokeśvaraṃ (lokeṣvaraṃ, ed) samālikhya maṇḍalādiṣu tasya vai /
amoghapāśamudrayā vaśīkuryāj jagat sa tu //(2,1559)

lokeśvaraṃ samālikhya maṇḍalādiṣu tasya vai /
amoghapāśamudrayā vaśīkuryāj jagat sa tu //(2,1560)

loke.varaṃ samālkijya maṇḍalādiṣu sarvataḥ /
puras tasya tu bandhnīyāt padmasphoṭāgramudrayā //(2,1561)

lokeśvaraṃ samālikhya maṇḍalādiṣu tasya vai /
purataḥ padmaghaṇṭayā sarvāveśanam uttamam iti //(2,1562)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //
oṃ padmāṅkuśākarṣaya sarvamahāsattvān hūṃ jjaḥ //
oṃ amoghapāśakrodha hūṃ hoḥ //
oṃ padmasphoṭa vaṃ //
oṃ padmaghaṇṭāveśaya sarvam aḥ // (2,1563)

catuḥpadmamukhaṃ sattvaṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /
svam ātmānaṃ tataḥ siddho bahurūpī bhavet kṣanāt //(2,1564)

bhāvayan padmapadmaṃ tu svam ātmānaṃ tathātmanā /
vajradharmasamādhistho prāpnoti padam akṣaram //(2,1565)

lokeśvarajaṭāmadhye bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /
buddhabimbaṃ svam ātmānam amitāyuḥsamo bhavet //(2,1566)
%amitāyuḥsamo] em., amitāyusamo, ed.

bhāvayan svayam ātmanā viśvarūpasamādhinā /
viśvarūpasamādhistho lokeśvarasamo bhaved iti //(2,1567)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //
padmaviśva /
dharmakāyapadma /
buddhābhiṣeka /
lokeśvara // (2, 1568)

tato mahāmaṇḍalasarvamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //

tatra prathamaṃ tāvan mahāmudrājñānaṃ bhavati //
candramaṇḍalamadhyasthān yathālekhyānusārataḥ /
padmapratiṣṭhasattvān svaṃ bhāvayet svayam ātmaneti //

athāsāṃ karma bhavati //
baddhvā buddhamahāmudrām amitāyusamo bhavet /
vajrapadmaṃ samādhāya lokeśvarasamo bhavet //

buddhābhiṣekaṃ baddhvā vai sugataiḥ so 'bhiṣicyate /
padmapadmā samādhiṃ tu dadyād viśvā suvaiśvatām //

vaiśvarūpyaṃ vineyāṃs tu buddharatnābhiṣekadaḥ /
padmasattvisamādhiṃ tu padmakrodheśvarīṃ śriyam //

vajralokeśvarīṃ siddhim uttamāṃ padmarāgiṇīm /
buddheśvarī tu buddhatvaṃ vajrapadmā susiddhidā //

kāmeśvarī surāgitvaṃ dadyāt tuṣṭiṃ tu sādhutā /
bhṛkutiḥ krodhaśamarī padmasūryā sutejadā //

padmacandrā mahākāntiṃ dadyād dhāsā suhāsatām /
tarayā cottarā siddhiḥ saubhāgyaṃ padma khaḍgayā //

nīlakaṇṇthā mahākarṣā siddhiṃ paṇḍalavāsinī /
padmanatreśvarī siddhim abhayā abhayaṃdadā //

pracaṇḍā duṣṭadamanī padmamuṣṭiḥ susādhikā /
lāsyā ratiṃ dhanaṃ mālā svaraṃ gītā sukhaṃ nṛtyā // (2, 1578)

dhūpā hlādaṃ sukhaṃ puṣpā dīpā dṛṣṭiṃ gandhā sugandhatām /
hayagrīvā samākarṣā amoghā tu vaśaṃkarī //

padmasphoṭā mahābandhā sarvāveśā tu ghaṇṭiketi // (2, 1580)

tataḥ padmakulasamayamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //
vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya samāṅguṣṭhāntyasañjanāt /
mudreyaṃ dharmasamayā buddhadharmapradāyikā //

vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya samāgryā nāma madhyamā /
buddhavidyottamasyeyaṃ mudrā buddhatvadāyikā //

vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya madhyamā vajrasaṃyutā /
vajravidyottamasyeyaṃ mudrā vajratvadāyikā // (2, 1583)

sā eva maṇimadhyā tu vajraratnapradāyikā /
madhyakuḍmalayogena padmasiddhipradāyikā //

vajrāñjaliṃ tu saṃdhāya lintu vajrakarmakarī bhavet /
dharmavajraṃ samādhāya samayaḥ sidhyate kṣaṇāt //

vajrabandhaṃ samāgraṃ tu buddhasiddhipradāyikā /
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sattvamudrāṃ viśeṣataḥ //

vajrāñjaliṃ samādhāya samadhyotthitā tathā /
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhavikacā viśvapadmeti kīrtitā //

sā evāṅguṣṭhaparyaṅkā kuñcitāgrāgryavigrahā /
madhyavajrajaṭāmūrdhani jaṭābandheti kīrtitā //

vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya samāṅguṣṭham adhargatam /
tarjanī dvayasaṃkocā samutthānā samādhitaḥ //

samāñjaliṃ samādhāya tarjanī vajrapīḍitā /
vikasitāṅguṣṭhamukhayor mudrāmogheśvarasya tu // (2, 1590)

vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya samuttānaṃ tu bandhayet /
samāṅguṣṭhakṛtā padme padmabuddheti kīrtitā //

aṅguṣṭhavajratāgrābhyām aṅkuśaṃ khaḍgam eva ca /
antyadvayavikāsā ca madhyānāmāgrakuḍmalā //

samāñjaliṃ samādhāya valitāṅguṣṭhakuñcitā /
tarjanyā tarjanīṃ gṛhyākarṣanyet padmavāṇayā //

samāñjaliṃ tathottānāṃ bandhayet sādhumudrayā /
sādhukārās dātavyāḥ sādhupadmeti kīrtitā //

samāñjaliṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kuñcitāgryā mukhasthitā /
kaniṣṭhābhyāṃ tu vikacā padmabhṛkuṭir ucyate // (2, 1595)

vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya hṛdayaṃ tu prasārayet /
padmasūryeti vikhyātā sarvāṅgulisumaṇḍalā //

samāñjaliṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya tarjanīṣṭhaṃ maṇīkṛtā /
padmaratnadhvajāgrī tu  mūdhni bāhuprasāritā //

vajrabandhaṃ śiromūrdhni prasāryāgramukhaiḥ saha /
svamukhenāṭṭahāsena ekādaśamukhī bhavet // (2, 1598)

samādhipadmāṃ saṃdhāya samāṅguṣṭhasamutthitā /
padmatārasya mudreyaṃ sarvasiddhipradāyikā //

padmatārasya mudrā tu padmayogāgryabandhanāt /
padmakhaḍgasya mudreyaṃ khaḍgākāranijanāt //

kuḍmalāntyamahāpadmā stabdhāṅguṣṭhagadā tathā /
kuñcitāgryamahāśaṃkhā vajrabandhena cakritā //

vajrāñjalīṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya dakṣiṇ' oṃkāraveṣṭitā /
vāmāgryāṅguṣṭhajāpāt tu sarvāgravikacāmbujā //

vajrāñjalīṃ samādhāya vāmadakṣiṇatas tathā /
nṛtyan salīlavalitā mūrdhnisthā nṛtyapadminī //

vajrāñjaliṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya sarvāgravikacā tathā /
parivartya tu padmena hṛdi sthāpya dṛḍhaṃ karī //

vajrāñjalīṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya guhyayakṣaprayogataḥ /
prasāritāñjalipuṭā mukhasthā padmayakṣiṇī //

vajramuṣṭiṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kuñcayitvā tu madhyame /
svāṅguṣṭhapṛṣṭhanihite padmamusṭir udāhṛtā // (2, 1606)

vajradhātuprayogeṇa vajrāñjalisamutthitā /
