sarvapūjāgryadevīnāṃ samayāgryas tu bandhayet //

vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya saṃdhayet tarnajīdvayam /
saṃkocāt purataḥ saṃdhed hayagrīveti kīrtitā //

padmāñjaliṃ samādhāya tarjanīgranthibandhanā /
amoghapāśamudreyaṃ tarjanyaṅguṣṭhaśaṅkalā //

padmāñjaliṃ samādhāya vajrāveśaprayogataḥ /
aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ tu saṃpīḍyo kaniṣṭhānāmikāntarāv iti // (2, 1610)

atha padmakuladharmamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //
hrī /
grī /
prī /
hī /
śrī /
śī /
dī /
hiḥ /
gī /
dhī /
krī /
vī /
vi (or viḥ)/
rī /
ṣṭrī /
aḥ //
padmamuṣṭiṃ dvidhīkṛtya karmamudrāḥ sa sādhayed iti // (2, 1611)

sarvatathāgatadharmasamayān mahākalparājāt sakalajagadvinayamahāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ //



atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatadharmadhāraṇīsamayasaṃbhavamudrādhiṣṭhānapadmaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //
oṃ sarvatathāgatadharmasamaye hūṃ //

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ imāṃ svakulasaṃbhavāṃ vidyottamām abhāṣāt //
oṃ vajrasamaye hūṃ //

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvo mahā sattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //
oṃ maṇiratnasamaye hūṃ //

atha vajranetro bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //
oṃ padmasamaye hūṃ //

atha vajraviśo bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //
oṃ karmasamaye hūṃ // (2, 1617)

atha bhagavān āryāvalokiteśvaro bodhisattva idaṃ svakulasamayamudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat // (2, 1618)

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mudrāmaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ padmaguhyam iti smṛtam // (2, 1619)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	tasya madhye supadme vai vajradhātvīśvarīṃ likhet // (1620)

	tasya [vai] sarvapārśveṣu samayāgryo yathopari /
	dharmavajryādayo lekhyāḥ svavidyābhiḥ samanvitāḥ // (1621)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //
	oṃ sarvatathāgatadharmeśvari hūṃ //
	oṃ dharmasamaye vajrapadmini hūṃ // (1622)

	oṃbuddhābhiṣekaratnasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ tārāsamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ viśvamukhe hūṃ // (1623)

	vajravegena niṣkramya vi.varūpāgryamaṇḍalam /
	tatra madhye likhet padmaṃ padmais tu parivāritam // (1624)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu padmamudrāpratiṣṭhitāḥ /
	padmacihnāḥ samāliekhyāḥ svamudrāḥ sugatātmanām // (1625)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:
	hrīḥ oṃ padmatathāgata //
	oṃ samantabhadrapadmavajrāṅkuśakośadhāriṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ padmarati //
	oṃ padmatuṣṭi // (1626)

	vajravegena cākramya dvitīye maṇḍale tathā /
	buddhābhiṣekā samālekhyā jaṭāmadhye mahāmbujam // (1627)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	padmacihna samopetāḥ samayāgryo niveśayet // (1628)

tatrāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	śrīḥ
	oṃ bhṛkuṭi taṭi vai taṭi padme hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajvāle // (1629)

	oṃ saumini padme hūṃ //
	oṃ padmahāsiny ekādaśavaktre diri diri iṭṭe vaṭṭe cale pracale kusumadhare ili praviśa siddhiṃ me prayaccha hūṃ // (1630)

	vajravegena cākramya tṛtīyaṃ maṇḍalam tathā /
	tatra madhye supadme tu padmamudrāṃ niveśayet // (1631)

	tathaiva sarvapārśveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	padmacihnasamopetāḥ padmasaṃsthās tu saṃlikhet // (1632)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:
	dhīḥ //
	oṃ tāre tut tāre hūṃ //
	oṃ dhī hūṃ // (1633)

	oṃ padmacakraśaṃkhagadādhāriṇi nīlakaṇṭhe sidhya sidhya hūṃ //
	oṃ paṇḍaravāsini padmasaṃbhave vada vada hūṃ // (1634)

	vajravegena cākramya caturthe maṇḍalottame /
	padmamadhye likhet padmaṃ jvālāmālākulaprabham // (1635)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	padmacihnāḥ samālekhyāḥ padmamadhyapratiṣṭhitāḥ // (1636)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:
	strīḥ //
	oṃ padmanatreśvari pūjaya sarvātathāgatān naṭa naṭa hūṃ //
	oṃ abhyaye padmakavacabandhe rakṣa māṃ hūṃ haṃ // (1637)

	oṃ mahāpracaṇḍi padmayakṣiṇi viśvarūpadhāriṇi bhīṣāpaya sarvaduṣṭān khāda khāda hūṃ phaṭ //
	oṃ padmamuṣṭi aḥ aḥ // (1638)

	vajravegena cākramya buddhapūjāḥ samālikhet /
	padmāṅkuśyādayo mudrāḥ padmacihnāḥ samāsataḥ // iti // (1639)

athāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:
	oṃ padmaratipūje hoḥ //
	oṃ padmābhiṣekapūje raṭ //
	oṃ padmagītapūje gīḥ //
	oṃ padmanṛtyapūje kṛt // (1640)

	oṃ dhūpapadmini hūṃ //
	oṃ padmapuṣpi hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakulasundari dharmāloke pūjaya hūṃ //
	oṃ padmagandhe hūṃ // (1641)

pūjādevyaḥ //
	oṃ padmāṅkuśy ākarṣaya mahāpadmakulān hayagrīvasamaye hūṃ jaḥ //
	oṃ amoghapāśakrodhasamaye praviśa prav.eśaya sarvasamayāṃ hūṃ // (1642)

	oṃ padmaśaṅkale vaṃ //
	oṃ padmaghaṇṭādhāri śīghram āveśaya samayāṃ ṣaṇmukhi aḥ // (1643)

atha mudrāmaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā, padmaśiṣyān yathāvat praveśayet //
evaṃ vaden:
	na tvayā kasya cid vaktavyaṃ yad atra guhyam /
	mā te narakapatanaṃ bhaved du.khāni cātra janmanīti // (1644)

tataḥ samāveśyaivaṃ vadet /:
	tvatcakṣuṣpathi kīdṛśo 'vabhāsaḥ / (1645)
%or -cakṣurgocare, or tvadlocanagocare, or -pathi

tad yathā vadati tathā siddhir iti / (1646)

tad yadi śvetālokaṃ paśyet tasyottamasiddhijñānaṃ śikṣayet /
atha pītaṃ paśyet tasyārthotpattijñānaṃ śikṣayet /
atha raktaṃ paśyet tato 'nurāgaṇajñānaṃ śikṣayet /
atha kṛṣṇaṃ paśyet tato 'bhicārukajñānaṃ śikṣayet /
atha victraṃ paśyet mukhabandhaṃ muktvā, (1647)

iti jñātvā, yathāvan mukhabandhaṃ muktvā, (1648)

yathābhājanatayā jñānāny utpādayet /
mudrājñānaṃ ca śikṣayet / (1649)

evaṃ vajradhātvādiṣv api sarvamaṇḍaleṣu yathābhājanatayā mudrājñānāni śikṣayed, iyaṃ parīkṣā // (1650)

athottamasiddhiniṣpattijñānaṃ bhavati //:
	lokeśvaramahāsattvaṃ viśvarūpaṃ svam ātmānā /
	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrām agryāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (1651)

	buddhābhiṣekasamayāṃ dṛḍhīkṛtvā samāhitaḥ /
	bhāvayaṃs tu svam ātmānam agryāṃ siddhim avāpnute // (1652)

	padmapadmamahāsattvaṃ bhāvayet svayam ātmanā /
	ātmānam uttamāṃ siddhiṃ prāpnoti susamāhitaḥ // (1653)

	amogheśvaramayīṃ karmamudrāṃ svayaṃ bhuvaḥ /
	sādhaya vidhivac chīghram agryāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // iti // (1654)

athaiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ padmasattvo 'haṃ sidhya hoḥ //
	oṃ buddhābhiṣeko 'haṃ sidhya māṃ //
	oṃ dharmasamādhir ahaṃ sidhya hoḥ //
	oṃ amogheśvaro 'haṃ sidhya māṃ // (1655)

tato 'rthaniṣpattijñānaṃ bhavati //:
	hiraṇyaṃ tu mukhe viddhvā bhāvayet svayam ātmanā /
	viśveśvaramahāmudrām ekaṃ bhūyāt sahasraśaḥ // (1656)

	suvarṇatolakaṃ gṛhya samayāgryā mahādṛḍham /
	bhāvayan svayam ātmānam eko bhūyāt sahasraśaḥ // (1657)

	muktāphalaṃ mukhe viddhvā bhāvayet svayam ātmanā /
	lokeśvaraṃ svam ātmānam eko bhūyāt sahasraśaḥ // (1658)

	sarvaratnāni saṃgṛhya pāṇibhyāṃ karmamudrayā /
	bhāvayan svayam ātmānam eko bhūyāt sahasraśaḥ // iti // (1659)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ padmahiraṇyaprada huṃ jjaḥ //
	oṃ padmasuvarṇaprada huṃ jjaḥ //
	oṃ padmamuktāprada huṃ jjaḥ //
	oṃ padmasarvaratnaprada huṃ jjaḥ // (1660)

athānurāgaṇajñānaṃ bhavati //:
	viśveśvaramahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /
	padmaṃ gṛhya puraḥ sthāti yasya so 'syānurajyati // (1661)

	raktapadmaṃ dṛḍhaṃ gṛhya mahāsamayamudrayā /
	bhāvayan svayam ātmānaṃ rāgayet sarvayoṣitaḥ / (1662)

	bhāvayet svayam ātmānaṃ padmaṃ gṛhya yathā tathā /
	nirīkṣed vajradṛṣṭyā vai sarvalokaṃ sa rāgayet // (1663)

	karmamudrāprayogeṇa padmaṃ gṛhya yathāvidhi /
	karābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃs taṃ tu rāgayet sarvayoṣitaḥ // iti // (1664)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ viśveśvaramahāpadma hoḥ //
	oṃ samayapadma hoḥ //
	oṃ yogapadma hoḥ //
	oṃ karmapadma hoḥ // (1665)

[athābhicārukajñānaṃ bhavati //:]
	viśveśvaramahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /
	chinded yasya puraḥ padmaṃ tasya mṛtyuḥ kṣaṇād bhavet // (1666)

	padmaṃ gṛhya dṛḍhaṃ samyak samayāgryā tayaiva hi /
	sphoṭayet taṃ tu sudṛḍhaṃ yasya nāmnā sa naśyati // (1667)

	samādhimudrāṃ saṃdhyāya padmaṃ gṛhya yathā tathā /
	yasya nāmnā tu padmaṃ vai chindet sa tu vinaśyati // (1668)

	karmamudrāprayogeṇa padmaṃ gṛhya yathāvidhi /
	sphoṭayed yasya saṃkruddhaḥ sphuṭet tasya tu jīvitam // iti // (1669)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāpadmacheda (chedaya, Ch) māraya hoḥ phaṭ //
	oṃ mahāpadmasphoṭa nāśaya (sphoṭaya nāśaya, Ch) raṭ phaṭ // (1670)

	oṃ dharmapadmacheda (chedaya, Ch) vināśaya dhṛt phaṭ //
	oṃ karmapadmasphoṭa sphoṭaya (sphoṭaya, Ch) jīvitam asya kṛt phaṭ // (1671)

tato dharmasamayarahasyamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:
	padmaṃ tu yoṣitāṃ cintya vajraṃ tasyopari svayam /
	rāmayan padmapadmāgryā samāpattyā tu sidhyati // (1672)

	padmaṃ tu yoṣitāṃ cintya buddhaṃ tasyopari svayam /
	rāmyam buddhamukuṭāṃ bhāvayan so 'sya sidhyati // (1673)

	padmaṃ tu yoṣitāṃ cintya padmaṃ tasyopari svayam /
	rāgayan padmapadmāgrīṃ śuddhāṃ siddhim avāpnute // (1674)

	padmaṃ tu yoṣitāṃ cintya viśvaṃ tasyopari svayam /
	rāmayan viśvapadmāgrīṃ viśvāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // iti // (1675)

tatraiṣāṃ hḍayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ vajrapadmasaṃyoga sādhaya hrīḥ //
	oṃ buddhamukuṭasaṃyoga sādhaya śrīḥ //
	oṃ padmapadmasaṃyoga sādhaya dhīḥ //
	oṃ viśvapadmasaṃyoga sādhaya strīḥ // (1676)

tato yathāvat padmakulaguhyamahāmudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:
	kuḍmalāñjalir agrasya vajrakrodhāṅgulī dvike /
	dvyagrā maṇis tathā padmaṃ vajrabandhaṃ tathaiva ca // (1677)

	vajrabandhāṃ samānīya samamadhyāṅkurotthitā /
	tarjanyanāmasaṃkocā mudrā śakyamuner dṛḍhā // (1678)

	dharmavajrā hṛdisthā tu parivartya lalāṭagā /
	samādhiyogāc cotsaṅge parivartya tu mūrdhagā // (1679)

	vajradhātvīśvarīṃ baddhvā caityaṃ padmaprayogataḥ /
	saṃdhayen madhyamābhyāṃ tu buddhapadmeti kīrtitā // (1680)

	sā evāṅkuṣṭhavajrā tu dvyagrakhaḍgāṅkuśī tathā /
	padmavajradharasyaitā guhyamudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // (1681)

	sā evāṅguṣṭhamuktā tu tarjanyā tarjanī grahā /
	valitā suratiḥ proktā sādhukāryā tathaiva ca // (1682)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya samāṅguṣṭhapraveṣitā /
	kuñcitāgryamukhasthā tu bhṛkuṭyāṃ madhyapadminī // (1683)

	sā eva hṛdaye caiva sūryamaṇḍaladarśikā /
	dhvajabandhena sā eva śiraḥpṛṣṭhe prasāritā // (1684)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kuñcitāgryāgravigrahā /
	tathaiva padmakhaḍgā tu padmayogāgryasaṃdhanāt // (1685)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya vāmāṅguṣṭhapraveśanāt /
	śaṃkham aṅguṣṭhadaṇḍotthā sarvāgrotthāntyapadminī // (1686)

	sā eva sarvasaṃkocā kaniṣṭhā padmasaṃyutā /
	akṣamālāgragaṇanī dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhayogataḥ // (1687)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kaniṣṭhā padmasaṃyutā /
	samāgrā padmanetrā tu pranartan parivartitā // (1688)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kaniṣṭhāgra padmasaṃyutā /
	kuñictāgrā sugāḍhaṃ tu dvyaṅguṣṭhakavacīkṛtā // iti // (1689)

	sā evāṅguṣṭhadaṃṣṭrā tu samāṅguṣṭhapraveśitā /
	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi samayāgryo niruttarāḥ // (1690)

	vajrabandhaṃ tale kṛtvā tarjanī padmasaṃsthitā /
	aṅguṣṭhā baddhaparyaṅkā guhyaviśveśvarī smṛtā // (1691)

	tathaiva vajrabandhena kaniṣṭhamadhyabandhitā /
	aṅguṣṭhamukhayor vajraṃ jaṭāmadhye tathāgatam // (1692)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu padmam aṅguṣṭhasaṃdhitam /
	kṛtvā tu mukhatodvāntaṃ (kṛtvā mukhata udvāntaṃ ?)
	sthitotsaṅge samādhinā // (1693)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu mukhataḥ samasaṃdhitā /
	sarvāṅgulyo dṛḍhīkṛtya tarjanī vajrasaṃyutā // (1694)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu tarjanī padmasaṃdhitā /
	aṅguṣṭhā baddhaparyaṅkā madhyasaṃkocavigrahā // (1695)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu vajram aṅguṣṭhasaṃdhitā /
	khaḍgāṅkuśī tathā grābhyāṃ kaniṣṭhā padmasaṃyutā // (1696)

	tathaiva valitāṃ kṛtvā tarjanyaṅguṣṭhasaṃgraham /
	utthitāṃ tarjanīṃ vāmāṃ karṣayet sudṛḍhaṃ tathā // (1697)

	sā eva tu samīkṛtya tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayogataḥ /
	sādhukārapradātrī tu padmatuṣṭer mahātmanaḥ // (1698)

	tathaiva vajrabandhaṃ tu sarvāgramukhasaṃdhitaṃ /
	dvyaṅguṣṭhamukhapīḍaṃ tu samāgryā saṃniveśitam // (1699)

	sā eva hṛdi sūryā tu mūrdhni padmadhvajīkṛtā /
	parivartya ca hāsā tu sthitā padmāṭṭahāsinī // (1700)

	vajrabandhaṃ tale kṛtvā dharmavajrāgrayogataḥ /
	kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhasaṃdhī tu tārāyāḥ samayo hy ayam // (1701)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu jyeṣṭhābhyāṃ khaḍgapadminī /
	talacakrā tathaiveha japadātrī tathaiveha japadātrī tathaiva ca // (1702)

	tathaiva vajrabandhā tu khaṭakadvayamokṣitā /
	punaś ca hṛdayabandhe guhyarakṣeti kīrtitā // (1703)

	tathaiva vajrabandhe tu kaniṣṭhā padmasaṃyutā /
	tarjanī dṛḍhasaṃkocā vikacāṅguṣṭhadaṃṣṭriṇī // (1704)

	sā eva muṣṭiyogena dvyaṅguṣṭhamukhapīḍitā /
	padmaguhyamahāmuṣṭisamayāgrī prakalpitā // (1705)

	sarvāsām eva cānyāsāṃ padmalāsyādisaṃjñitām /
	vajrabandhaṃ tale kṛtvā bandhas tādṛśa eva hi // iti // (1706)

tataḥ padmakulaguhyadharmamudrā bhavanti //:
	hrāḥ//
	grā //
	prā //
	hā //
	śrā //
	śā //
	dāḥ //
	haḥ //
	gā //
	dhā //
	krā //
	vā //
	va //
	rā //
	ṣṭrā
	maḥ //
karmamudrāḥ samāsena muṣṭir eva dvidhīkṛteti // // (1707)

sarvatathāgatadharmasamayān mahākalparājāt padmaguhyamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (1708)


[dharma-]jñāna-maṇḍala-vidhi-vistara

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatadharmajñānasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhānapadaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ dharmasamādhijñānatathāgata hūṃ // (1709)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ imaṃ svakuladharmasaṃbhavaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:
	oṃ vajradharma hūṃ // (1710)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:
	oṃ ratnadharma hūṃ // (1711)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:
	oṃ dharmadharma hūṃ // (1712)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:
	oṃ karmadharma hūṃ // (1713)

atha āryāvalokiteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ svadharmamaṇḍalam abhāṣat // (1714)
	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jñānamaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ dharmajñānam iti smṛtam // (1715)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	tasya madhye samālekhyaṃ jñānavajre tathāgatam // (1716)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu mahāsattvā yathāvidhi /
	viśveśvarādayo lekhyāḥ samāpannāḥ samāhitāḥ // iti // (1717)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ jñānabuddha hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānaviśveśvara hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānabuddhamukuṭa hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānadharmeśvara hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānāmogheśvara hūṃ // (1718)

	oṃ jñānapadmabuddha hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmarāja hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmamāra hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmatuṣṭi hūṃ // (1719)

	oṃ jñnapadmabhṛkuṭi hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmasūrya hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmacandra hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmahansa hūṃ // (1720)

	oṃ jñānapadmatāra hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmakumāra hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmanārāyaṇa hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmabhāṣa hūṃ // (1721)

	oṃ jñānapadmanṛtyeśvara hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmarakṣa hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmayakṣa hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmamuṣṭi hūṃ // (1722)

	oṃ jñānapadmalāsye hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmamāle hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmagīte hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānapadmanṛtye hūṃ // (1723)

	oṃ padmajñānadhūpe hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānapuṣpe hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānadīpe hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānagandhe hūṃ // (1724)
	%% These four should be emended?

	oṃ padmajñānāṅkuśa hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānāmoghapāśa hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānasphoṭa hūṃ //
	oṃ padmajñānāveśa hūṃ // (1725)
	%% These four should be emended?

athātra padmadharamamaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā,
yathāvat praveśyaivaṃ vadet /:

	na tvayānyasya vaktavyam /
	mā te narakapatanaṃ bhavet /
	duḥkhāni vā

iti / (1726)

tato 'sya jñānāny utpādayet //:
	lokeśvarasamāpattyā hṛdi padmaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	prāptapadmasamādhis tu śīghram utpatati kṣaṇāt // (1727)

	lokeśvarasamāpattyā lalāṭe padmabhāvanāt /
	abhyasan sudṛḍhībhūtāḥ khegāmī bhavate kṣaṇāt // (1728)

	jihvāyāṃ bhāvayan padmaṃ lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	saṃsiddho bhavate śīghram ākāśena sa gacchati // (1729)

	bhāvayan padmam uṣṇīṣe lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	saṃsiddho bhavate śīghram ūrdhvam utpatati kṣaṇāt // (1730)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ padmajñānahṛdayāviśa //
	oṃ padmajñānābhiṣekāviśa //
	oṃ padmajñānavidyottamāviśa //
	oṃ padmajñānoṣṇīṣāviśa // (1731)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā padmabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	anena vidhinā siddho adṛśyo bhavati kṣaṇāt // (1732)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā padmabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	tatrārūḍhaḥ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayann adṛśyo bhavet // (1733)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā padmabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	yadā paśyet tadā gṛhṇec chīgram adṛśyo bhavati // (1734)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā padmabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	dṛṣṭvā tu bhuktvā tat padmam adreśyo bhavati kṣaṇāt // iti // (1735)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ padmākāśa //
	oṃ padmaratha //
	oṃ padmajñāna gṛhṇa //
	oṃ padmarasāyana // (1736)

	vicitravarṇasaṃsthānaṃ padmabimbaṃ tu pāṇinā /
	gṛhya baddhvā mahāmudrāṃ sarvarūpadharo bhavet // (1737)

	vicitravarṇasaṃsthānaṃ padmabimbaṃ tu lekhayet /
	tatra bhāvayamānas tu bahurūpadharo bhavet // (1738)

	vicitravarṇasaṃsthānaṃ padmabimbaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā chandarūpī bhaviṣyati // (1739)

	vicitravarṇasaṃsthānaṃ padmabimbaṃ ghaṭāpayet /
	tatrārūḍhas tu khegāmī kāmarūpī bhaved dhruvam // iti // (1740)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ padmadharaviśvarūpapravartakāviśa //
	oṃ viśvapadma pravartaya mām // (1741)

	oṃ samādhiviśvapadmāviśa //
	oṃ viśvapadmāsanotkṣipākāśaṃ, viśvarūpam adhitiṣṭha mām // (1742)

	baddhvā caikatarāṃ samyaṅ mahāmudrāṃ samādhitaḥ /
	padmaṃ gṛhya pradātavyaṃ vaśībhavati śāśvataḥ // (1743)

	baddhvā caikatarāṃ samyaṅ mudrāsamayasaṃjñitām /
	tayā gṛhya tu vai padmaṃ dadyād vaśyakaro bhavet // (1744)

	baddhvā caikatamāṃ mudrāṃ samādhivhitāṃ śubhām /
	jñānapadmaṃ daded yasya so 'sya śīghraṃ vaśībhavet // (1745)

	baddhvā caikatamāṃ mudrāṃ karmākhyāṃ samayānvitaḥ /
	yasya dadyāt samupaśaḥ [sa nū vaśyaḥ?]
	padmadānāt kṣaṇād bhavet // iti // (1746)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:
	oṃ mahāpadma hoḥ //
	oṃ samayapadma hoḥ //
	oṃ jñānapadma hoḥ //
	oṃ karmapadma hoḥ // (1747)

tato jñānamaṇḍalamahāmudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:
	dharmamaṇḍalayogena mahāmudrās tu sādhayet /
	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi samayāgryaḥ prasādhayet // (1748)

	dharmamaṇḍalayogena padmapadmaṃ tu saṃsthapet /
	dharmamuṣṭiṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya karmamudra dvidhīkṛtāḥ // iti // (1749)

sarvatathāgatadharmasamayān mahākalparājād [dharma]jñānamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (1750)



[padma-]karmamaṇḍalavidhivistara

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatadharmakarmasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhānapadmaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvatathāgatakarmāgri hūṃ // (1751)

atha vajrapāṇir [bodhisattva] imāṃ svakulakarmasaṃbhavāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ hūṃ di // (1752)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ ratnakarmasamaye hūṃ // (1753)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ padmakarmi hūṃ // (1754)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ viśvakarmi hūṃ // (1755)

athāryāvalokiteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ svakarmamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (1756)

	atāthaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi karmamaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ padmakarmam iti smṛtam // (1757)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	buddhasya sarvataḥ sarvāḥ padmacihnadharā likhet // iti // (1758)

tatrāsāṃ vidyāhṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ padmabhūriṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ viśvakarmeśvari hūṃ // (1759)

	oṃ tathāgataiśvaryābhiṣekakarmavidye hūṃ //
	oṃ dharmakarmeśvari jñānapūjāsamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ amoghakarmeśvari hūṃ // (1760)

	oṃ padmakarmabuddhe hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmavajriṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakāminīmāraṇapūjākarmasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmatuṣṭi hūṃ // (1761)

	oṃ padmakarmabhṛkuṭi hūṃ traḥ //
	oṃ padmakarmasūrye hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmadhvaje hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmahāse haḥ // (1762)

	oṃ padmakarmatāre hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmakumāri hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmanārāyaṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmabrāhmi hūṃ // (1763)

	oṃ padmakarmanṛtyeśvari hūṃ //
	oṃ padmarakṣākarmasamaye hūṃ //
	   [oṃ padmarakṣarakṣākarmasamaye hūṃ //?]
	oṃ mahāpracaṇḍi ghātani padmadaṃṣtrākarmakari hūṃ //
	oṃ padmakarmamuṣṭi ghātaya hūṃ // (1764)

	oṃ ratipūje hūṃ jaḥ //
	oṃ abhiṣekapūje hūṃ hoḥ //
	oṃ gītapūje hūṃ dhaḥ //
	oṃ nṛtyapūje hūṃ vaḥ // (1765)

	oṃ dhūpapūje hūṃ aḥ //
	oṃ puṣpapūje hūṃ traḥ //
	oṃ ālokapūje hūṃ dhiḥ //
	oṃ gandhapūje hūṃ vaṃ // (1766)

	oṃ hayagrīva ānaya hūṃ jaḥ //
	oṃ amoghapāśakrodhe pīḍaya hūṃ phaṭ //
	oṃ padmaśaṅkalabandhe hūṃ phaṭ //
	oṃ padmaghaṇṭa āveśaya hūṃ phaṭ // (1767)

athātra karmamaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā yathāvat praveśyaivaṃ vadet //:

	na tvayā, kulaputra, kasyacid ayaṃ vaktavyaḥ /
	mā te narakapatanaṃ bhavet /

iti // (1768)

tato jñānāny utpādayed iti //

tataḥ padmadeśanājñānaṃ ṣikṣed iti // (1769)

	lokeśvaramahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pāpāni deśayañ chīghraṃ savapāpān sa śodhayet // (1770)

	samayāgrīṃ samādhāya lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	deśayan sarvapāpāni ānantaryāṇi śodhayet // (1771)

	lokeśvarasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	deśayan sarvapāpāni sarvapāpapraṇāśanam // (1772)

	baddhvā caikatamāṃ samyak karmamudrāṃ samāsataḥ /
	deśayan sarvapāpāni sarvakarmaviśodhanam // iti // (1773)

athaiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //

	oṃ sarvapāpasaṃśodhanamahāpadma //
	oṃ sarvānantaryaśodhanasamayapadma //
	oṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśadharmapadma //
	oṃ sarvakarmāvaraṇaviśodhakakarmapadma // (1774)

tataḥ sarvāvaraṇaparikṣayajñānaṃ śikṣayet //

	lokeśvaramahāmudrāṃ bhāvayet susamāhitaḥ /
	śudhya śudhya iti prodya sarvakarmāni śodhayet // (1775)

	baddhvā vai karmasamayāṃ lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	budhya budhya pravartaṃs tu sarvakarmāṇi śodhayet // (1776)

	lokeśvarasamāpattyā dharmamudrāṃ tu bhāvayet /
	dhī dhī dhīti procyan vai sarvakarmāṇi śodhayet // (1777)

	baddhvā vai karmamudrāṃ tu lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	hī hī hī hīti saṃdhāya sarvakarmāṇi śodhayet // iti // (1778)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //

	oṃ pāpakṣayapadma //
	oṃ āvaraṇakṣayapadma //
	oṃ nīvaraṇakṣayapadma //
	oṃ karmakṣayapadma // (1779)

tataḥ sarvatathāgatapūjājñānaṃ ṣikṣayet //:

	lokeśvaramahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	oṃ oṃ oṃ oṃ iti brūyāt sarvapūjāṃ pravartanam // (1780)

	baddhvā vai samayāgrīṃ tu lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	bhū bhū bhū bhūr iti prokte sarvabuddhān sa pūjayet // (1781)

	lokeśvarasamāpattyā dharmapadmaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	he he he heti saṃdhāya sarvabuddhān sa pūjayet // (1782)

	padmakarmamayīṃ mudrāṃ baddhvā gāḍhaṃ samāhitaḥ /
	dhe dhe dhe dha iti procya sarvabuddhān sa pūjayet // iti // (1783)

tatrāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ oṃkārapadma //
	oṃ bhūkārapadma //
	oṃ hekāradharmapadma //
	oṃ dhekārakarmapadma // (1784)

tataḥ siddhijñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	lokeśvaramahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	hrī hrī hrī hrīti varteta siddhir lokeśvarī bhavet // (1785)

	baddhvā vai samayāgrīṃ tu lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	śrī śrī śrī śrīti saṃdhāya prāpnuyāt siddhim uttamām // (1786)

	lokeśvarasamāpattiṃ bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	dhig dhig dhig dhig iti prokte padmakrodhas tu sidhyati // (1787)

	karmamudrāṃ samādhāya mahāpadmamayīṃ śubhām /
	siḥ siḥ siḥ sīti saṃdhāya padmasiddhim avāpnute // iti // (1788)

athāsāṃ hṛayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ hrīḥ sidhya //
	oṃ śrīḥ sidhya //
	oṃ dhik sidhya //
	oṃ siḥ sidhya // (1789)

tataḥ karmarahasyamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:

	lokeśvarasamāpattyā ramayan sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	aho sukha iti prokte sarvabuddhān sa pūjayet // (1790)

	lokeśvarasamāpattyā ramayan sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	priye priyeti vai prokte buddhānāṃ bhavati priyaḥ // (1791)

	lokeśvarasampattyā ramayan sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	aho rateti vai prokte ratir bhavet sa śāśvatī // (1792)

	lokceśvarasamāpattyā ramayan sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	sukha sukha iti prokte sukhaṃ tasya na hīyate // (1793)

athāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ sarvabuddhapūjāpravartanapadma //
	oṃ prītikarapadma hoḥ //
	oṃ ratipravartanapadma ho //
	oṃ mahāsukhapadma dṛdha ho // (1794)

tataḥ karmamahāmudrā yathāvac chikṣayet //

	tataḥ sukuḍmalāñjaliṃ samayamudrāvajrakāryam /
	karmamaṇḍalayogena sarvasthāneṣu sthāpayet // (1795)

	yataḥ padmakuladharmamudrātrakārayoktavyā /
	karmasamayāṃ dvidhīkṛtya karmamudrāḥ sa sādhayet // iti // (1796)

sarvatathāgatadharmasamayān mahākalparājāt padmakarmamaṇḍlavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (1797)

atha bhagavān punar api vajradharmasamayamudrādhisṭḥānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyedaṃ svamudrāhṛdayaṃ niścacāra //:

	oṃ vajradharmapadma hūṃ // (1798)

atha vajrapāṇir bodhisattva idaṃ svamudrāhṛdayam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajra jīḥ // (1799)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajraratnamukuṭi hūṃ // (1800)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ dharmapadma dhī (or dhe?) // (1801)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvamukhi hūṃ // (1802)

athāryāvalokteśvaro bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ caturmudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (1803)

	āthātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi caturmudrāgramaṇḍalam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ mahāmaṇḍalasaṃnibham // (1804)

	mudrāmaṇḍalamadhye tu buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet /
	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu vajrapadmādayo likeht // (1805)

athātra mahāmaṇḍala ākarṣaṇādividhivistaraṃ kṛtvā, yathāvat praveśya brūyāt /:

	na tvayedaṃ kasya cid vaktavyaṃ mā te mahāduḥkha.ṃ bhaved akālamaraṇaṃ viṣamakriyayā

iti // (1806)

tato jñānāny utpādayet //:

	padmaṃ hastena vai gṛhya samājighran prayatnataḥ /
	tena gandhena saṃyojya buddhān āśu prasidhyati // (1807)

	buddhabimbaṃ jaṭāmadhye pratiṣṭhāpya samāhitaḥ /
	sarvalokaṃ vaśaṃkuryād darśayan garvayā vajran // (1808)

	padmapadmamahābimbaṃ kārayitvā samādhinā /
	upaviśya yathātmānaṃ manasā sa tu mārayet // (1809)

	caturmukhaṃ tu vai padmaṃ kārayitvā kareṇa tu /
	saṃgṛhyāveśanādīni bhrāmayan prakaroti saḥ // (1810)

athāiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //: (1811)

	oṃ gandhapūjāgrya sādhaya hrīḥ //
	oṃ padmamukuṭatathāgata vaśīkuru sarvān lokeśvarābhiṣekasamaya hoḥ // (1812)

	oṃ padmapadma māraya sarvapratyarthikān, samādhijñāna dhik //
	oṃ viśvapadma sarvakarmakaro bhava lalilvali lali hūṃ phaṭ // (1813)

tato mudrārahasyajñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	raktaḥ san sarvakāryāṇi sādhayet samayo hy ayam /
	duḥsādhyā 'pi hi mudrā vai kṣaṇāt sidhyati yogata iti // (1814)

tatrāsya samayo bhavati //:

	oṃ sādhaya padmarāgasamaya aḥ // (1815)

tato mahāmudrādisarvamudrābandhaṃ śikṣayet //: (1816)

[caturmudrāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ (Tib.)] (1817)

athāryāvalokiteśvaro mahābodhisattva idaṃ sarvajagadvinayaṃ nāma hṛdayam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvajagadvinayamahāsattvāgaccha, śīghraṃ
	vaiśvarūpyaṃ saṃdarśaya,
	mama ca sarvasiddhayaḥ prayaccha hrīḥ // (1818)

athāryāvalokiteśvaro mahābodhisattva idaṃ sarvajagadvinayaṃ nāma maṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (1819)

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jagadvinayamaṇḍalam /
	mahāmaṇḍalayogena saṃlikhed bāhyamaṇḍalam // (1820)

	tasyābhyantarataḥ padmaṃ tathaiva ca samālikhet /
	tatra sarvābjavisphātiviśvarūpaṃ samālikhet // iti // (1821)

athātra mahāmaṇḍale yathāvad vidhivistareṇa praveśya,
tathaivoktvā, (1822)

sarvajagadvinayajñānaṃ śikṣayet //: (1823)

	maṇḍalaṃ tu samālikhya jagadvinayasaṃjñitam /
	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrāṃ bhaved viśvadharopamaḥ // iti // (1824)

tato jagadvinayarahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	viśvarūpasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	dvayendriyasamāpattyā maṇḍale tu sa sidhyati // (1825)

tato mahāmudrādimudrābandhaṃ śikṣayet, tathaiva siddhayaḥ //
evaṃ paṭādiṣv iti //
mudrāyām apy ekamudrāmaṇḍalayogena tathaiva siddhaya iti // // (1826)

atha sarvatathāgatā punaḥ samājam āgamyāvalokiteśvarāya mahābodhisattvāya sādhukārāṇy adadan //: (1827)

	sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /
	vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe // (1828)

	subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /
	sarvatāthāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham // iti // (1829)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvatathāgatadharmasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (1830)



sarvatathāgatakarmasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ (1831)

(sarvārthasiddhimahāmaṇḍalavidhivistara)

atha khalu sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya,
sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaratnaṃ tam eva vajradharam āryākāśagarbhaṃ mahābodhisattvam anena nāmāṣṭaśatenādhyeṣitavantaḥ //: (1832)

	ākāśagarbha sattvārtha mahāsattva mahādyute /
	mahāratna suratnāgrya vajraratna namo 'stu te // (1833)

	abhiṣeka mahāratna mahāśuddha mahāśubha /
	buddharatna viśuddhāṅga ratnaratna namo 'stu te // (1834)

	ākāśākāśasaṃbhūta sarvākāśamahānabha /
	ākāśadhātu sarvāśa sarvāśāgrya namo 'stu te // (1835)

	ratnasaṃbhava ratnorṇa buddhorṇa sutathāgata /
	sarvaratna susarvāgrya ratnakārya namo 'stu te // (1836)

	ratna ratnāgrya ratnogra(?) ratna sarvatathāgata /
	ratnottama mahākāśa samākāśa namo 'stu te // (1837)

	alaṃkāra mahāśobha śobhākara suśobhaka /
	śuddha sarvārtha śuddhārtha dānacarya namo 'stu te // (1838)

	dharmaratna viḍuddhāgrya saṃgharatna tathāgata /
	mahābhiṣeka lokārtha pramodārtha namo 'sut te // (1839)

	dāna pradāna dānāgrya tyāga tyāgārya dāyaka /
	sarvasattvārtha tattvārtha mahārtha namo 'stu te // (1840)

	cintārāja mahāteja dānapāramitānaya /
	tathāgata mahāsattva sarvabuddha namo 'stu te // (1841)

	tathāgatamahāratna tathāgatamahāprabha /
	tathāgatamahāketo mahāhāsa namo 'stu te // (1842)

	tathāgatābhiṣekāgrya mahābhiṣeka mahāvibho /
	lokanātha sulokāgrya lokasūrya namo 'stu te // (1843)

	ratnādhikādhikatara ratnabhūṣaṇa ratnadhṛk /
	ratnāloka mahāloka ratnāloka namo 'stu te // (1844)

	ratnotkara suratnottha maṇe vajramaṇe guṇa /
	ratnākara sudīptāṅga sarvaratna namo 'stu te // (1845)

	mahātma yaṣṭi ratneśa sarvāśāparipūraka /
	sarvābhiprāyasaṃprāpti ratnaraśī namo 'stu te // (1846)

	ābhāgrya vyāpi sarvātma varaprada mahāvara /
	vibhūte sarvasaṃpatte vajragarbha namo 'stu te // (1847)

	yaḥ kaścid dhārayen nāmnām idaṃ te 'ṣṭaśataṃ śivam /
	sarvabuddhābhiṣekaṃ tu sa prāpnoty anaghaḥ kṣaṇāt // (1848)

	adhyeṣayāmas tvāṃ ratnaṃ bhāṣasva dhanasaṃcayam /
	sarvabuddhābhiṣekāgryam utpādaya nijaṃ kulam // iti // (1849)

athākāśagarbho bodhisattva idaṃ sarvatathāgatavacanam upaśrutya,
sarvatathāgatābhiṣekasamayaṃ nāma svahṛdayam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajraratna hūṃ // (1850)

atha bhagavān vairocanas tathāgata idaṃ sarvatathāgatamaṇisamayaṃ nāma vidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvatathāgatāśāparipūraṇamahāratna hūṃ // (1851)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva imaṃ svakulasaṃbhavaṃ vidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajra hūṃ traḥ // (1852)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ maṇi hūṃ // (1853)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva imaṃ svakulasaṃbhavaṃ vidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ padma hrīḥ // (1854)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //

	oṃ viśvaratna hūṃ // (1855)

athāryākāśagarbho bodhisattva mahāsattvaḥ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaratnaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpannaḥ // (1856)

samanantarasamāpanne cātha tāvad eva sarvatathāgatahṛdayebhyo vajramaṇiratnaraśmayo niścaritāḥ // (1857)

te sarvalokadhātavo 'vabhāsya, sarvasattvān sarvatathāgatābhiṣekair abhiṣicya, punar apy ekadhyībhūtvā, bhagavata ākāśagarbhasya mahābodhisattvasya hṛdaye 'nupraviṣṭā iti // (1858)

atha tata ākāśagarbhahṛdayāt sa eva bhagavān vajrapāṇi samantaraśmijvālāgarbhā vicitravajramaṇiratnābhiṣekādyābharaṇālamkārālaṃkṛtakāyā mahāvajramaṇiratnacihnamudrāvyagrakarā mahābodhisattvakāyā bhūtvā viniḥsṛtya, (1859)

sarvalokadhātuṣu mahāratnavarṣādibhī ratnotpattibhiḥ saṃtoṣya punar āgatya, bhagavato vairocanasya sarvato vajradhātumahāmaṇḍalayogena candramaṇḍalāśritā bhūtvedam udānam udānayiṃsuḥ // (1860)

	aho hi sarvabuddhānāṃ sarvaratnasamuccayam /
	vajraratnakulaṃ tv edaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ jagadarthataḥ // iti // (1861)

athākāśagarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ svakulam utpādya,
sarvatathāgatebhyaḥ sarvāśāparipūryai niryātyedaṃ sarvārthasiddhiṃ nāma mahāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (1862)

	athātaḥ saṃpuravakṣyāmi mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ sarvasiddhir iti smṛtam // (1863)

	caturasraṃ caturdvāraṃ catustoraṇaśobhitam /
	catuḥsūtrasamāyuktaṃ paṭṭasragdāmabhūṣitam // (1864)

	sarvamaṇḍalakoṇeṣu dvāraniryūhasaṃdhiṣu /
	khacitaṃ vajraratnais tu sūtrayed bāhyamaṇḍalam // (1865)

	tasyābhyantarataḥ kāryaṃ vajraratnasamaṃ puram /
	aṣṭasatambhāgrayogena sūtraṇaṃ tatra kārayet // (1866)

	pañcamaṇḍalaśobhaṃ tu nānāratnakarojjvalam /
	svamudrāparivāraṃ tu tatra buddhaṃ niveśayet // (1867)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ buddharatna hūṃ //
	oṃvajramaṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ vajraratāṅkura hūṃ //
	oṃ vajraratnapadma hūṃ //
	oṃ vajraratnavarṣa hūṃ // (1868)

	vajravegena cākramya sarvāśāsiddhimaṇḍalam /
	tatrasthaṃ vajragarbhaṃ tu likhed ratnavarapradam // (1869)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu ratnamudrāsamanvitāḥ /
	mahāsattvāḥ samālekhyā yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ // (1870)

athaiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ sarvārthasiddhiprada hūṃ //
	oṃ vajramaṇicihnākāśagarbha bhagavan sidhya sidhya hūṃ // (1871)

	oṃ ratnāṅkuśākarṣaya sarvārthān ānaya śīghraṃ sarvatathāgatasatyam anusmara hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇirāga vaśīkuru sarvārthān ānayākāśagarbha hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnatuṣṭi hūṃ // (1872)

	vajravegena cākramya ratnamālasya maṇḍalam /
	tatra madhye likhet samyag ratnamālādharaṃ param // (1873)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	mahāsattvāḥ samālekhyā maṇicihnāgrapāṇayaḥ // (1874)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnadṛṣṭi traḥ //
	oṃ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaratnamāla hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇisūrya hūṃ // (1875)

	oṃ cintāmaṇidhvajasarvāśāprapūrakākāśagarbha hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnāṭṭahāsa hasa hasa hūṃ // (1876)

	vajravegena cākramya ratnapadmasya maṇḍalam /
	ratnasthaṃ tu samālekhyaṃ ratnapadmadharaṃ vibhum // (1877)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu mahāsattvān samālikhet /
	maṇicihnaṃ samāsena yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ // (1878)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnapadma hūṃ //
	oṃ tyāgasamādhijñānagarbha hūṃ // (1879)

	oṃ ratnakośāgrya hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇicakra pravartaya hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnabhāṣa hūṃ // (1880)

	vajravegena cākramya ratnavṛṣṭes tu maṇḍalam /
	tatra lekhyaṃ mahāsattvaṃ ratnavṛṣṭipravarṣayan // (1881)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu mahāsattvān yathāvidhi /
	ratnacihnasamopetān mudrāhastān samāsataḥ // (1882)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnavṛṣṭi pravarṣaya sarvārthasaṃpado bhagavan maṇihasta hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇipūjāsamaya hūṃ // (1883)

	oṃ maṇibandhakavaca hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇidaṃṣṭrākarālamahāyakṣa hara hara sarvārthān bhīṣāpaya hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnabandhasamaya hūṃ // (1884)

	vajravegena cākramya koṇabhāgeṣu sarvataḥ /
	ratnalāsyādayo lekhyā yathāvad anupurvaśaḥ // (1885)

tatraiṣāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnarati hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnamāle hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnagīte hūṃ //
	oṃ ratnanṛtye hūṃ // (1886)

	vajravegena niṣkramya bāhyamaṇḍalam uttamam /
	bāhyamaṇḍalakoṇeṣu dhūpapūjādayo likhet // (1887)

tatraiṣāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ dhūparatne //
	oṃ puṣpamaṇi //
	oṃ ratnāloke //
	oṃ maṇigandhe // (1888)

	dvārapālās tu kartavyā dvāramadhyacatuṣṭaye /
	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi maṇḍalavidhivistaram // (1889)

athātra hṛdayāni bhavanti //

	oṃ sarvaratākarṣa āryāruṇamahāsattva bhagavantam ākāśagarbhaṃ codayākarṣaya śīghraṃ ho jaḥ //
	oṃ sarvaratnapraveśasamaya praveṣaya samayān mahāmaṇirājakulaṃ ratnapāśa hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇibandha hūṃ vaḥ //
	oṃ maṇiratāveśa aḥ // (1890)

athātra mahāmaṇḍale svayaṃ maṇiratnācāryo yathāvat praviśya vidhivistaram ātmanaḥ kṛtvā,
tato ratnādhiṣṭhitakalaśodakena maṇiśiṣyān abhiṣicya,
vajramaṇisamayamudrāṃ bandhayed anena hṛdayena //:

	oṃ vajramaṇisamaya vaṃ // (1891)

tato yathāvarṇaprāptitayā vastram uttarāsaṃgaṃ kṛtvā,
tādṛśenaivākṣiṇī baddhvā praveśayed anena hṛdayena //:

	oṃ hūṃ praviśa maṇirājakulam // (1892)

tataḥ praveśya, vaktavyaṃ:

	na tvayedaṃ kasya cid vaktavyam /,
	mā te sarvajanmasu dāridryaduḥkhān mokṣo na bhaven,
	narakavāsaś ca dṛḍho bhaved

ity uktvā samayaṃ sphoṭayet // (1893)

mahāyānābhisamayaṃ coccārayet //
tataḥ samāviṣṭasya vajravācā paripṛcchet //:

	kutra mahānidhir asti /
	kathaṃ vā prāpyate // (1894)

tato bhagavān ākāśagarbho bodhisattvaḥ sarvaṃ jalpāpayatīty uktamātre mukhabandhaṃ muktvā, mahāmaṇḍalaṃ darśayet // (1895)

sarvatathāgatābhṣekasamayaṃ codāharet //
yāvad bhagavāṃs tathāgata āgata iti // (1896)

tato yathāvibhavataḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā sarvakāryāṇi sādhayed iti // (1897)


athātra jñānamudrā bhavanti //:

	vajragarbhamahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	nidhānaṃ khanate yatra nidhānaṃ tatra paśyati // (1898)

	baddhvā tu samayāgrīṃ vai nidhānaṃ yatra vidyate /
	pīḍayet tatra tāṃ mudrāṃ svayam uttiṣṭhate tadā // (1899)

	vajragarbhasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	manasā caiva jānāti nidhānaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati // (1900)

	baddhvā karmamayīṃ mudrāṃ vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	tāṃ mudrām āviśed yatra nidhānaṃ tatra lakṣayet // (1901)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāmaṇiratnāviśa hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇipīḍa darśaya //
	oṃ ratnasamādhi brūhi //
	oṃ ratnāveśa darśaya // (1902)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya yatra kāyaṃ tu veṣṭayet /
	tatra ratnanidhānaṃ tu jñātavyaṃ samayāttmabhiḥ // (1903)

	baddhvā tu samayāgrīṃ  vai yatrāviśya parisphuṭet /
	nidhānaṃ tatra vijñeyaṃ mahāratnamayaṃ bhavet // (1904)

	samādhimudrāṃ baddhvā vai yady āviśya svayaṃ punarḥ /
	brūyād yatra nidhānaṃ tu mahāratnamayaṃ bhavet // (1905)

	karmamudrāṃ tu baddhvā vai yadāviśya parasparam /
	hastau bandhe tu samayāṃ nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // iti // (1906)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāratnakāya darśaya ratnam //
	oṃ ākāśagarbha maṇiratna sphuṭa sphuṭa yatra nidhiḥ //
	oṃ maṇiratnajñāna svayaṃ brūhi //
	oṃ punaḥ samayabandha darśayasva // (1907)

	baddhvā tu vai mahāmudrāṃ yatrāśaṅkā bhavet tadā /
	tatra jñānena viñeyaṃ nidhānaṃ ratansaṃbhavam // (1908)

	yatra śaṅkā bhavet tatra samayāgrīṃ tu bandhayet /
	yadā mokṣaṃ svayaṃ yāyān nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // (1909)

	samādhimudrāṃ baddhvā vai śaṅkā yatra bhaved dhruvā /
	jñānam upādya vijñeyaṃ nidhis tatrāsti śāśvataḥ // (1910)

	yatra bhūyo bhavec chaṅkā karmamudrāṃ tu tatra vai /
	badhnīyād vidhivat tāṃ tu sphuṭej jñeyo nidhiḥ punaḥ // (1911)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ nidhijñānāviśa //
	oṃ ratnasamaya muñca nidhibandhān //
	oṃ dharmaratna brūhi nidhānam //
	oṃ sarvakarmāṇi sphoṭaya darśaya nidhibandhotkṣipa // (1912)

	mahāmudrāṃ tu saṃdhāya nidhānaṃ parimārgayet /
	yatrasthasya samāveśo bhavet tatra vinirdiśet // (1913)

	baddhvā tu samayāgrīṃ vai nidhiṃ tu parimārgayet /
	yatrastho dṛḍhatāṃ yāyān nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // (1914)

	samādhimudrāṃ saṃdhāya nidhānaṃ parimārgayet /
	yatrastho jñānavān bhūyān nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // (1915)

	baddhvā karma mayīṃ mudrāṃ nidhiṃ tu parimārgayet /
	yatrasthaḥ karmamudrāṃ tu bhrāmayet tatra nirdiśet // (1916)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāratnaparīkṣāviśa //
	oṃ ratnasamayadṛḍha darśaya //
	oṃ ratnaparīkṣājñānāviśa //
	oṃ maṇikarma bhrāmaya // (1917)

tato maṇirahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā nidhānaṃ parimārgayet /
	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrāṃ samāveśān nidhiṃ labhet // (1918)

	baddhvā tu samayāgrīṃ vai rāmayaṃs tu striyaṃ tathā /
	yatra mudrā dṛḍhībhūyām nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // (1919)

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā nidhānaṃ parimārgayet /
	bhāvayañ jñānamudrāṃ tu nidhijñānaṃ pravartate // (1920)

	baddhvā tu karmamudrāṃ vai dvayendriaysamādhitaḥ /
	sphuṭed yatra tu sā mudrā nidhiṃ tatra vinirdiśet // (1921)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāmaṇisaṃyogāviśa //
	oṃ samayasaṃyoga dṛḍho me bhava //
	oṃ nidhijñānāviśāviśa saṃyoga //
	oṃ sarvakarmasphoṭasaṃyoga // (1922)

tato mahāmaṇikulasarvamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

atha mahāmudrā bhavanti //: (1923)

	candramaṇḍalamadhyastho (or -madhye tu)
	yathālekhyānusārataḥ /
	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrāḥ sarvārthottamasiddhayaḥ // (1924)

tato mahāmudrāṇāṃ karmā.i bhavanti /:

	buddhamudrā tu bhddhaṃtvaṃ susiddhir vajragarbhayoḥ /
	ratnāṅkuśā samākarṣā maṇirāgānurāgā // (1925)

	maṇituṣṭayā(or ratnatuṣṭayā) tu saṃtoṣā
	maṇidṛṣṭyārthakārikā /
	maṇimālābhiṣekā tu maṇisūryā sutejadā // (1926)

	cintāmaṇir yathecchādā ratnahāsārthahārikā /
	dharmaratnāpi dharmāptis tyāgāgrī lābham uttamam // (1927)

	ratnakośā mahākośaṃ maṇicakrādhipatyatām /
	bhāṣā mārgaṇasiddhis tu ratnavṛṣṭir mahādhanam // (1928)

	maṇipūjā supūjyaś ca ratnavārmā dṛḍhaṃkarī /
	ratnadaṃṣṭrā hared arthān maṇimuṣṭyā tu sidhyati // (1929)

athātra mahāmaṇḍale samayamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:

	vajraratnamayīmudrā sarvabuddhābhiṣekadā /
	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā vajraratnaṃ tu sidhyati // (1930)

	vajradvikaṃ maṇīkṛtvā dhanaṃ vajradharāl labhet /
	sā evāṅguṣṭhavajreṇa maṇiṃ dadyād dhṛdi sthitam // (1931)

	kuḍmalāgryā maṇiṃ baddhvā lokeśo dhanado bhavet /
	vajrakarmamaṇir dadyān mahāviśvamaṇidhvajam // (1932)

	vajradhātvagramaṇinā buddharatnatvam āpnuyāt /
	samāgrāpṛṣṭhasaṃkocā vajram aṅguṣṭhabandhataḥ // (1933)

	iyaṃ vajramaṇiḥ proktā vajragarbhasya pāṇitaḥ /
	anayā baddhamātrayā mahāvajramaṇiṃ labhet // (1934)

	ratnavajraṃ samādhāya samamadhyotthitāṅkurām /
	anayā baddhamātrayā svabhiṣekāny avāpnuyāt // (1935)

	sa eva madhyamānāmakaniṣṭhā kuḍmalīkṛtā /
	anayā tu dhanaṃ dadyād avaloktanāmadhṛk // (1936)

	vajraratnaprayogena tarjanyaṅguṣṭhakanyasā /
	madhyamābhyāṃ nakhasaṃdhānā samānāmāṅkurotthitā // (1937)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya tarjanībhyāṃ maṇīkṛtā /
	prasāritaṅguṣṭhamukhā hṛdi sarvārthasiddhidā // (1938)

	vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya madhyamāmaṇiyojitā /
	mudreyaṃ maṇicihnasya maṇiratnapradāyikā // (1939)

	sā evāṅkuśayogena tarjanībhyāṃ samanvitā /
	sarvārthakārṣaṇī mudrā maṇiratnāṅkuśī smṛtā // (1940)

	sā eva valitā caiva tarjanyā tarjanīgrahā /
	vāṇākarṣaṇayogena karṣayan rāgayej jagat // (1941)

	sā eva sādhukārā tu tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayojitā /
	sā evāṅguṣṭhasaṃdhānasaṃchannāgryāṅgulī tathā // (1942)

	aṅguṣṭhāntarayoś caiva punar agryā mukhekṣaṇāt /
	maṇidṛṣṭis tu sā khyātā dṛṣṭvārthānāṃ prahārikā // (1943)

	sarvārthasiddhimālā tu svabhiṣekapradāyikā // (1944)

	sā eva hṛdaye 'ṅguṣṭhamukhasaṃdhānayojitā /
	hṛdaye maṇisūryā tu mahātejaḥpradāyikā // (1945)

	mūrdhnisthā ca samānāmapatākāgravidāritā /
	mahāvajramaṇiḥ pūrvaṃ sarvāśāparipūrikā // (1946)

	sā eva hāsasaṃsthā tu līlayā parivatitā /
	ratnāṭṭahāsā nāmnā vai hāsāt sarvārthakārikā // (1947)

	sarvāgramaṇipadmā tu dhanahārī samādhinā /
	sā evāntyādidānā tu mahādānapradāyikā // (1948)

	adhargatasamāṅguṣṭhatarjanīmaṇisaṃsthitā /
	maṇikośā hared arthān jagatāṃ vikrameṇa tu // (1949)

	vajrabandhāgracakrā tu samāṅguṣṭhapraveśitā /
	tarjanīmaṇisaṃsthānāc cakravartitvadāyikā // (1950)

	sā evāñjaliyogena mukhataś ca samuddhṛtā /
	sa tu saṃdhāya vācā vai svājñayā harate dhanam // (1951)

	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā ratnavarṣaṃ pravarṣate /
	sarvāṅgulyupastambhā tu catuḥśo varṣate dhanam // (1952)

	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā nṛtyann uṣṇīṣamadhyataḥ /
	saṃpūjya vidhivat sarve sarvaratnaiḥ prapūjyate // (1953)

	sarvārthasiddhimudrāṃ tu kaṇṇthādeśe pariṣvajet /
	maṇibandheti vikhyātā rakṣākavacinī smṛtā // (1954)

	sā eva sarvasiddhyarthā yakṣayogā mukhasthitā /
	maṇidaṃṣṭreti vikhyātā bhayāt sarvārthahāriṇī // (1955)

	vajrabandhaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya kuñcitāgryā suyantritā /
	saṃgṛhyāṅguṣṭhayoḥ samyaṅ maṇimuṣṭis tu siddhidā // (1956)

	pūjāgrasamayānāṃ tu vajradhātuprayogataḥ /
	yathāvan maṇiyogena samayāgryo 'tra kalpitāḥ // (1957)

	madhyamāmaṇiyogena tā eva tu vikalpitāḥ /
	ekāṅkuśyādiyogena sarvakarmaprasādhikāḥ // iti (1958)

atha mahāmaṇikuladharmamudrājñānaṃ bhavati //:
	traḥ /
	graḥ /
	triḥ /
	hrīḥ /
	śriḥ /
	iḥ /
	raḥ /
	haḥ /
	dhrīḥ /
	dhiḥ /
	kṛ /
	vā /
	rī /
	ḍhaḥ /
	ya /
	aḥ // (1959)

	ratnamuṣṭiṃ dvidhīkṛtya karmamudrās tu sādhe// iti (1960)

sarvatathāgatakarmasamayān mahākalparājāt sarvārthasiddhimahāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ // // (1961)


(ratnaguhyamudrāmaṇḍalavidhivistara)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatābhiṣekadhāraṇīsamayasaṃbhavaratnādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajraratnastūpe hūṃ // (1962)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva imāṃ svakulasaṃbhavāṃ mudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajrābhiṣekamāle 'bhiṣiñca samaye hūṃ // (1963)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajraratnābhiṣeka hūṃ // (1964)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajradharmābhiṣiñca māṃ // (1965)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvābhiṣekapūjāsamaye hūṃ // (1966)

atha bhagavān āryākāśagarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ svakulasamayamudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (1967)

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣkyāmi mudrāmaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ ratnaguhyam iti smṛtam // (1968)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	tasya madhye yathānyāyaṃ buddhamudrāṃ samālikhet // (1969)

	paryaṅkasthaṃ maṇiṃ pūrvaṃ vajradhātoḥ puro likhet /
	maṇimālāṃ maṇiṃ padme maṇiṃ maṇiparivṛtam // (1970)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ trāḥ //
	oṃ maṇisamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnābhiṣekamāle hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnapadmi hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnavṛṣṭisamaye hūṃ // (1971)

	vajravegena niṣkramya sarvasiddhes tu maṇḍale /
	vajraratnasya madhye tu mahāratnamaṇiṃ likhet // (1972)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu svamudrāmaṇisaṃyutā /
	yathāvad anupūrveṇa ratnācāryaḥ samālikhet // (1973)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ sarvārthasiddhiprade mahāvajraratnasamayamaṇi sarvārthān me sādhaya dhāraṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnākarṣe hūṃ // (1974)

	oṃ maṇiratnasamayāṅkuśy ākarṣaya maṇikulaṃ jaḥ //
	oṃ maṇirāgasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇisādhvi [hūṃ] // (1975)

	vajravegena cākramya dvitīyamaṇḍalaṃ tathā /
	tatra madhye maṇiṃ lekhyaṃ netradvikasamanvitam // (1976)

	tasyās tu sarvapārśveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	maṇicihnasamopetāḥ svamudrās tu samālikhet // (1977)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ vajramaṇiratnanetrānaya vaśīkuru sarvārthasaṃpadaḥ śīghraṃ dṛṣṭyaṅkuśi hūṃ //
	oṃ vajraratnamāle 'bhiṣiñca hūṃ // (1978)

	oṃ maṇiratnasūrye jvālaya sarvaṃ mahātejini hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇicandradhvajāgri hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇihāse hasa hūṃ // (1979)

	vajravegena cākramya tṛtīyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tathā /
	tatra madhye samālekhyaṃ maṇipadmasamanvitam // (1980)

	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	maṇicihnasamopetāḥ svamudrās tu samālikhet // (1981)

	vajravegena cākramya maṇipadmaṃ samālikhet /
	tasya pārśveṣu sarveṣu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ // (1982)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ maṇisamādhipadmini hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnatyāgasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇisamayakośe hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇisamayacakre hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇibhāṣāgri hūṃ // (1983)

	vajravegeṇa cākramya caturthaṃ maṇḍalottamam /
	tatrasthaṃ ratnavṛṣṭyā tu vajraṃ ratnasamanvitam // (1984)

	saṃlikheta yathāvat tu karmamudrāparivṛtam /
	maṇicihnaprayogais tu yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ // (1985)

athāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnavṛṣṭi sādhaya mahāmaṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ mahāpūjāsamaye nṛtya nṛtya aḥ //
	oṃ maṇiratnasamayarakṣe //
	oṃ vajramaṇiratnadaṃṣṭrākarāle hara hara hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇisamayamuṣṭi // (1986)

athātra maṇiguhyamaṇḍale yathāvat karma kṛtvā,
śiṣyān praveśya brūyāt //:

	na tvayā kasyacid ayaṃ nayo vaktavyaḥ,
	mā te mahādāridryamahākālakriyānarakapatanaṃ syāt.

ity uktvā, (1987)

svamaṇisamayajñānāny utpādayet //: (1988)

	vajraratnaṃ nabhe likhya vajraratnasamādhinā /
	ātmanas tu lalāṭe vai sthāpya rājā bhaved dhruvam // (1989)

	vajraratnaṃ samālikhya samayāgrīṃ tu bandhayet /
	sthāpyābhiṣekasthāneṣu rājyatvaṃ bhavate dhruvam // (1990)

	vajraratnaṃ samālikhya vajraratnasamādhinā /
	taj jñānaratnaṃ saṃsthāpya bhaved rājā svayaṃ kṛtaḥ // (1991)

	vajraratnaṃ nabhe likhya karmamudrāṃ tu bandhayet /
	svasthāne tat pratiṣṭhāpya bhaved rājā svayaṃ kṛtaḥ // iti (1992)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	mahāvajraratnābhiṣiñca māṃ //
	samayaratnābhiṣiñca mām //
	dharmaratnābhiṣiñca mām //
	karmaratnābhiṣiñca mām // (1993)

	vajraratnaṃ tu hṛdaye mahāmudrāṃ tu bhāvayet /
	bhāvayann abhiṣekaṃ tu prāpnoti paramādbhutam // (1994)

	vajraratnaṃ lalāṭe tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	baddhvā vai ratnavajrīṃ tu bhaved rājā tu sarvataḥ // (1995)

	vajraratnaṃ tu jihvāyāṃ vajraratnasamādhinā /
	bhāvayann abhiṣekaṃ tu prāpnuyād dharmarājyatām // (1996)

	vajraratnaṃ svam uṣṇīṣe bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	baddhvā vai karmamudrāṃ tu bhaved rājā sukarmakṛt // iti (1997)

athāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ vajraratnahṛdayābhiṣiñca hoḥ //
	oṃ vajraratnābhiṣeka traḥ //
	oṃ vajraratnajñānābhiṣeka vaṃ //
	oṃ vajraratnoṣṇīṣādhitiṣṭhasva mām // (1998)

	paṭādiṣu samālikhya vajraratnaṃ svam ātmanā /
	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrāṃ mahārājā bhavet sa tu // (1999)

	paṭādiṣu samālikhya vajraratnam anuttaram /
	bhāvayet sattvavajrāṃ tu samayānāṃ bhavet patiḥ // (2000)

	paṭādiṣu samālikhya vajraratnaṃ svam ātmanā /
	bhāvayan dhyānamudrāṃ tu bhaved dharmādhipo dhruvam // (2001)

	paṭādiṣu samālikhya vajraratnam anuttaram /
	bhāvayet karmamudrāṃ tu bhavet karmādhipaḥ svam // iti  (2002)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	vajraratnabimbādhitiṣṭha //
	vajraratnabimba pratiṣṭha //
	vajraratnabimbāviśa //
	vajraratnabimba kuru // (2003)

	sauvarṇaṃ vāpi raupyaṃ vā vajraratnaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	anyaratnamayaṃ vāpi hṛdi bhāvyābhiṣicyate // (2004)

	sauvarṇam anyaratnaṃ vā vajraratnaṃ tv anuttaram /
	sthāpya bhūyo lalāṭe tu bhaved rājā mahādhanaḥ // (2005)

	sauvarṇam anyaratnaṃ vā vajraratnaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	svamukhe caiva prakṣipya bhaved vācāṃ patis tu saḥ // (2006)

	sarvarṇam anyaratnaṃ vā vajraratnaṃ tu dhārayet /
	uṣṇīṣe bhāvayan bhūyaḥ sarvakarmapatir bhavet // iti (2007)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ vajraratnahṛdayābharaṇa hūṃ //
	oṃ vajraratnābhiṣekamahārthaprada //
	oṃ vajraratnavācaspate //
	oṃ vajraratnamahākarmapate // (2008)

tato maṇikulasamayamudrārahasyajñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā taṃ maṇiṃ strībhage tathā /
	praveśya tu mahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnute // (2009)

	samayāgryāmaṇiṃ baddhvā strībhage samayāgryayā /
	baddhayā tu bhavet siddhir abhiṣekeṣu sarvaśaḥ // (2010)

	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā dharmamudrāṃ tu bhāvayan /
	taṃ maṇiṃ strībhage viddhvā bhavet siddhir anuttarā // (2011)

	karmamudrāmaṇiṃ viddhvā strībhage karmamudrayā /
	baddhayā tu bhavet siddhiḥ sarvakarmasv anuttarā // iti (2012)

tatrāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ mahāsiddhiḥ //
	oṃ samayābhiṣekasiddhiḥ //
	oṃ dharmasiddhiḥ //
	oṃ karmasiddhiḥ // (2013)

athātra maṇḍale mahāmudrābandho bhavati //:

	ratnavajrāṅkurāṃ baddhva madhyānāmāntimāṅgulī /
	prasāritās tu saṃdhāya mūrdhni sthāpyāgrasiddhidhā // (2014)

	vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya granthitāgryā yugorṇagā /
	dvyaṅguṣṭhānāmikā vajrā parivartyābhi.ekadā // (2015)

	vajraratnaprayogeṇa sā eva parivartitā /
	tarjanyagramukhāsaṅgād abhiṣekaṃ dadāti sā // (2016)

	sā evāṅguṣṭhajyeṣṭhābhyāṃ dharma vajriprayogataḥ /
	baddhvā lalāṭagā caiva mahādharmābhiṣekadā // (2017)

	karmavajraṃ samādhāya lalāṭe paivartya vai /
	sarvābhiṣekamālāṃ tu sthāpayann abhiṣiñcati // (2018)

	ratnasaṃbhavamudrāṃ tu samayāṃ vajradhātujām /
	baddhvā ratnapratiṣṭhāṃ tu lalāṭe tv abhiṣicyate // (2019)

	aṅguṣṭhā baddhaparyaṅkā tarjanīdvayasaṃdhitā /
	maṇimukhāgryayoḥ kuryān mahāvajramaṇiṃ labhet // (2020)

	vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya maṇimuṣṭiṃ prasārayet /
	maṇis tu madhyamābhyāṃ tu maṇimālābhiṣekadā // (2021)

	vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya madhyamāmaṇiyojitā /
	dvyagrānāmavikāsā tu padmaṃ kṛtvā tu sidhyati // (2022)

	madhyamābhyāṃ maṇiṃ baddhvā sarvāṅgulayaḥ samutthitāḥ /
	bhāvayaṃs tu maṇīn eva bhavet suparivāravān // (2023)

	vajraratnaṃ samādhāya madhyamāṅguṣṭhayogataḥ /
	samānāmakaṇiṣṭhā tu jihvāmukha maṇipradā // (2024)

	sa eva tarjanī vajrasaṃsthā eva tthāṅkuśī /
	tarjanyā tarjanī karṣā tābhyāṃ tuṣṭipradāyikā // (2025)

	madhyamābhyāṃ maṇiṃ baddhvā dvyagrasaṃkocasaṃsthitā /
	buaddhvānāmāṅgulimukhāv aṅguṣṭhadvayacchāditā // (2026)

	sā eva sūryā vartā tu mūrdhni bāhuprasāritā /
	maṇidhvajāgrakeyūrā hāsayogena yogitā // (2027)

	vajrabandhaṃ samādhāya jyeṣṭhānāmamukhotthitā /
	tābhiḥ padmaṃ tu saṃbhāvya madhyamābhyāṃ maṇīkṛtā // (2028)

	sā evāntyapradānā tu vajrakośaprayogitā /
	vajracakraprayogā tu sā eva mukhatoddhṛtā // (2029)

	vajraratnāṅkurāṃ baddhvā sarvāṅgulyaḥ prasārayet /
	tāṃ tu mūrdhni pratiṣṭhāpya ratnavṛṣṭiṃ tu varṣayet // (2030)

	sā eva cakrayogā tu hṛdi ratnadvidhīkṛtā /
	maṇigrahāgradaṃṣṭrā tu muṣṭir madhyamasaṃdhitā // iti (2031)

tataḥ samayamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	etā eva mahāmudrāḥ saṃpuṭīkṛtya bandhayet /
	guhyaguhyāḥ samāsena siddhiṃ dadyuś caturguṇam // iti (2032)

	yathā yad vajraguhye tu sarvakālaṃ na bandhayet /
	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmamudrāḥ samāsataḥ // iti (2033)

	traiḥ /
	graiḥ /
	haiḥ /
	saiḥ /
	gryaḥ /
	khaḥ /
	dvyaiḥ /
	haiḥ /
	dhraiḥ /
	dhryaiḥ /
	kraiḥ /
	vaiḥ /
	kyaḥ /
	raiḥ /
	vyaḥ /
	maiḥ // (2034)

	guhyaguhyāgramuṣṭis tu dvidhīkṛtya sarvakarmikā // iti // (2035)

sarvatathāgatakarmasamayān mahākalparājād ratnaguhyamudrāmaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ // // (2036)


ratnajñānamaṇḍalavidhivistara (2037)

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatābhiṣekajñānasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhanaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekajñānottama hūṃ // (2038)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajrajñānābhiṣekasamaya hūṃ // (2039)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ maṇiratnābhiṣekajñāna hūṃ // (2040)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ dharmābhiṣekajñāna hūṃ // (2041)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imaṃ svavidyottamam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvābhiṣekajñāna hūṃ // (2042)

athākāśagarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ svakulajñānamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (2043)

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jñānamaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ ratnajñānam iti smṛtam // (2044)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	hṛdi cihnās tu saṃlekhyā dharmamanḍalayogataḥ // iti (2045)

athātra maṇḍale jñānahṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ sarvārthasiddhijñāna hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇijñāna hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇijñānaṅkuśa //
	oṃ maṇijñānarāga //
	oṃ maṇijñānatuṣṭi // (2046)

	oṃ maṇijñānadṛṣṭi hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇijñānābhiṣeka //
	oṃ maṇijñānasūrya //
	oṃ maṇijñānadhvaja //
	oṃ maṇijñānāṭṭahāsa // (2047)

	oṃ maṇijñānapadma hūṃ //
	oṃ jñānamaṇityāga //
	oṃ jñānamaṇikośa //
	oṃ jñānamaṇicakra //
	oṃ jñānamaṇibhāṣa // (2048)

	oṃ jñānamaṇiratnavarṣa //
	oṃ maṇijñānanṛtyapūjāsamaya //
	oṃ maṇijñānarakṣa //
	oṃ maṇijñānayakṣa //
	oṃ maṇijñānamuṣṭi(or -muṣṭe?) // (2049)

athātra maṇḍale yathāvad vidhivistaraṃ kṛtvā,
śiṣyān evaṃ brūyāt /:

	na tvayādṛṣṭadharmamaṇḍalasya vaktavyam /
	mā te maraṇakālaḥ śīghram evāsiddhasya syāt /

ity uktvā (2050)

maṇikuladharmajñānāny utpādayet //:

	vajragarbhaṃ samālikhya paṭādiṣu samādhinā /
	bhāvayan yācayed arthān dehi ratna iti bruvan // (2051)

	vajragarbhaṃ samālikhya paṭādiṣu samādhinā /
	bhāvayan yācayed ratnān dehi dehīti vāg bruvan // (2052)

	vajragarbhaṃ samālikhya paṭādiṣu vibhāvayan /
	samāpattyā tu saddharmaṃ dehi jñāneti yācayet // (2053)

	vajragarbhaṃ samālikhya paṭādiṣu vibhāvayan /
	samāpattyā tu satkarma karme dehīti yācayet // iti (2054)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ dehi sarvārthān bhagavan vajragarbha //
	oṃ dehi sarvaratnān bhagavan vajragarbha //
	oṃ dehi saddharmaṃ bhagvan vajragarbha satsattva //
	oṃ dehi bhagavan satkarma bhagavan vajragarbha // (2055)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā bhāvyan susamāhitaḥ /
	ākāśagarbhaṃ satsatvaṃ yācayed arthasaṃpadaḥ // (2056)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	ākāśagarbhaṃ satsattvaṃ yācayed ratnasaṃcayam // (2057)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā bhavayan susamāhitaḥ /
	ākāśagarbhaṃ satsattvaṃ yācayed dharmasaṃpadaḥ // (2058)

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	ākāśagarbhaṃ satsattvaṃ yācayet karmasaṃcayam // iti (2059)

atraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ jñānagarbha dehi sarvārthān //
	oṃ jñānagarbha dehi sarvaratnān //
	oṃ jñānagarbha dehi sarvadharmān //
	oṃ jñānagarbha dehi sarmakarmān // (2060)

	vajragarbhaṃ hṛdi likhya bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	yadā tu hṛdayaṃ kampet tataḥ siddho dhanaṃ dadet // (2061)

	vajragarbhaṃ lalāṭe tu samālikhya vibhāvayan /
	yadā tu karmapate śīrṣam abhiṣekaṃ sa lapsyati // (2062)

	vajragarbhaṃ mukhe viddhvā lābhayet tatra eva hi /
	yadā tu sphuṭate tat tu tadā vāg asya sidhyati // (2063)

	vajragarbhaṃ svamūrdhne tu pratiṣṭhāpya bhāvayet /
	yadā tu jvalate tat tu tadaivordhvaṃgamo bhavet // iti (2064)

tatiraṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ hṛdayagarbha dehi dhanam //
	oṃ ratnābhiṣekagarbhābhiṣiñca //
	oṃ vāggarbha sidhya //
	oṃ ratnagarbhoṣṇīṣākāśaṃ gaccha // (2065)

	vajragarbhamahāmudrāṃ bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	yācayed dehi siddhiṃ me ili ratneti sidhyati // (2066)

	ākāśagarbhasamayīṃ baddhvā tu samāhitaḥ /
	yācayed abhiṣekāṇi mili ratneti lapsyati // (2067)

	vajragarbhasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	yācayed dehi me dharmaṃ cili ratneti lapsyati // (2068)

	ākāśagarbhakarmagrīṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	yācayet sarvaratnāni kili ratneti sidhyati // (2069)

atraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ ili //
	oṃ mili //
	oṃ cili //
	oṃ kili // (2070)

tato maṇijñānarahasyamudrājñānāni bhavanti //:

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā vajragarbhaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā parāṃ siddhim avāpnute //(2071)

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā vajragarbhaṃ tu bhāvayet /
	ālekhyaṃ citralikhitaṃ prāpnuyād abhiṣecanam // (2072)

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā vajragarbhaṃ tu bhāvayan /
	taṃ priyaṃ yasya ramayet sarvalokaṃ sa rāgayet // (2073)

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā vajragarbhaṃ tu bhāvayan /
	sarvākāśarajobimbaiḥ sarvasiddhir bhaved dhruvam // iti (2074)

tatrāsāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	ākāśaguhyajñāna sādhaya hūṃ //
	cittaguhyajñānābhiṣiñca hūṃ //
	priyānusmṛtijñānaguhya sarvalokaṃ rāmaya hūṃ //
	sarvaguhyajñāna sarvasiddhiṃ me prayaccha hūṃ // (2075)

tato mahāmudrāṃ yathāvad badhnīyāt /
tādṛśaiva siddhiḥ // (2076)

tato dharmasamayamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:
vajramaṇiṃ vajrajñānamaṇḍalayogena sthāpayet // (2077)

atha dharmamudrā bhavanti //:

	saḥ /
	rāḥ /
	gaḥ /
	sāḥ /
	raḥ /
	teḥ /
	keḥ /
	hāḥ /
	dhaṃ /
	tīḥ /
	he /
	bhā /
	ka /
	raṃ /
	yaḥ /
	saḥ / (2078)

	karmamudrāḥ samāsena yathāsthāneṣu saṃsthapet // iti // (2079)

sarvatathāgatakarmasamayān mahākalparājād ratnajñānamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (2080)


ratnakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistara

atha bhagavān punar api sarvatathāgatābhiṣekakarmasamayasaṃbhavādhiṣṭhānaṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ sarvatathāgatakarmābhiṣeka hūṃ // (2081)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva imāṃ svakarmasaṃbhavāṃ vidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajrahūṃkārābhiṣeke // (2082)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //

	oṃ sarvākāśasamatābhiṣkekaratne hūṃ //
	oṃ sarvatathāgatasamantābhiṣeka hūṃ // (2083)

atha vajranetro bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhaṣat //

	oṃ saddharmābhiṣekaratne // (2084)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattva imāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ viśvābhiṣeke // (2085)

athākāśagarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ svakulakarmamaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (2086

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi karmamaṇḍalam uttamam /
	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ ratnakarmam iti smṛtam // (2087)

	mahāmaṇḍalayogena sūtrayet sarvamaṇḍalam /
	tasya madhye yathānyāyaṃ buddhabimbaṃ niveśayet // (2088)

	mahāsattvaprayogeṇa ratnasattvaḥ samālikhet // iti (2089)

tatrāsāṃ mudrā bhavanti //:

	oṃ maṇiratnapūjāgrya //
	oṃ sarvārthasiddhivajraratnābhiṣeke hūṃ //
	oṃ vajramaṇidhāriṇisamaye hūṃ // (2090)

	oṃ maṇiratnākarṣakarmasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnarāgaratikarmapūje pravarta //
	oṃ maṇiratnasādhukārapūjāsamaye // (2091)

	oṃ mahāmaṇiratnadṛṣṭyākarṣe //
	oṃ maṇiratnamālāpūje //
	oṃ maṇiratnasūryālokapūje //
	oṃ maṇiratnadhvajapatākāpūje //
	oṃ maṇiratnāṭṭahāsapūje // (2092)

	oṃ padmamaṇisamādhisamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ sarvatyāgānusmṛtisamādhikarmakāri hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnatīkṣṇasamaye chinda cchinda hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnacakrasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnabhāṣe vada vada hūṃ // (2093)

	oṃ maṇiratnavṛṣṭikarmasamaye hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnakarmaṇi hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnakavace rakṣa hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnadaṃṣṭri khāda khāda hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnakarmamuṣṭi hūṃ // (2094)

	oṃ maṇiratnalāsye pūjaya hoḥ //
	oṃ maṇiratnamālābhiṣeke pūjaya //
	oṃ maṇiratnagīte pūjaya //
	oṃ maṇiratnanṛtye pūjaya // (2095)

	oṃ maṇiratnadhūpe pūjaya //
	oṃ maṇiratnapuṣpe pūjaya //
	oṃ maṇiratnadīpe pūjaya //
	oṃ maṇiratnagandhe pūjaya // (2096)

	oṃ maṇiratnāṅkuśyākarṣe jjaḥ //
	oṃ maṇiratnapāśe hūṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnasphoṭe vaṃ //
	oṃ maṇiratnāveśe aḥ // (2097)

athātra karmamaṇḍale yathāvad vidhivistaraṃ kṛtvā,
praveśyaivaṃ vadet /

	na tvayā kasyacid ayaṃ vaktavyaḥ /
	mā te karmāvaraṇādhiṣṭhitasyaiva maraṇaṃ bhavet

ity uktvā, (2098)

maṇikarmajñānāni śikṣayet //

	vajragarbhamahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	pūjayan sarvapūjābhiḥ sarvabuddhān vaśaṃ nayet // (2099)

	baddhvā caikatarāṃ mudrāṃ samayāgrīṃ samādhinā /
	pūjayan sarvabuddhāṃs tu svabhiṣekān sa lapsyati // (2100)

	vajragarbhasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pūjayan sarvabuddhāṃs tu nāśayej jagad uttamam // (2101)

	baddhvā karmamayīṃ mudrāṃ vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	pūjayan sarvabuddhāṃs tu sarvārthāṃl labhate kṣaṇāt // iti (2102)

tatraiṣāṃ hṛdayāni bhavanti //:

	oṃ ratnapūja vaśīkuru //
	oṃ ratnapūjāsamayābhiṣiñca //
	oṃ ratnapūjādharma nāśaya patim //
	oṃ ratnapūjākarma sarvārthān me dada // (2103)

atha rahasyamudrākarmajñānaṃ bhavati //:

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	pūjayan sarvabuddhāṃs tu sarvalokaṃ sa rāgayet // iti (2104)

tato yathāvan mahāmudrājñānenottamasiddhaya iti // (2105)

atha samayamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //

	vajraratnaṃ samādhāya sarvasthāneṣu saṃsthapet /
	vajrakāryaprayogeṇa yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ // (2106)

atha dharmamudrājñānaṃ bhavanti //:

	tvaḥ /
	jaḥ /
	gaḥ /
	dhuḥ /
	nuḥ /
	jāḥ /
	bhuḥ /
	śaḥ /
	rmmāḥ /
	kṣṇaḥ /
	nuḥ /
	ṣaḥ /
	rmaḥ /
	kṣaḥ /
	kṣaḥ /
	dhiḥ // (2107)

	vajraratnāṃ dvidhīkṛtya karmamudrāḥ sa sādhayet // iti (2108)

sarvatathāgatakarmasamayān mahākalparājād ratnakarmamaṇḍalavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (2109)


atha bhagavān ratnamudrāṃ nāma samādhiṃ samāpadyemāṃ svavidyottamām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajraratne trāṃ // (2110)

atha vajrapāṇir bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajramāle hūṃ // (2111)

atha vajragarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	om maniratne // (2112)

atha vajranetro bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //:

	om dharmaratne // (2115)

atha vajraviśvo bodhisattvo mahāsattva imāṃ svamudrām abhāṣat //

	oṃ viśvavṛṣṭi // (2114)

athāryākāśagarbho bidhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ maṇikulacaturmudrāmaṇḍalam abhāṣat //: (2115)

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mudrāmaṇḍalam uttamam /
	caturmudrāprayogeṇa maṇḍalaṃ parikalpayet // (2116)

tato yathāvat praveśya śikṣayet /:

	na tvayā kasya cid vaktavyam

iti // (2117)

tato jṇānāny utpādayet //:

	vajraratnaṃ samādhāya vajraratnasamādhinā /
	lalāṭe tu pratiṣṭhāpya sarvasiddhim avapnuyat // iti ( 2118)

athātra hṛdayaṃ bhavati //:

	oṃ vajraratna sarvābhiṣekasarvasiddhayo me prayaccha rala rala hūṃ traḥ // (2119)

tato rahasyamudrāṃ darśayet //:

	paṭiṃ vāpi priyāṃ vā pi striyaṃ vā puruṣo 'pi vā /
	lalāṭadvayasaṃdhānād buddhaṃ dvāv api sidhyataḥ // (2120)

tatrāsyāḥ sādhanahṛdayaṃ bhavati //:

	oṃ vajraratna sakhividyādharatvaṃ prayaccha śīghram abhiṣiñcāhi
	ha ha ha ha trāḥ // (2121)

tato yathāvac caturmudrābandhaṃ caturvidhiṃ śikṣayet /
tathaiva sidhya iti //
catumudrāmaṇḍalam // (2122)

athākāśagarbho bodhisattvo mahāsattva idaṃ sarvārthasiddhiṃ nāma hṛdayam abhāṣat //:

	oṃ vajramaṇidhara sarvārthasiddhiṃ me prayaccha
	ho bhagavan vajraratna hūṃ // (2123)

athātra maṇḍalaṃ bhavati //:

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāmaṇḍalam uttamam /
	yathāvat tu samālekhyaṃ sarvasiddhes tu maṇḍalam // iti (2124)

athātra jñānarahasyamudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //:

	rūpādīnāṃ tu kāmānām aviraktaḥ sukhāni tu /
	niryātayaṃs tu buddhebhyaḥ kalpasiddhim avāpunte // iti (2125)

tataś caturvidhaṃ mudrājñānaṃ śikṣayet //
evaṃ paṭādiṣu sattvaṃ mudrāṃ vā maṇḍaleṣu likhya sādhayed iti // (2126)

atha sarvatathāgataḥ punaḥ samājam āgamyākāśagarbhaṃ mahābodhisattvam anena sādhkāradānenācchāditavantaḥ // (2127)

	sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /
	sādhu te vajradharmāya sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe // (2128)

	subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /
	sarvatāthāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham // iti (2129)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvatathāgatakarmasamayo nāma mahākalparājaḥ parisamāptaḥ // (2130)

(2131: no text)

sarvakalpopāyasiddhividhivistaratantra (2132)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattva idaṃ sarvatathāgatamahātattvavidhivistaratantram udājahāra //: (2133)

(2134: no text)

tatra prathamaṃ tāvat tathāgatamahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //: (2135)

	tathāgatamahāmudrāṃ baddhvā sarvakhadhātuṣu /
	buddhabimbān adhiṣṭhāya svahṛdi tu praveśayet // (2136)

	ihaiva janmani varaṃ yadīcched uttamaṃ śivam /
	buddhatvaṃ tena kāryedaṃ na cet siddhir yathopari // (2137)

((atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvas tathāgatakulottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //:)) (2138)

((tatra prathamaṃ tāvan mahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //)) (2139)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya mahātattvam udāharan /
	padaśaḥ sarvam evāhaṃ bhāvayet sattvayogataḥ // (2140)

	ihaiva janmani padaṃ yadīcchet sauriṇaṃ śubham /
	ātmanas tena kāryedaṃ na cet siddhir yathopari // (2141)

atha samayamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //: (2142)

	yathā vajradharaḥ siddhis tathāham iti bhāvayan /
	buddhasauritvam āpnoti na cet siddhir yathopari // iti (2143)

atha dharmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavanti //: (2144)

	svabhāvaśuddhyā vācā vai sarvadharmā iti bruvan /
	buddhasauritvam āpnoti na cet siddhir yathopari // iti (2145)

atha karmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //: (2146)

	sarvasya sarvaśuddhitvāt sarvakarmāṇi śodhayan /
	buddhasauritvam āpnoti na cet siddhir yathopari // iti (2147)

tathāgatakulottamasiddhayaḥ // (2148)

atha vajrapāṇiḥ svakulottamasiddhitantram udājahāra // (2149)

((tatra prathamaṃ tāvan mahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati)): (2150)

	buddhājñāt sarvasattvārthāt sarvasiddhiprayogataḥ /
	sādhayaṃs tu mahāmudrāṃ buddhatvam iha janmani // iti (2151)

atha samayamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	yathā vajradharaḥ siddhas tathāham iti bhāvayan /
	mahāmudrāprayogeṇa kṣaṇāt sauritvam āpnute // iti  (2152)

atha dharmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	anakṣareṣu dharmeṣu prapañco na hi vidyate /
	idaṃ vadaṃs tu dharmāgrīṃ bhāvayan sauritāṃ vrajet // iti (2153)

atha karmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	yat karoti hi karmaṃ vai śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham /
	niryātayañ jinebhyas tu kṣaṇāt sauritāṃ vrajet // iti (2154)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ padmakulottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2155)

tatra prathamaṃ tāvan mahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	rāgaḥ śuddhaḥ svabhāvena tīrthikair avamanyate /
	tasyāvirāgo dharmo 'smin mahāyāne tu sidhyati // iti (2156)

atha samayamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	abhyasaṃs tu mahāmaitrīṃ samādhidṛḍhayogataḥ /
	sphārayed vidhivad yogāt kṣaṇāt sauritvam āpnuyāt // iti (2157)

atha dharmamudrotamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	svabhāvaśuddhaḥ saṃrāga iti brūyād imaṃ nayam /
	rāgapāramitāprāptaḥ kṣaṇāt sauritvam āpnuyāt // iti (2158)

atha karmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	darśanasparśanābhyāṃ tu śravaṇasmaraṇena vā /
	syām ahaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ sarvaduḥkhāntakasiddhiḥ // iti (2159)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvo maṇikulottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2160)

tatra mahāmudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	sarvabuddhābhiṣeko 'haṃ bhaveyaṃ vajrgarbhavat /
	iti bhāvanāṃ bhāvayan vai kṣaṇāt sauritvam āpnute // iti (2161)

atha samayamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	bhaveyaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ sarvāśāparipūrakaḥ /
	ākāśagarbhasadṛśaḥ kṣaṇāt sauritvam āpnute // iti (2162)

atha dharmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	ātmanas tu samutsṛjya dhanadān suharṣitaḥ /
	vadan dharmamayīṃ mudrām iha sauritvam āpnute // iti (2163)

atha karmamudrottamasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	daridrāṇāṃ hitārthāya dhanotpādanatatparaḥ /
	udyogāt sauritāṃ yāti na cet siddhir yathopari // iti (2164)

sarvakulamudrāṇāṃ buddhabodhisattvottamasiddhyavāptividhivistaraḥ // // (2165)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar api sarvatathāgatasamayasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2166)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //

	yasya rāgasamāpattis tasya rāgeṇa śodhayet /
	iti buddhamahāmudrājñānasya samayaḥ smṛtaḥ // (2167)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	kāmānām avirāgas tu samayaḥ sumahānayam /
	tathāgatakule śuddho nātikramyo jinair api // (2168)

atha vajrakulasamayasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	akrodhasyāpi sattvārthān mahākrodhapradarśanam /
	mahāvajrakule tv eṣa samayo duratikramaḥ // (2169)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamayasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	svabhāvaśuddhajñānena kuryād yathābhirucitaḥ /
	mahāpadmakule tv eṣa samayo duratikramaḥ // (2170)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamayasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	alpatve vā bahutve vā yathābhirucitaṃ punaḥ /
	avandhyo divaśaḥ kāryo dānena samayo hy ayam // iti (2171)

sarvakulasamayasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2172)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmamudrājñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2173)

tatredaṃ tathāgatadharmasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	buddho dharma iti khyāta ity uktvā dharmatākṣaram /
	buddhadharmamahāmudrājñānasya paramaṃ nayam // (2174)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmasiddhitantram //

	rāgāc chuddhataro nāsti dharmaḥ sarvasukhapradaḥ /
	tathāgatakule 'py eṣa dharmaḥ siddhikaraḥ paraḥ // (2175)

tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmasiddhitantram //:

	buddhājñāc chodanārthād vā sattvatrāṇārthatas tathā /
	akruddho 'pi hi saṃduṣṭān mārayañ chuddhim āpnute // (2176)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmasiddhitantram //

	aliptaṃ salilaiḥ padmaṃ tathā rāgo na duṣyati /
	iti bruvann akāryāṇi kurvan pāpair na lipyate // (2177)

tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmasiddhitantram //

	dānāt samo na dharmo 'sti pratipattyā bravīti hi /
	mahāmaṇikuladharmaḥ, na cet siddhir yathopari // iti (2178)

sarvakuladharmasiddhividhivistaratantram // (2179)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2180)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	buddhatvaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ bodhisattvatvam eva ca /
	yathāvad vinayaṃś caiva karmamudrāgrasiddhidā // (2181)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulakarmasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	caturvidhābhiḥ pūjābhiḥ sadāyogāc caturvidham /
	catuḥkālaprayogeṇa kurvan karmāṇi sādhayet // (2182)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakarmasiddhitantram //

	duṣṭasattvopaghātāya yad yat kāryaṃ karoti saḥ /
	karmavajrakule 'py eṣa sarvasiddhipradāyakaḥ // (2183)

tatredaṃ padmakulakarmasiddhitantram //:

	bhayātmanām abhayado yathāvad vinayaṃs tathā /
	etat padmakulakarmabuddhasiddhipradāyakam // (2184)

atha maṇikulakarmasiddhitantram //

	abhiṣekas tathā dānaṃ sarvāśāparipūrayaḥ /
	buddhānāṃ dehināṃ caiva karma sarvārthasādhakam // iti (2185)

sarvakulakarmasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2186)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmatāmudrājñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2187)

tatredaṃ tathāgatadharmatājñānasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	vajrasattvasamādhis tu buddhānāṃ dharmatā smṛtā /
	etad buddhasya buddhatvaṃ na buddho bhavate 'nyataḥ // (2188)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmatājñānasiddhitantram //

	bhāvayaṃs tu mahāmudrāṃ sādhayet sarvasiddhayaḥ /
	tathāgatakule 'py eṣa dharmatottamasiddhidā // (2189)

tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmatājñānasiddhitantram //:

	baddhābhiḥ samayāgryābhiḥ sarvakarmāṇi sādhayet /
	mahāmudrāprayogeṇa vajrasiddhim avāpnuyāt // (2190)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmatājñānasiddhitantram //:

	dharmamudrāprayogeṇa dharmamudrā pravartayet /
	anayā sādhayan dharmān dharmatā vajradharminaḥ // (2191)

tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmatājñānasiddhitantram //:

	karmamudrāprayogeṇa karmavajraṃ hṛdi sthitam /
	bhāvayan dharmatām etām avāpnoti svakarmatām // iti (2192)

sarvakuladharmatājñānasiddhitantram // // (2193)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatthāgatajñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2194)

tatredaṃ tathāgatajñānasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	vajrasattvasamādhisthaś candravajraprayogataḥ /
	yathāvarṇe tu tau vetti tathā lokaṃ tu vetti saḥ // (2195)

	śuddhe śuddham iti jñeyaṃ pāṇḍare tu prabhāsvaram /
	rakte raktaṃ taraṃ kruddhaṃ yādṛgvarṇatadātmakam // (2196)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulajñānasiddhitantram //

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya candramaṇḍalasaprabhām /
	svayaṃ kāyaṃ yathā vetti tathā vedyaṃ jaganmanaḥ // (2197)

tatredaṃ vajrakulajñānasiddhitantram //:

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā kruddhaḥ san maṇḍalāni tu /
	yādṛśāni tu paśyed vai vijñeyaṃ tādṛśaṃ mahaḥ // (2198)

tatredaṃ padmakulajñānasiddhitantram //

	sūkṣmam akṣarapaṅkutir vā paśyann ākāśabhūmiṣu /
	yādṛgvarṇaṃ samāsena vetti cittaṃ sa tādṛśam // (2199)

tatredaṃ maṇikulajñānasiddhitantram //:

	sarvalokaṃ nirīkṣan vai pratibhāso hi yādṛśaḥ /
	paśyate tādṛśaṃ caiva jagaccittaṃ tu lakṣayet // iti (2200)

	etā eva samāpattyo gamanāgamanāni tu /
	kurvantyaś ca bhramantyo vā yathā paśyet tathā gamaḥ // (2201)

	yasya yasya ca sattvasya samāpattya tu cintayet /
	tasya tasya tathā caiva sarvacittāni budhyati // (2202)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // // (2203)

sarvakulajñānasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2204)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasiddhijñānatantram udājahāra //: (2205)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasiddhijñānatantram //:

	sattvādhiṣṭhānayogena buddhabimbātmabhāvanā /
	anena jñānayogena buddhasiddhim avāpnuyāt // (2206)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasiddhijñānatantram //:

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā śvetapītābhamaṇḍalān /
	svamudrāsattvam ātmānaṃ sākṣād iva sa paśyati // (2207)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasiddhijñānatantram //:

	tādṛśeṣv eva bimbeṣu madhye śyāmaṃ niyacchati /
	siddhir vajrakulasyāgrā bhavec chīghraṃ yad icchati // (2208)

tatredaṃ padmakulasiddhijñānatantram //:

	tāny evākāśanīlāni padmākārāṇi paśyati /
	mahāpadmakule vidyāsiddhayaḥ saṃ bhavanti hi // (2209)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasiddhijñānatantram //:

	ākāśe vānyadeśe vā ta evākāśanirmalāḥ /
	sphuranto raśmimaṇḍāni paśyan siddhiṃ laghv āpnuyāt // iti (2210)

	vajrasattvādayaḥ sattvāś candramaṇḍalasaprabhāḥ /
	prāg darśayanti cātmānaṃ siddhikāle svarūptataḥ // // (2211)

sarvakulasiddhijñānavistaratantram // // (2212)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatābhijñāsiddhijñānamudrātantram udājahāra //: (2213)

tatredaṃ tathāgatābhijñāsiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhisthaḥ sarvakāye tathāgatān /
	bhāvayan bodhisattvāṃś ca darśayet kāyatas tathā // (2214)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulābhijñāsiddhitantram //

	vajrasattvamahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñām avāpnoti vidhinā tena sādhakaḥ // (2215)

tatredaṃ divyacakṣurjñānaṃ bhavati //:

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya cakṣur vijñānam āvahet /
	tena yac cintayet kiñcit sudūrād api paśyati // (2216)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2217)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya śotravijñānam āvahet /
	tena yac cintayet kāryaṃ sudūrasthaṃ śṛṇoti hi // (2218)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2219)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya manovijñānam āvahet /
	tena yaṃ sattvam udvīkṣec cittaṃ jānāti tasya saḥ // (2220)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya ātmano vā parasya vā /
	manasā paśyate rūpaṃ yato janma sa āvahet // (2221)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2222)


atha rddhividhijñānasiddhir bhavati // (2223)

	mahāmudrāṃ samādhāya yāṃ yām ṛddhim abhīpsati /
	yatra vā tatra vā tad vai saṃdarśayet samādhinā // (2224)

ity āha bhagavān mahābodhicittaḥ // (2225)


tatredaṃ vajrakulābhijñāsiddhitantram //:

	trilokavijayāgrīṃ vai baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñām avāpnoti vidhinā tena sādhakaḥ // (2226)

	kurddhaḥ san sarvakāryāṇi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	divyacakṣvādiyogena sarvābhijñānatve kṣaṇāt // (2227)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2228)

tatredaṃ padmakulābhijñāsiddhitantram //:

	jagadvinayamudrāgrīṃ saṃdhāya susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñām avāpnoti vidhinā tena sādhakaḥ // (2229)

	rāgākulas tu vidhivad yathānukramatas tathā /
	divyacakṣuvādiyogena sarvābhijño bhaviṣyati // (2230)

ity āha bhagavāṃl lokeśvaraḥ // (2231)

tatredaṃ maṇikulābhijñāsiddhitantram //:

	sarvārthasiddhisanmudrāṃ baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñām avāpnoti vidhinā tena sādhakaḥ // (2232)

	buddhapūjāṃ prakurvan vai yathānukramatas tathā /
	divyacakṣvādiyogena pañcābhijñāṃ sa paśyati // (2233)

iti āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2234)

sarvakulābhijñāsiddhijñānavidhivistaratantram // // (2235)


atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasatyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2236)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasatyasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	satyānuparivrtinyā vācā tu śapathakriyā /
	pālayaṃs tu mahāsatyaṃ laghu buddhatvam āpnuyāt // (2237)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2238)


tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasatyasiddhitantram //:

	samaye śapathā kāryā tthāgatakulodgatā /
	pālayan vajrasatyaṃ tu siddhim agryām avāpnute // (2239)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2240)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasatyasiddhitantram //:

	vajradhāryām u śapathāṃ kṛtvā tu duratikramām /
	pālayet satyam etad dhi yadīcchet siddhim uttamām // (2241)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2242)

tatnredaṃ padmakulasatyasiddhitantram //:

	saddharmaśaptathāṃ kṛtvā mahāpadmakulottamām /
	pālayet satyasamayaṃ yadīcchet siddhim uttamām // (2243)

it āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2244)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasatyasiddhitantram //:

	buddhapūjāsu śapathāṃ kṛtvā tu duratikramām /
	pālayed uttamaṃ satyam abhiṣekaṃ sa lapsyati // (2245)

ity āha bhagavān buddhapūjā //

sarvakulaśapathasiddhitantram // // (2247)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayatattvasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2248)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayatattvasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	samayas tvam iti prokte sarvamudrākuleṣv api /
	svayaṃ baddhvā dṛḍhaṃ yānti tataḥ paścād asādhitāḥ // (2249)

ity āha bhagavān mahāsamayatattvaḥ // (2250)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayatattvasiddhitantram //:

	suratas tvam iti proite sarvamudrā asādhitāḥ /
	svayaṃ baddhvā tu sidhyante tattvacodān mahātmanaḥ // (2251)

ity āha bhagavān mahāsamayatattvaḥ // (2252)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamayatattvasiddhitantram //:

	ekahūṃkāramātreṇa sarvamudrāḥ samāsataḥ /
	svayaṃ bandhed bandayed vāpi svayaṃ vāpi parasya vā // iti (2253)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamayatattvasiddhitantram //:

	sarvaśuddha iti prokte svato vāpi parasya vā /
	strīsaṅgādyās tu saṃyogā na mokṣaṃ yānti sarvaśaḥ // iti (2254)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamayatattvasiddhitantram //:

	oṃkāreṇaiva sidhyante sarvamudrā samāsataḥ /
	sarvalokeṣu caivāgryāḥ pūjāś caiva svayaṃbhuvām // iti (2255)

sarvakulasamayatattvasiddhimudrāvidhivistaratantram // // (2256)


atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasiddhimudrātantram udājahāra //: (2257)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	buddhamudrāṃ tu saṃdhāya tathāgatam anusmaran /
	sādhayan sidhyate śīghraṃ buddhabodhir api sthirā // (2258)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattvamahāmudrāṃ baddhvā tu paribhāvayan /
	purato vajrasattvaṃ ca siddhiḥ śīghratarā bhavet // (2259)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasiddhitatnram //:

	baddhvā tu samayāgrīṃ vai vajrasattvasamādhinā /
	bhāvayan vajrasattvaṃ ca siddhis tu dviguṇā bhavet // (2260)

tatredaṃ padmakulasiddhitantram //:

	baddhvā dharmamayīṃ mudrāṃ lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	bhāvayaṃl lokanāthaṃ ca siddhis tu dviguṇā bhavet // (2261)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasiddhitantram //:

	karmamudrāṃ samādhāya vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	bhāvayan vajragarbhaṃ ca siddhis tu dviguṇā bhavet // (2262)

sarvakulasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2263)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasarvasiddhisādhanatantram udājahāra //: (2264)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasarvasiddhisādhanatantram //:

	ātmano vātha purato buddhānsmṛtisādhakaḥ /
	baddhvā vai sarvamudrās tu tataḥ sidhyanti tatkṣaṇāt // (2265)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2266)

tatredaṃ tathagatakulasarvasiddhisādhanatantram //:

	sādhayet sarvamudrās tu kāmo 'ham iti bhāvayan /
	vajrajāpaprayogeṇa sarvasiddhyagrasādhanam // (2267)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2268)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasarvasiddhisādhanatantram //:

	vajrabimbaṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	badhnīyāt sarvamudrās tu siddhiṃ yānti hi tatkṣaṇāt // (2279)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatavajraḥ // (2270)

tatredaṃ padmakulasiddhisādhanatantram //:

	padmabimbaṃ svam ātmānaṃ bhāvayan svayam ātmanā /
	sarvajñānamayī siddhir mahāpadmakule psyate(?) // (2271)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2272)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasarvasiddhisādhanatantram //:

	bhāvayet svayam ātmānaṃ maṇiratnaṃ karojjvalam /
	sarvapūjāmayī siddhir mahāmaṇikule smṛtā // (2273)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2274)

sarvakulottamasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2275)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatādhiṣṭhānamudrāsiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2276)

tatredaṃ tathāgatādhiṣṭhānasiddhitantram //:

	vajradhātvīśvarīṃ mudrāṃ baddhvā tu samāhitaḥ /
	hṛdy ūrṇāyāṃ gale mūrdhni sthāpya buddhair adhiṣṭhyate // (2277)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2278)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulādhiṣṭhānasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	sattvavajrīṃ dṛḍhikṛtya vajrasattvsamādhinā /
	hṛdy ūrṇāyāṃ tathā kaṇṭhe mūrdhni sthāpyādhiṣṭhyate // (2279)

tatredaṃ vajrakulādhiṣṭhānasiddhitantram //

	vajrahūṃkāramudrāṃ vai baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	hṛdy ūrṇākaṇṭhamūrdhasthā samādhiṣṭhāti tatkṣaṇāt // (2280)

ity āha bhagavān vajranāthaḥ // (2281)

tatresaṃ padmakulādhiṣṭhānasiddhitantram //:

	vajrapadmāṃ dṛḍhīkṛtya lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	hṛdy urṇākaṇṭha mūrdhasthā svāshiṣṭhānāya kalpate // (2282)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2283)

tatredaṃ maṇikulādhiṣṭhānasiddhitantram //:

	mahāvajramaṇiṃ baddhvā vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	hṛdy ūrṇākaṇṭhamūrdhasthā svadhiṣṭhānāya kapayet // (2284)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // (2285)

sarvakulādhiṣṭhānasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2286)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatābhiṣekamudrāsiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2287)

tatredaṃ tathāgatābhiṣekasiddhitantram //:

	vajraratnāṃ samādhāya lalāṭe tu pratiṣṭhitām /
	kṛtvā tu vajraratnety abhiṣikto jinair bhavet // (2288)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2289)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulābhiṣekasiddhitantram //:

	vajradhātvīśvaryādyābhir buddhamudrābhir agrataḥ /
	samārabhya catuḥpārśve mālayā tv abhiṣicyati // iti (2290)

tatredaṃ vajrakulābhiṣekasiddhitantram //:

	vajrābhiṣekamālāṃ tu saṃdhāyaca lalāṭagām /
	tayā mālābhiṣekeṇa vajiriṇā so 'bhiṣicyati // iti (2291)

tatredaṃ padmakulābhiṣekasiddhitantram //: (2292)

	dharmavajrīṃ samādhāya puraḥ śīrṣe pratiṣṭhitām /
	tayābhiṣikto buddhais tu lokeśavarye 'bhiṣicyati // (2293)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2294)

tatredaṃ maṇikulābhiṣekasiddhitantram //: (2295)

	vajraratnāṅkurāṃ baddhvā lalāṭe tu pratiṣṭhām /
