	tayābhiṣikto buddhais tu pūjaiśvarye 'bhiṣicyati // (2296)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ //  (2297)

sarvakulābhiṣekasiddhitantram // // (2298)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasamādhisiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2299)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamādhisiddhitantram //:

	ākārataḥ sarvabuddhānāṃ mudrāṃ baddhvā samāhitaḥ /
	japan vai mantravidyās tu śīghraṃ siddhim avāpnute // (2300)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2301)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasamādhisiddhitantram //

	samādhir vajradharmeṇa sattvādhiṣṭhānayogataḥ /
	hṛnmudrāmantravidyās tu śīghraṃ sidhyati jāpataḥ // (2302)

ity āha bhagavān buddhasamādhiḥ // (2303)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamādhisiddhitantram //:

	rāgāt tvam asi saṃbhūtaḥ krodho 'ham iti bhāvayan /
	hṛnmudrāmantravidyānām āśusiddhikaraṃ bhavet // (2204)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2205)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamādhisiddhitantram //:

	mantrīspharaṇatāyogaḥ sādhayed dhṛdayādayaḥ /
	lokeśvarakule jāpaḥ siddhiṃ śīghram avāpnute // (2206)

ity āha bhagavān āryāvalokiteśvaraḥ // (2207)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamādhisiddhitantram //

	sarvākāśasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	hṛnmudrāmantravidyās tu samādhayaṃs tu sarvago bhavet // (2308)

ity āha ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2309)

sarvakulasamādhisiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2310)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatapūjāmudrāsiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2311)

tatredaṃ tathāgatapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	pūrvaṃ dhūpādibhiḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	tatas tu siddhikāmo vai sādhayan siddhim āpnuyāt // iti (2312)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	guhyapūjācatuṣkeṇa pūjāguhyam udāharan /
	ātmaniryātanādyair vā pūjāṃ kurvaṃs tu sidhyati // (2313)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2314)

tatredaṃ vajrakulapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	krodhavajramahāpūjāṃ krodhaguhyam udāharan /
	krodhamuṣṭiṃ prakurvan vai śīghraṃ sidhyet kulaṃ mama // (2315)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2316)

tatredaṃ padmakulapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	gambhīrodārasūtrāntaprayogasamudāhṛtāḥ /
	niryātayan manovāgbhiḥ śīghraṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (2317)

ity āha bhagavān āryāvalokiteśvaraḥ // (2318)

tatredaṃ maṇikulapūjāsiddhitntram // :

	chatradhvajapatākābhiḥ rājapūjābhir arcayan /
	sidhyate maṇikulaṃ sarvaṃ dadan dānāni sidhyati // (2319)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // (2320)

	svādhiṣṭhānādiyukto vajrasattvasamo bhavet /
	caturbhiḥ prātihāryais tu vajraviśvaṃ sa sādhayet //
	sarvasiddhayaḥ (2321)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2322)

sarvakulādhiṣṭhānābhiṣekasamādhipūjāsiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2323)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatābhijñājñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2324)

tatredaṃ tathāgatābhijñājñānasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	kāye buddhasamādhis tu svabhijñā saugatī tv iyam /
	tasyāḥ suprativedhatvād bauddhīṃ siddhim svāpnuyāt // iti (2325)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulābhijñājñānasiddhitantram //:

	divyacakṣvādayo 'bhijñā bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā vajrasattvatvam āpnuyāt // (2326)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2327)

tatredaṃ vajrakulābhijñājñānasiddhitantram //:

	krodhābhijñāṃ samutpādya sādhayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā parāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // iti (2328)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2329)

tatredaṃ padmakulābhijñājñānasiddhitantram //:

	rāgābhijñāṃ samutpādya bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā śuddhāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (2330)

ity āha bhagavān vajranetraḥ // (2331)

tatredaṃ maṇikulābhijñānasiddhitantram //:

	pūjābhijñāṃ samutpādya bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	pañcābhijñaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā sarvasiddhir varā bhavet // (2332)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2333)

sarvakulābhijñājñānasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2334)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamahābodhijñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2335)

tatredaṃ tathāgatamahābodhijñānasiddhitatram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhistho buddhānusmṛtimān svayam /
	buddhabodhir iyaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2336)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2337)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulamahābodhijñānasiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhistho mahāmudrāṃ tu bhāvayan /
	mahābodhir iyaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2338)

ity āha bhagavān mahābodhisattvaḥ // (2339)

tatredaṃ vajrakulamahābodhijñānasiddhitantram //

	krodharājasamādhisthaḥ samayāgryākaragrahaḥ /
	mahābodhir iyaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2340)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2341)

tatredaṃ padmakulamahābodhijñānasiddhitantram //:

	lokeśvarasamādhistho dharmamudrāṃ japaṃs tathā /
	mahābodhir iyaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2342)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2343)

tatredaṃ maṇikulamahābodhijñānasiddhitantram //

	vajragarbhasamādhisthaḥ karmamudrāsukarmakṛt /
	mahābodhir iyaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2344)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2345)

sarvakulamahābodhijñānasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2346)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatānurāgaṇasiddhitantram udājahāra // : (2347)

tatredaṃ tathāgatānurāgaṇasiddhitantram //:

	sattvārthaṃ ca prakurvan vai buddhabodhyarthikaḥ svayam /
	buddhānusmṛtimān bhūtvā sarvabuddhānurāgaṇām // (2348)

ity āha vajrarāgaḥ // (2349)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulānurāgaṇasiddhitantram //

	yathāviṣaya yāṃ(-vān?) bhūtvā vajrasattvaṃ tu sādhayet /
	tattvacodanayā śīghram anuraktaḥ sa siddhyati // (2350)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2351)

tatredaṃ vajrakulānurāgaṇasiddhitantram //

	buddhājñākāritārthaṃ hi duṣṭānām abhicārukaiḥ /
	krodhāt sattvaviśuddhyartham idaṃ vajrānurāgaṇam // (2352)

ity āha bhagavāṃs trilokavijayaḥ // (2353)

tatredaṃ padmakulānurāgaṇasiddhitantram //:

	rāgāvalokanaṃ maitrī kāruṇyaṃ dharmavāditā /
	sarvābhayapradānaṃ ca sarvabuddhānurāgaṇam // (2354)

ity āha bhagavān vajranetraḥ // (2355)

tatredaṃ maṇikulānurāgaṇasiddhitantram //:

	abhiṣekapradānaṃ ca pradānaṃ dhanasaṃcayam /
	tac ca buddhārthato yojyam idaṃ buddhānurāgaṇam // (2356)

ity āha bhagavān āryākāśagarbhaḥ // (2657)

sarvakulānurāgaṇasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2358)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2359)

tatredaṃ tathāgatavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram //:

	rāgo vai nāvamantavyo viśuddhaḥ sukahdas tathā /
	sarvasattvārthato yoga idaṃ buddhavaśaṃkaram // (2360)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2361)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram //:

	kāmaṃ sevya sukhātmā tu suratas tvam iti bruvan /
	sādhayed vajrasattvaṃ tu tattvacodavaśīkṛtam // (2362)

ity āha bhagavān samantabhadraḥ // (2363)

tatredaṃ vajrakulavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram //

	buddhājñāt sattvaśuddhyartham abhayārthaṃ ca dehinām /
	buddhaśāsanarakṣārthaṃ mārayan vaśam ānayet // (2364)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2365)

tatredaṃ padmakulavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram //:

	rāgaśuddhiṃ parīkṣan vai padmapattravikāsataḥ /
	rañjed vā rāgayec caiva vinayārthaṃ vaśaṃkaram // (2366)

ity āha bhagavān āryāvalokiteśvaraḥ // (2367)

tatredaṃ maṇikulavaśīkaraṇasiddhitantram //:

	sarvabuddhābhiṣekārthaṃ vajraratnaṃ dine dine /
	śīrṣe sthāpyābhiṣicyatāṃ sarvabuddhān vaśaṃ nyaset // (2368)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2369)

sarvakulavaśīkaraṇasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2370)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamāraṇasiddhitantam udājahāra // (2371)

tatredaṃ tathāgatamāraṇasiddhitantram //

	aspaśyan sarvasattvārthaṃ buddhatattvān aśodhayan /
	manasā kāyavāgbhyāṃ vā marayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2372)

ity āha bhagavāṃs tathāgataḥ // (2373)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulamāraṇasiddhitantram //:

	alābhāt sarvasiddhīnām anudyogāt kulasya ca /
	āsphoṭanena vajrasya mārayan laghu sidhyate // (2374)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2375)

tatredaṃ vajrakulamāraṇasiddhitantram //:

	aduṣṭadamanāt krodhād asattvavinayāt tathā /
	ātmano duḥkhadānāc ca hūṃkāreṇa tu mārayet // iti (2376)

((ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ //)) ((ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ //)) (2377)

tatredaṃ padmakulamāraṇasiddhitantram //:

	akāruṇyād amaitryās tu duḥsattvānām aśodhanāt /
	ātmanaś ca visaṃvādān mārayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2378)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2379)

tatredaṃ maṇikulamāraṇasiddhitantram //:

	atyāgād ātmano 'narthāt arthahārād anarthataḥ /
	dāridryāc caiva sattvānāṃ mārayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2380)

ity āha bhagavān sarvāśāparipūrakaḥ // (2381)

	kecid aprāptiyogena buddhānāṃ māraṇātmakāḥ /
	teṣām uddharaṇārthāya laghu siddhipradā vayam // (2382)

ity āha bhagavān āryasamantabhadraḥ // (2383)

sarvakulamāraṇasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2384)


atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatarakṣāmudrāsiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2385)

tatredaṃ tathāgatarakṣāsiddhitantram //:

	sarvasattvāparityāgo buddhapūjātmatā sadā /
	nityaṃ buddhamanaskārī rakṣeyaṃ paramādbhūtā // (2386)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2387)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakularakṣāsiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattve sakṛdvārāṃ nāmamātraparigrahaḥ /
	iyaṃ rakṣā tu mahatī śāśvatī siddhidā kṣaṇāt // (2388)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2389)

tatredaṃ vajrakularakṣāsiddhitantram //:

	vidyātantreṣu saṃtoṣas trilokavijayātmatā /
	bhakir vai vajrahūṃkāre rakṣeyaṃ svaparasya vā // (2390)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2391)

tatredaṃ padmakularakṣāsiddhitantram //:

	rāgaśuddhir mahāmaitrī sattveṣv abhayadānatā /
	lokeśvaranāmajāpaś ca rakṣeyaṃ paramādbhūtā // (2392)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2393)

tatredaṃ maṇikularakṣāsiddhitantram //:

	avandhyo di.vaśaḥ kāryo yathāśaktyā prayogataḥ /
	tyāgena buddhasattvābhyāṃ rakṣeyaṃ paramādbhūtā // (2394)

ity āha bhagavān vajrarakṣaḥ // (2395)

sarvakularakṣāsiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2396)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvo bhagavantam etad avocat /:

	pratigṛhāṇa, bhagavann, idaṃ sarvatathāgatakulatantraṃ,
	yena sarvasattvāḥ sarvakalpaiśvaryatayādhigamaṃ kṛtvā,
	śīghram anuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbotsyante.

iti // (2397)

atha bhagavān vajrapāṇaye bodhisattvāya mahāsattvāya sādhukāram adāt //: (2398)

	sādhu sādhuvajrapāṇe subhāṣitaṃ, parigṛhīto 'smābhir adhiṣṭhitaś ca // iti (2399)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya, vajrapāṇaye mahābodhisattvāya sādhukārāṇy adadan /: (2400)

	sādhu te vajradattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /
	vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhute vajrakrmaṇe // (2401)

	subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /
	sarvatāthāgataguhyaṃ mahāyābhisaṃgraham // iti // (2402)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvakalpopāyasiddhividhivistaratantraṃ parisamāptam // // (2403)



sarvakulakalpaguhyavidhivistaratantram (2404)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgataguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2405)

tatrādita eva tathāgatottamasiddhiguhyatantram //

	buddhabodhisamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	sukhena labhyate bodhir iti cintyāvabudhyati // (2406)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataḥ // (2407)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulottamasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	sattvavajrāṃ hṛdi baddhvā bhāryā me tvam atipriyā /
	dṛḍhībhava iti prokte sarvamudrās tu sādhayet // (2408)

	anena vidhiyogena asiddhiā'pi svakarmabhiḥ /
	guhyabhāryam iti prokte sutarāṃ siddhim āpnuyāt // (2409)

ity āha bhagavān sattvavajraḥ // (2410)

tatredaṃ vajrakulottamasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	yathā tathā hi kupito vajrahūṃkāramudrayā /
	mārayan sarvabuddhāṃs tu bhayāt siddhiṃ dadanti hi // (2411)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatahūṃkāraḥ // (2412)

tatredaṃ padmakulottamasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	samādhimudrāṃ samādhāya nirīkṣan vajradṛṣṭinā /
	svadāraṃ paradāraṃ vā priyāṃ siddhim avāpnute // (2413)

ity āha bhagavān padmarāgaḥ // (2414)

tatredaṃ maṇikulottamasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā sukham agram iti bruvan /
	svendriyaṃ sarvabuddhānāṃ niryātya laghu sidhyati // (2415)

ity āha bhagavān maṇirāgaḥ // (2416)

sarvakulottamasiddhiguhyatantram // // (2417)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayasiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2418)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	samayas tvam iti proktvā rāgayet sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	mā virāgaya sattvārthaṃ bruvan buddhān sa rāgayet // (2419)

ity āha bhagavān mahāvairocanaḥ // (2420)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasamayasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	rāgo hi nāvamantavyo rāmayet sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	vajriṇo guhyasamayam idaṃ rakṣaṃs tu sidhyati // (2421)

ity āha bhagavān vairocanaḥ // (2422)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamayasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	mārayan mārayel lokaṃ kāyavākkarmasatkriyaiḥ /
	hūṃkārais tu viśuddhyarthaṃ samayo hy arthasiddhidaḥ // iti (2423)

ity āha bahgavāṃs trilokavijayaḥ // (2424)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamayasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	rāgaḥ śuddhātmanāṃ śuddho hy aśuddhas tīrthyayoginām /
	śuddhātmanāṃ tu samayaṃ pālayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2425)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2426)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamayasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	baddhvā vajramaṇiṃ pūrvaṃ vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	duṣṭānāṃ tu harann arthān samayaḥ siddhido bhavati // (2427)

ity āha bhagavān vajraratnaḥ // (2428)

sarvakulasamayasiddhiguhyavidhivistaratantram // // (2429)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmasiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2430)

tatredaṃ tathāgatadharmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	svabhāvaśuddhiṃ dharmāṇāṃ bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	sarvakāryāṇi kurvan vai bauddhīṃ siddhim avāpnute // (2431)

ity āha bhagavān vajradhātuḥ // (2432)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	sarvasattvānurāgaś ca viṣayeṣv avirāgitā /
	rāmārāgaṇaśuddhis tu guhyadharmaḥ susiddhidaḥ // (2433)

ity āha bhagavān vajraguhyaḥ // (2434)

tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmasiddhiguhyatantram //

	nāsāhūṃkārayogena sarvaduṣṭāṃs tu mārayan /
	sūkṣmavajrasamādhisthaḥ parāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (2435)

ity āha bhagavān dharmahūṃkāraḥ // (2436)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa rāmayet sarvayoṣitaḥ /
	dharmasiddhim avāpnoti vajradharmsamādhinā // iti (2437)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2438)

tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	dvayendriyasamāpattyā sarvāśāḥ paripūrayan /
	yoṣitāṃ vā priyāṇāṃ vā siddhim āpnoty anuttarām iti // (2439)

ity āha bhagavān vajraratnaḥ // (2440)

sarvakuladharmasiddhiguhyavidhivistaratantram // // (2441)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmasiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2442)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmasiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhistho buddhānusmṛtibhāvakaḥ /
	strīkāryaṃ praviśan yonyā vaśīkuryāt tu yoṣitaḥ // (2443)

ity āha bhagavān vairocanaḥ // (2444)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulakarmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhistho bhagena praviśaṃs tathā /
	striyāḥ kāye spharet samayaṅ niśceṣṭām api rāgayet // (2445)

ity āha bhagavān vajrarāgaḥ // (2446)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakarmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	vajrahūṃkāramudrāṃ vai baddhvā tu susamāhitaḥ /
	praviśaṃs tu bhage kruddhaḥ manasā sa tu pātayet // (2447)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasamayaḥ // (2448)

tatredaṃ padmakulakarmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	dharmakarmamayī mudrāṃ baddhvā padmasamādhinā /
	bhagena praviśan rakṣed api sarvās tu yoṣitaḥ // (2449)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapadmaḥ // (2450)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	karmavajramaṇiṃ baddhvā vajraratnasamādhinā /
	bhagena praviśan strīṇām kṣaṇād āviśya natrtati // (2451)

ity āha bahgavān vajraratnaḥ // (2452)

sarvakulakarmasiddhiguhyavidhivistaratantram // // (2453)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamaṇḍalaśuddhisiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2454)

tatredaṃ tathāgatacakraśuddhisiddhiguhyatantraṃ bhavati //:

	dharmacakrasamākāraṃ kuryād vā guhyamaṇḍalam /
	mudrābhāryāparivṛtaṃ tatra buddhaṃ ni.veśayet // (2455)

	praviṣṭvaiva hi tad guhyaṃ brūyād buddhasya tatkṣaṇāt /
	bhāryā hy etās tava vibho dadasva mama sarvada // (2456)

	evaṃ brvaṃs tu sarveṣu kulamudrānayeṣu ca /
	guhyasiddhim avāpnoti buddhānām asamatviṣām // (2457)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2458)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasarvamaṇḍalasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	vajradhātupratīkāśaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tu samālikhet /
	tathāgatakulānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ paramaṃ nayam // (2459)

	siddhikāmas tvaran brūyāt praviṣṭvā karmamaṇḍalam /
	surate samayas tvaṃ hoḥ vajrasattvādya siddhyayām // (2460)

	idaṃ japaṃs tu hṛdayaṃ sādhayet sarvasiddhayaḥ /
	tattvacodanayogena tuṣṭaḥ sann āśu sidhyati // (2461)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2462)


tetredaṃ vajrakulasarvamaṇḍalaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	trilokavijayākāraṃ sarvavajrakulasya hi /
	sarvamaṇḍalayogaṃ tu saṃlikheta vicakṣaṇaḥ // (2463)

	taṃ praviṣṭvaiva śīghraṃ hi brūyāt siddhiṃ tu yācayan /
	rāgāt tvam asi saṃbhūta evaṃ sarveṣu sidhyati // (2464)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2465)

tatredaṃ padmakulamaṇḍalaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	jagadvinayayogena sarvapadmakuleṣu vai /
	maṇḍalāni likhet prājñas taṃ praviṣṭvaiva vāg vadet // (2466)

	rāgadharmamahāpadma prasidhya laghu me vibho /
	evam uktvā tu sarveṣu maṇḍaleṣu sa sidhyati // (2467)

ity āha bhagvān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2468)

tatredaṃ maṇikulamaṇḍalaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	sarvārthasiddhiyogena maṇḍalāni samālikhet /
	mahāmaṇiklānāṃ tu taṃ pratiṣṭvaiva vāg vadet // (2469)

	sarvābhiprāyasiddhīnāṃ rāgāśāsiddhir uttamā /
	sidhya sidhya mahāsattva bhagavan sarvasiddhaye // (2470)

	evaṃ brvaṃs tu sarveṣu maṇḍaleṣu praveṣataḥ /
	mahāsiddhim avāpnoti pūjāguhya anuttaram // (2471)

	tataḥ prabhoṛti siddhātmā sādhayan siddhayaḥ sadā /
	yadā na laghu siddhiḥ syāt sidhyate tattvacodanaiḥ // (2472)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2473)

sarvakulamaṇḍalaguhyasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2474)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatahāgatasarvamudrāguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2475)

tatredaṃ tathāgatamudraguhyasiddhitantram //:

	tathāgatamahādevyaḥ priyāḥ sarvasukhapradāḥ /
	satyānuparivartinyā vāksatyaiḥ śāpitā yan na sidhyate //
	[satyānuvarivāksatyaiḥ sādhintā yan na sidhyate //] (2476)

ity āha buddho bhagavān // (2477)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulamahāmudrāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	mahāmudrāṃ tu vai baddhvā yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ /
	idaṃ tattvaṃ rahasyaṃ ca vajravācā vaden nayam // (2478)

	vajrasattvaḥ svayam ahaṃ tvaṃ me bhāryā hṛdi sthitā /
	sarvaṃ kāyaṃ pariṣvajya vajragarve samutkṣipa // (2479)

	vajragarvā mahādevī tattvacodānurāgitā /
	sarvakāye dṛḍhībhūtvā yathāvat sidhyate laghuḥ // (2480)

ity āha bahgavān vajragarvāpatiḥ // (2481)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamayamudrāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	sidhya sidhyādya samaye samayo 'haṃ tvaṃ priyā mama /
	iti codanayā śīghram anuraktā prasidhyati // (2482)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasamayaḥ // (2483)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmamudrāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	budhya budhya mahāsattvi bhāryā me tvam atipriyā /
	iti codanayā śīghram anuraktā tu sidhyati // (2484)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2485)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmamudrāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	sarvakarmakarī bhāryā tvaṃ me sidhyādya vajriṇi /
	iti codanayā śīghram anuraktā tu sidhyati // (2486)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2487)

sarvakulasarvamudrāguhyasiddhividhivistaratantram // /// (2488)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasamayaguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2489)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	tīrthikānāṃ hitārthāya buddhabhāryā pragopitā /
	lekhyā mudrāprayogeṇa iti vijñāya sidhyati // (2490)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamayaḥ // (2491)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	sarvasattvamanovyāpi sarvasattvasukhapradaḥ /
	sarvasattvapitā caiva kāmo 'gra[ḥ] samayāgriṇām // (2492)

ity āhur bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ // (2493)

	idaṃ tat sarvabuddhānāṃ rahasyaṃ paramādbhutam /
	vijñāya śraddadhac chrāddho duḥsādhyo 'pi hi sidhyati // (2495)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //

	rāgaśuddhyai viraktānāṃ tīrthyadṛṣṭikṛtātmanām /
	māraṇaṃ samayaṃ tv agram idaṃ vijñāya sidhyati // (2496)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2497)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	mahābhūtoḍbhavaṃ sarvaṃ kathaṃ tv aśucir udyate /
	tīrthikānāṃ vināśāya dhruvaṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (2499)

ity āha bhagavān vajranetraḥ // (2499)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //

	strīprasaṅgāt tu ratnānāṃ saṃcayaḥ kriyate yadā /
	striyo hy anuttaraṃ ratnam iti cintya sa sidhyati // (2500)

ity āha bhagavān ājñākaraḥ // (2501)

sarvakulasamayaguhyasiddhividhivisataratantram // // (2502)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatapūjāguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2503)

tatredaṃ tathāgatapūjāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	strībhiḥ parivṛto bhūtvā parihāsakriyāsukham /
	niryātya buddhapūjāyāṃ pūjāsiddhim avāpnuyāt // (2504)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2505)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulapūjāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	surataśramakhinnas tu tat saukhyaṃ suratodbhavam /
	catuḥpraṇāmapūjāyāṃ niryātya laghu sidhyati // (2506)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2507)

tatredaṃ vajrakulapūjāguhyasiddhitantram //:

	hūṃkārasamayāṃ baddhvā pariṣvajya striyaṃ janam /
	tat pariṣvaṅgasaukhyaṃ tu niryātya hi sa sidhyati // (2508)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2509)

tatredaṃ padmakulapūjāsiddhiguhyatantram //:

	lokeśvaram ahaṃ bhāvya priyāvaktraṃ nirīkṣan vai /
	tan nirīkṣaṇasaukhyaṃ tu niryātya hi sa sidhyati // (2510)

ity āha bhagavān padmanetraḥ // (2511)

tatredaṃ maṇikulapūjāsiddhiguhyatantram //:

	karmamudrādharo bhūtvā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ /
	striyaṃ pariṣvajya pūjāyāṃ vibhūṣitaṃ niryātya sidhyati //(2512)

ity āha bhagavān vajraratnaḥ // (2513)

sarvakulapūjāsiddhiguhyavidhivistaratantram // // (2514)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgataguhyapūjāsiddhitantram udajahāra // (2515)

tatredaṃ tathāgataguhyasiddhipūjāsiddhitantram //:

	ramayan paradārāṇi yathākaś cin na vedayet /
	bhāvayan buddham ātmānaṃ pūjayā siddhim āpnuyāt // (2516)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2517)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulaguhyapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	vajralāsyāṃ samādhāya vajramālāṃ tu bandhayet /
	vajragītāṃ tato baddhvā pūjayed vajranṛtyayā // (2518)

	kāmaratyābhiṣekagryā nṛtyagītasukhāt sukham /
	nānyad asti hi teneyaṃ guhyapūjā niruttarā // (2519)

tatredaṃ vajrakulaguhyapūjāsiddhitantram // :

	yathāvad vidhiyogena pūjayan guhyapūjayā /
	trilokavijayaṃ bhāvya pūjāsiddhim avāpnuyāt // (2520)

ity āha bhagavān vajraguhyaḥ // (2521)

tatredaṃ padmakulaguhyapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	yathāvad guhyayogena karmamudrāsu pūjayan /
	jagadvinayamudrāsthaḥ pūjāsiddhim avāpnute // (2522)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2523)

tatreda. maṇikulaguhyapūjāsiddhitantram //:

	yathāvad guhyayogena karmamudrāsu sādhayet /
	sarvārthasiddhiyogena pūjāsiddhim avāpnute // (2524)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // // (2525)

sarvakulaguhyapūjāsiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2526)


atha bhagavān vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakulodghāṭanaguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra // (2527)

tatredaṃ tathāgatatattvotpattisiddhiguhyatantram //:

	samādhijñānasaṃbhūtaṃ buddhatvaṃ hi samāsataḥ /
	sattvarāgaṇayogena śīghram āpnoty anuttaram // (2528)

ity āha bhagavāṃs tathāgataḥ // (2529)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulamahātattvodghāṭanasiddhiguhyatantram //

	anādinidhanaḥ sattva ākāśotpattilakṣaṇaḥ /
	samantabhadraḥ sarvātmā kāmaḥ sarvajagatpatiḥ // (2530)

	yac cittaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ dṛḍhatvāt sattva ucyate /
	samādhānād vajrasamo niścayair yāti vajratām // (2531)

	sattvādhiṣṭhānayogena vajrasattvaḥ punar bhavet /
	sa eva bhagavān sattvo vajrakāmas tathāgataḥ // (2532)

	svacittaprativedhādibuddhabodhir yathāvidhiḥ /
	sa eva bhagavān sarvatathāgatakulaṃ bhavet // (2533)

ity āha bhagavān anādinidhanasattvaḥ // (2534)

	tathāgatakulaṃ saiva saiva vajrakulaṃ smṛtam /
	saiva padmakulaṃ śuddhaṃ saivoktaṃ maṇisatkulam // (2535)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatacakraḥ // (2536)

sarvakulotpādanaguhyasiddhividhivistaratantram // (2537)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamudrābhidhānasiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2538)

tatredaṃ tathāgatacihnābhidhānasiddhiguhyatantraṃ bhavati //:

	sa eva bhagavān sattvo vajrasattvo hṛdi sthitaḥ /
	samādhānāt samādhis tu buddhabodhiprasādhakaḥ // (2539)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2540)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulacihnābhidhānasiddhiguhyatantram //:

	vajraṃ suprativedhatvād aṅkuśaṃ grahamocakaḥ /
	sūkṣmavedhitayā vāṇaṃ sādhakakāras tu tuṣṭitaḥ // (2541)

	ratnas tu racanād uktaḥ sūryas tejovidhānataḥ /
	ketuḥ samucchrayaḥ proktaḥ smito hāsas tu kīrtitaḥ // (2542)

	rāgaśuddhitayā padmaṃ kośaḥ kleśāricchedanāt /
	cakro maṇḍalayogāt tu vāglāpāj japa ucyate // (2543)

	sarvavajraṃ tu viśvatvād varmadurbhedyayogataḥ /
	daṃṣṭrā bhīṣaṇayogāt tu bandho mudrāprayogataḥ // (2544)

	yathā hi bhagavān śaśvan vajrasattvas tu sarvagaḥ /
	tathā vajraṃ tu cihnādi bhāvayann iti sidhyati // (2545)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatacihnaḥ // (2546)

sarvakulacihnābhidhānasiddhiguhyatantram // // (2547)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram udājahāra //: (2548)

tatredaṃ tathāgatamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram //

	baddhvā vai vajraparyaṅkaṃ karābhyāṃ vajrabandhataḥ /
	vajrasattvasamādhisthaḥ śīghraṃ buddhatvam āpnuyāt // (2549)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2550)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram //:

	yathārājñāṃ svamudrābhir mudryate rājaśāsanam /
	mahātmanāṃ svamudrābhir āmudryante tathā janāḥ // (2551)

	kāyavākcittavajrāṇāṃ pratibimbaprayogataḥ /
	mahātmanāṃ mahāmudrā iti vijñāya sidhyati // (2552)

ity āha bhagavān mudraḥ // (2553)

tatredaṃ vajrakulamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram //:

	yathā hi samayais tīvraiḥ kaś cid bandho bhavej janaḥ /
	anatikramaṇīyais tu tathā sarvatathāgatāḥ // (2554)

	baddhā hi vajrabandhāgryamudrāsamayabandhanaiḥ /
	nātikramanty ā maraṇād iti vijñāya sidhyati // (2555)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasamayaḥ // (2556)

tatredaṃ dharmakulamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram // :

	anatikramaṇīyā hi vajravāksarvaśo jinaiḥ /
	ayaṃ bandha iti jñātvā dharmam asya prasidhyati // (2557)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2558)

tatredaṃ karmakulamudrābandhotpattisiddhiguhyatantram //

	anatikramaṇīyā hi vajrājñā karma bhūri ca /
	ājñāvatas tu tat karma vijñāya laghusidhyati // (2559)

ity āha bhagavān vajraḥ // (2560)

sarvakulamudrābandhotpattisiddhividhivistaraguhyatantram // // (2561)


atha khalu bhagavān vajrapāṇiṃ mahābodhisattvam evam āha //:

	idam api mayā bhagavan parigṛhītam adhiṣṭhitaṃ ceti // (2562)

atha sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya, vajrapāṇaye sarvatathāgatādhipataye sādhukārāṇy adaduḥ // (2563)

	sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /
	vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhute vajrakarmaṇe // (2564)

	subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /
	sarvatathāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham // iti // (2565)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvakulakalpaguhyavidhivistaratantraṃ samāptam // // (2566)


(sarvakalpaguhyottaratantravidhivistaraḥ) (2567)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2568)

tatredaṃ tathāgatadharmottamasiddhitantram //:

	buddhadharmasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	buddhānusmṛtiyogena siddhim āpnoti hy uttamām // (2569)

ity āha bhagavāṃs tathāgataḥ // (2570)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmottamasiddhitantram //:

	sarvasattvasamādhistho bhāvayan susamāhitaḥ /
	rāgānusmṛtiyogena prāpnuyāt siddhim uttamām // (2571)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamādhiḥ // (2572)

tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmottamasiddhitantram //:

	trilokavijayākāraṃ bhāvayan puratas tathā /
	vajrapāṇibalo bhūtvā trilokavijayī bhavet // (2573)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2574)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmottamasiddhitantram //:

	jagadvinayadharmaṃ tu bhāvayan puratas tathā /
	sarvākāravaropetaṃ vinayaṃ prakaroti saḥ //  (2575)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2576)

tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmottamasiddhitantram //:

	sarvārthasiddhirūpaṃ tu bhāvayan puratas tathā /
	sarvākāravaropetaṃ sarvasaṃpat sa lapsyate // (2577)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2578)

sarvakuladharmottamasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2579)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatadharmasamayasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2580)

tatredaṃ tathāgatadharmasamayasiddhitantram //:

	buddhānusmṛtimān bhūtvā vajra vajra iti bruvan /
	sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa buddhasiddhim avāpnute // (2581)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2582)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakuladharmasamayasiddhitantram //

	vajrasattvasamādhiṃ tu bhāvayan sūkṣmavajrataḥ /
	vajrasattvatvam āpnoti vajrasattvam udāharan // (2583)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2584)

tatredaṃ vajrakuladharmasamayasiddhitantram //:

	trilokavijayākāraṃ saṃsmaran puratas tathā /
	hūṃ hūṃ hūṃ hūm iti procya siddhim āpnoty anuttarām // (2585)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2586)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmasamayasiddhitantram // :

	jagadvinayarūpaṃ tu bhāvayan sūkṣmavajrataḥ /
	śudhya śudhya iti procya hy uttamāṃ siddhim āpnuyāt // (2587)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharmaḥ // (2588)

tatredaṃ maṇikuladharmasamayasiddhitantram //:

	sarvārthasiddhirūpaṃ tu bhāvayan sūkṣmavajrataḥ /
	sidhya sidhya iti procya hy arthasiddhiḥ parā bhavet // (2589)

ity āha bhagavān maṇidharmaḥ // (2590)

sarvakuladharmasamayasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2591)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2592)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram //

	anuakṣaraṃ tu saddharmaṃ samādhijñānasaṃbhavam /
	akāras tena dharmāṇām anutpāda iti smṛtaḥ // (2593)

	anena mudrāprayogeṇa bhāvayan prajñayā tataḥ /
	sarvākṣaramayaṃ jñānaṃ sidhyate saugataṃ kṣaṇāt // (2594)

ity āha bhagavān āryamañjuśrīsarvatathāgataḥ // (2595)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram //

	sarvatāthāgataṃ tattvam idaṃ sūtraṃ tu śaraddadhan /
	dhārayan vācyan siddhim āpnoty anuttarām // (2596)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2597)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram //:

	pāpasattvahitārthāya buddhājñākaraṇāya ca /
	duṣṭānāṃ vinayārthāya māraṇena tu sidhyati // (2598)

ity āha bhagavān vajrakulaḥ // (2599)

tatredaṃ padmakulasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram //:

	svabhāvaśuddhim āgamya paramārtham iti smṛtam /
	bhāvayann idam ādyaṃ tu dharmeṇāśu prasidhyati // (2600)

ity āha bhagavān avalokteśvaraḥ // (2601)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasaddharmajñānasiddhitantram //:

	sarvasattvārthadānaṃ ca sarvāśāparipūraye /
	imaṃ maṇikule dharmaṃ bhāvayann āśu sidhyati // (2602)

ity āha bhagavān dharmaratnaḥ // (2603)

sarvakuladharmajñānasiddhividhivistaratantram //  // (2604)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasamādhikarmasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2605)

tatredaṃ tathāgatasamādhikarmasiddhitantram //:

	samādhikarma buddhānāṃ buddhabodhiprasādhakam /
	idaṃ bhāvayamānas tu parāṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // iti (2606)

ity āha bhagavān vajradhātuḥ (Tib) //
ity āha bhagavān Buddhaḥ (Ch.) // (2607)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasamādhikarmasiddhitantram //:

	vajrasattvasamādhīnām uttamaṃ karma bhūri ca /
	sarvasattvakaraṃ viśvam iti bhāvena sidhyati // (2608)

ity āha bhagavān vajraḥ // (2609)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasamādhikarmasiddhitantram //:

	pāpaśuddhinimittaṃ hi sarvapāpapradāmakam /
	māraṇaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ śraddadhānāṃ tu sidhyati // (2610)

ity āha bhagavān vajrī // (2611)

tatredaṃ padmakulasamādhikarmasiddhitantram //:

	sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sarvaśuddhyā karoti saḥ /
	sarvakāryāṇi karmo 'yam iti bhāvena sidhyati // (2612)

ity āha bhagavān padmaḥ // (2613)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasamādhikarmasiddhitantram //

	sarvāśināṃ daridrāṇāṃ sarvāśāḥ paripūrayan /
	sarvārthasiddhiḥ sarvātmā sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ // (2614)

ity āha bhagavān ratnadhvajaḥ // (2615)

sarvakulasamādhikarmasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2616)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //  (2617)

tatredaṃ sūkṣmajñānasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	sūkṣmavajravidhiṃ śaśvad yojayan sarvabhāvataḥ /
	sarvākāravaropetāṃ pañcābhij.ām avāpnyāt // (2618)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2619)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram //

	nāncāryasya nānyasya nāśiṣyasyāsutasya vā /
	purataḥ prakāśayen mudrāḥ siddhir āsāṃ suguhyataḥ // (2620)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2621)

tatredaṃ vajrakulasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram //:

	sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa nāsāhūṃkārayogataḥ /
	vajrakrodhasamādhisthaḥ sarvakāryāṇi sādhayet // (2622)

ity āha bhagavān vajraḥ // (2623)

tatredaṃ padmakulasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram //

	vajradṛṣṭiṃ samādhāya sūkṣmavajraprayogataḥ /
	mahāpadmasamādhistho rāgaisddhim avāpnuyāt // (2625)

ity āha bhagavān padmarāgaḥ // (2625)

tatredaṃ maṇikulasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram //:

	dīptadṛṣṭiḥ susūkṣmā tu vajraratnasamādhinā /
	sūkṣmavajraprayogageṇa sarvārthākarṣaṇo bhavet // (2626)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2627)

sarvakulasūkṣmajñānasiddhitantram // (2628)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatahāgatacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2629)

tatredaṃ tathāgatacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram //:

	yadā mudrā samādhir vā sādhanāyopayujyate /
	tadā khe dhāvataḥ śubhās tatrākārāḥ sa paśyati // (2630)

	tadā jānīta matimān buddhacakṣur idaṃ mama /
	tataḥ prabhṛti buddhānāṃ sarvakalpāni sādhayet // (2631)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2632)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram //:

	yāvanto bhāvā vidyante sthāvarā jaṅgamās tathā /
	teṣāṃ ca pratibimbāni paśyati khe pradhāvataḥ // (2633)

	āgacchan gacchato vāpi vajracakṣurviśuddhitām /
	jānan vai pūjayā sddhim āpnoty anuttarām // (2634)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2635)

tatredaṃ vajrakulacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram //:

	savyāpasavyavartinyaḥ khe tāḥ paśyati cakṣuṣā /
	ākāśadhātavaḥ śīghraṃ bhramanto hy abhrasaṃnibhāḥ // (2636)

	tān dṛṣṭvā na hi bidhyeta mudrās tā vajrasaṃbhavāḥ /
	tāsāṃ grahaṇato mudrāḥ sidhyante mudracakṣuṣaḥ // (2637)

ity āha bhagavān vajraḥ // (2638)

tatredaṃ padmakulacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram //:

	śvetān raktān sitān pītān yadā paśyanti maṇḍalān /
	tadā saṃcintyatāṃ yānti sidhyante vajracakṣuṣaḥ // (2639)

((ity āha bhagavān vajrapadmaḥ //
ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ //)) (2640)

tatredaṃ maṇikulacakṣurjñānasiddhitantram //:

	ākāśe ratnasaṃkāśā hiraṇyādiṣu sādṛśaḥ /
	yadā tu paśyate khe tu khacakṣuḥ sidhyate sadā // (2641)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // (2642)

sarvakulacakṣurjñānasiddhividhivistaratantram // //


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2644)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmottamasiddhitantram //:

	karmamaṇḍalayogena pūjayan sarvanāyakān /
	rāgasaukhyavipākārthaṃ buddhasiddhim avāpnyāt // (2645)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2646)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmottamasiddhitantram //:

	guhyapūjāṃ prakurvāṇo rāgo 'ham iti bhāvayan /
	prāpnuyād uttamāṃ siddhiṃ vajrarāgasamadyutim // (2647)

ity āha bhagavān kāmaḥ // (2648)

tatredaṃ vajrakarmottamasiddhitantram //:

	guhyapūjāṃ prakurvānaḥ krodho 'ham iti bhāvayan /
	prāpnuyād uttamāṃ siddhiṃ trilokavijayottamām // (2649)

((ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // )) (2650)


tatredaṃ padakulakarmottamasiddhitantram //:

	antargatena manasā kāmaśuddhiṃ tu bhāvayan /
	svaretobindubhir buddhān pūjayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2651)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2652)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmottamasiddhitantram //:

	vajragarvāṃ samādhāya named āśayakampitaiḥ /
	praṇāmaparamo nityam abhiṣekāṃ samāpnyāt // (2653)

ity āha bhagavān vajrābhiṣekaratnaḥ // (2654)

sarvakulakarmottamasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2655)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2656)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	kāmādyāḥ sarvasaukhyā me sadaiva hṛdaye sthitāḥ /
	aho sattvārthatā nāma virāgo yatra deśayate // (2657)

	ayaṃ hi karmasamayas tathāgatasamādhinā /
	bhāvayan pūjayed buddhān uttamāṃ siddhim āpnuyāt // (2658)

ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2659)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	samantabhadrakāmo 'haṃ sarvasattvasukhapradaḥ /
	vajrasattvasamādhisthaḥ pūjayan siddhim āpnyāt // (2660)

ity āha bhagavān kāmaḥ // (2661)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	samantabhadrakrodho 'haṃ sarvasattvahitaṃ karaḥ /
	vajrahūṃkārayogena pūjayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2662)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2663)


tatredaṃ padmakulakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //:

	samantabhadrarāgo 'haṃ sarvasaukhyapradaḥ svayam /
	jagadvinayarūpasthaḥ pūjayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2664)

ity āha bhagavān padmarāgaḥ // (2665)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmasamayaguhyasiddhitantram //

	samantabhadro rājāhaṃ sarvasattvamahārthadaḥ /
	sarvārthasiddhirūpeṇa pūjayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2666)

ity āha bhagavān sarvārthasiddhiḥ // (2667)

sarvakulakarmasamayaguhyasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2668)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2669)

vajra(?) tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram //:

	dakṣiṇāgryābhimukhataḥ kavacan svasamādhinā /
	nibadhyoṣṇīṣasaṃsthā tu rakṣātyantaṃ bhaviṣyati // (2670)

iti āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (2671)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram //:

	saṃlikhya tu bhagākāraṃ kuḍye meḍhraṃ samutthitam /
	yāṃ striyaṃ cintayed vṛddhaṃ kuryāt sāsya vaśībhavet // (2672)

ity āha bhagavān āryavajrapāṇiḥ // (2673)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram //:

	bhūmau yakṣamukhaṃ likhya yasyāgryāṅulito nakham /
	nihatya cakṣurdeśe tu samākarṣet striyo varāḥ // (2674)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2675)

tatredaṃ padmakulakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram //:

	padmaṃ gṛhya karābhyāṃ tu nirīkṣan rāgaśuddhitām /
	vajradṛṣṭyā tu sa strīṇāṃ gamayed antitas tathā // (2676)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2677)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmadharmatottamasiddhitantram //:

	vajraratnasamādhistho maṇiṃ gṛhyan tu pāṇinā /
	ratnahūṃkārayogena mārayet sarvayoṣitaḥ // (2678)

(( ityāha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // )) (2679)

sarvakulakarmadharmatottamasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2680)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatakarmakāryasiddhitantram udājahāra // (2681)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakarmakāryasiddhitantram //:

	pūjākarmavidhiṃ yojya yad yat kāryaṃ tu cintayet /
	tat tad vijñāpya mudrāṃ tu sādhayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ // (2682)

((ity āha bhagavān vajradhātuḥ (Ch.)
ity āha bhagavān buddhaḥ // (Tib) )) (2683)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulakarmakāryasiddhitantram //

	guhyapūjāvidhiṃ yojya vajrasattvasamādhinā /
	yatkāryaṃ vadate tat tu śīghraṃ siddhim avāpnuyāt // (2684)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2685)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakarmakāryadiddhitantram //:

	kulaguhyamahāpūjāṃ kṛtvā krodhasamādhinā /
	yat kiñcit cintayet prājñaḥ sa śīghraṃ siddhim eṣyati // (2686)

ity āha bhagavān vajrakrodhaḥ // (2687)

tatredaṃ padmakulakarmakāryasiddhitantram //:

	kṛtvā tu mānaṣīṃ pūjāṃ lokeśvarasamādhinā /
	yat kāryaṃ cintayet prājñaḥ tat sarvaṃ śīghram āpnuyāt // (2688)

ity āha bhagavān padmadharaḥ // (2689)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmakāryasiddhitantram //

	kṛtvā dhūpādibhiḥ pūjāṃ vajragarbhasamādhinā /
	yat kāryaṃ cintayet prājñaḥ tat sarvaṃ sidhyati kṣaṇāt // (2690)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbhaḥ // (2691)

sarvakulakarmakāryasiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2692)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvatathāgatamudrābhāvanāsiddhitantram udājahāra //: (2693)

tatredaṃ tathāgatādhiṣṭhānayogasiddhitantraṃ bhavati //:

	sūkṣmavajraprayogeṇa buddhayogasamāhitaḥ /
	uttamāṃ siddhim āpnoti buddhamudrāprasādhakaḥ // (2694)

ity āha bhagavān vajrapāṇis tathāgataḥ // (2695)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulasattvādhiṣṭhānayogasiddhitantram //

	sattvo hi sarvapratyātmā mamāpy ātmani saṃsthitaḥ /
	ity adhiṣṭhāya sattvo 'ham ahaṃkāreṇa bhāvayan sidhyati // (2696)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayo vajrasattvaḥ // (2697)

tatredaṃ vajrakulavajrādhiṣṭhānayogatantram //:

	yathā sattvas tathā mudrā yathā mudrās tathā hy aham /
	anena bhāvayogena sarvamudrās tu sādhayet // (2698)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2699)

tatredaṃ padmakuladharmādhiṣṭhānayogatantram //

	dharmamudrāprayogeṇa sūkṣmavajreṇa bhāvanā /
	vāṅmudrāṇāṃ tu tāḥ sarvāḥ mahāsattvasamādhir hi // (2700)

ity āha bhagavān āryāvalokiteśvaraḥ // (2701)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakarmādhiṣṭhānayogatantram //

	sarvabuddhābhiṣekāṇi pūjāsamayasiddhayaḥ /
	bhagavān iti bhāvena sādhayed vajrakarmāṇi /
	vajrakarmāṇi sādhayet bhagavān iti bhāvayan // (2702)

ity āha bhagavān vajrakarmaḥ // (2703)

sarvakulamudrābhāvanāsiddhividhivistaratantram // // (2704)


atha bhagavantaḥ sarvatathāgatāḥ punaḥ samājam āgamya,
bhagavate sarvatathāgatacakravarine vajrapāṇaye mahābodhisattvāya sādhukārāṇy adaduḥ //: (2705)

	sādhu te vajrasattvāya vajraratnāya sādhu te /
	vajradharmāya te sādhu sādhu te vajrakarmaṇe // (2706)

	subhāṣitam idaṃ sūtraṃ vajrayānam anuttaram /
	sarvatāthāgataṃ guhyaṃ mahāyānābhisaṃgraham // iti (2707)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃgrahāt sarvakalpaguhyottamatantravidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // (2708)


(sarvakalpānuttaratantra) (2709)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisatt imāṃ gāthām abhāṣat //:

	durdṛṣṭāṃ viraktānām idaṃ guhyaṃ na yugyate /
	sarvasattvahitārthāya vakṣyāmi vidhayas tathā // iti (2711)

atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ punar api sarvatathāgatpacāravidhivistaram abhāṣat //: (2712)

tatrāyaṃ tathāgatakulopacāravidhivistaraḥ //: (2713)

tatrāyaṃ hṛdayopacāravidhivistaro bhavati //:
mahāmaṇḍalaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhūpapuṣpadīpagandhapūjāṃ mudrābhiḥ kṛtvā tato vajravācā jāpam ārabhet // (2714)

tatrāyaṃ jāpavidhir bhavati //:
yathāsthānasthitaś caturmāsaṃ catuḥsaṃdhyaṃ dhūpādibhir yathāvat pūjāṃ kṛtvā,
sarvatathāgatamahāyānābhisamayanāmāṣṭaśatena sarvatathāgatān adhiṣṭutya,
caturmudrāpraṇāmayogena praṇamann ātmaniryātanapūjā kāryānena mantracatuṣṭayena // (2715)

	oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjopasthānāyātmānaṃ niryātayāmi,
	sarvatathāgatavajrasattvādhiṣṭhasva mām // (2716)

	oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjābhiṣekāyātmānaṃ niryātayāmi,
	sarvatathāgatavajraratnābhiṣiñca mām // (2717)

	oṃ sarvatathāgatapūjāpravartanāyātmānaṃ niryātayāmi,
	sarvatathāgatavajradharma pravartaya mām // (2718)

	oṃ sarvatahāgatapūjākarmaṇa ātmānaṃ niryātayāmi,
	sarvatathāgatavajrakarma kuru māṃ // (2719)

tato 'viraktaḥ sarvakāmaguṇeṣu sarvāhāraḥ sarvakāmopabhogī hṛdayārthataḥ svam ātmānaṃ buddhabimbaṃ purato vāṅmātreṇāpi bhāvayan yathākāmakaraṇīyatayāṣṭaśataṃ vajravācā jāpann āśu prasidhyati. (2720)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2721)

athottamasiddhim icchet /
tataḥ icchantena paṭe bhagavantaṃ tathāgataṃ madhye lekhayet / (2722)

tasya caturmāhāsattvamaṇḍalayogena yathābhirucitavarṇābharaṇā mahāsattvāś candramaṇḍalapratiṣṭhitā lekhyāḥ koṇabhāgeṣu kuladevya iti // (2723)

tataḥ paṭasyodārāṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā, yathāvaj japayogena tāvaj japed yāvan māsacatuṣṭayam / (2724)

tataḥ sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ prabhāte sarvatathāgatatattvādim uttamasiddhim avāpnoti / (2725)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2726)

atha mudrāsādhanam icchantena sarvatathāgatasattvavajrimudrāṃ baddhvā,
paṭasyāgrato vajravācā śatasahasraṃ yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā yathāvad bandhan muñcaṃś ca japet // (2727)

tato 'nte sakalāṃ rātrim aviśramataḥ kaṃ cit kālaṃ muñcan yathavac ca bandhan japet / (2728)

tato mudrā jvalaty āviśaty uttiṣṭhati vācaṃ muñcati // iti (2729)

tato mudrābandhenotpatati /
kāmarūpī bhavati /
antardhāti /
sarvakarmāṇi ca karoti /
sarvamudrāś ca baddhamātrā yathāvat sarvakarmāṇi kurvanti / (2730)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2731)


atha samādhayo 'dhīpset /
tena sūkṣmavajrād ārabhya, yaṃ samādhiṃ abhirocet taṃ hṛdayayogato 'bhyaset tāvad yāvac caturmāsam / (2732)

tato 'nte sakalāṃ rātriṃ paryaṅkabaddhaḥ samāpannaḥ sthātavyaḥ. tetathāgatādyāḥ sarvasiddhaya āmukhībhavati // (2733)

tato yādṛśy abhirucis tādṛśīsiddhiḥ (2734)

itya āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2735)


atha karmasādhanaṃ bhavati //:
tathaiva japen māsaṃ ekaṃ sādhayet /
tato 'nte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet / (2737)

tataḥ sarvakarmasiddhim avāpntoti (2737)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ (2738)


atha karmāṇi bhavanti //:
sakṛd uccāritenātmaparagrāmanagararakṣā bhavati kabacabaddhādibhiḥ // (2739)

āveśayet ca candanena sugandhena spṛṣṭāspṛṣṭavajrāṅkuśaśarahastaratnasūryadhvajadantapaṅkutipadmakhaḍgacakrajihvāsarvavajrakavacadaṃṣṭrāmuṣṭimudrādīni sarvabhāvāny āveśayati sakṛj japtena / (2740)

māyākarma ca mayūrapattrapicchake vajrān viddhvā bandhayet /
tatas taṃ mayūrāṅgapicchakaṃ sattvavajrimudrayāvapīḍya tāvaj japed yāvat sarvatathāgatamudrāviśati // (2741)

tataś ca picchakān nānādyāni rūpāṇi paśyati // (2742)

tataḥ prabhṛti tena picchakena sarvarūpāṇi vidhivad darśayati / (2743)

tenaiva picchakena sakṛjjaptabhrāmitenātmanaḥ sarvarūpāṇi darśayati // (2744)

tenaiva picchakena laukikāni māyākarmāṇi darśayanti /
buddhabodhisattvabimbāny api darśayati // (2745)

daśasu dikṣu sarvabuddhakṣetreṣu tathāgatāḥ sasarṣanmaṇḍalāḥ samārasenādharṣaṇādibuddharddhivikurvitāni kurvanto darśayati /
yāvat sarvākāravaropetaṃ buddharūpam ātmānaṃ bhavatīti // (2746)

vaśīkaraṇaṃ kartukāmaḥ sarvatathāgatasattvavajrīmudrāṃ baddhvā tāvaj japed yāvat sā mudrā jvalati // (2747)

tataḥ prabhṛti mudrābandhena sarvatathāgatān apy ārāgayati vaśīkaroti kiṃ punaru anyān sattvān // (2748)

atha laukikottamasiddhayaḥ sādhayitukāmena tenādita eva tathaiva japatā māsam ekam aṣṭasāhasrikeṇa japena,
tato 'nte mudrāṃ baddhvā,
tathaiva sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet tāvad yāvan mudrā jvalati // (2749)

tataḥ prabhṛti mudrābandhena laukikasiddhividyādharasiddhīnām ekatarā bhavati // (2750)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2751)

tathāgatakulopacāravidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (2752)


atha vajrakulopacāravidhivistaro bhavati //:
tatrādita eva pūrvasevāṃ kuryāt /
tatraiva yathākāmakaraṇīyatayākṣaralakṣaṃ japet / (2753)

tato 'nte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet / (2754)

tataḥ prabhṛti sarvasattvanigrahānugrahakṣamo bhavati / (2755)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2756)


atha sādhayitum icchantena yathāvat paṭaḥ śeśrāpayitavyaḥ / (2757)

tatas tathaiva pūjāṃ kṛtvā,
māsam ekaṃ sarvakāmabhojī yathākāmakaraṇīyatayāṣṭasāhasrikeṇa jāpena catuḥsaṃdhyā vajravācā japet / (2758)

tāvad yāvan māsānte paṭasyodārāṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā,
vajrahūṃkāramahāmudrāṃ baddhvā,
tāvaj japed yāvat tasmān mudrābandhād dhūṃkāraśabda udbilasṛtaḥ / (2759)

tataḥ prabhāte maheśvarādayo devādhipatayaḥ sagaṇaparivārāḥ puraḥ sthitvājñāṃ mārgayanti // (2760)

tato vidyādhareṇaivaṃ vaktavyam (2761)

	yadāhaṃ brūyām ``āgacchatedaṃ kuruta'', tadā bhavadbhir āgatya mamājñā kāryā // iti (2762)

tataḥ prabhṛti sakalatrilokādhipatir bhavati // (2763)

yathecchayā ca muhūrtamātreṇa sakalaṃ tribhuvanam ājñāpayan bhramati /
punar apy eti ca nigrahānugrahaṃ kurvan, (2764)

divyāni trilokabhogāni copabhuñjan, yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā savasurādhipatiyoṣitādyāḥ sarvayoṣita ārāgayitvopabhuñjati /
na ca tasya kaś cit kiṃ cic chaknoti kartum / (2765)

hūṃkāreṇa ca sarvaduṣṭadevādīn pātayan, tato 'ntarakalpasahasrāṇi jīvati / (2766)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2767)


atha mudrāsādhanam icchet // (2768)

yathāvaj japaṃ kṛtvā,
māsānte vajrahūṃkārasamayamudraṃ baddhvā sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ prabhāte mudrā siddhā bhavanti // (2769)

tato yathāvan mudrābandhena hūṃkāraprayuktenākāśagamanaviśvasaṃdarśanāntardhānamāyāsaṃdarśanasarvāveśanākarṣaṇavaśīkaraṇasarvatuṣṭisaṃjananasarvaratnābhiharaṇamahātejojvālāsaṃdarśanaratnavṛṣṭisaṃdarśanamahāṭṭahāsapramuñcanasarvasattvasaṃśodhanachindanabhindanartucakraparivartanayathāvattattvollāpanasarvakarmapravartanarakṣājambhanastambhatrāsanamāraṇasarvasattvamudraṇakāmaratikriyāpravartanābhiṣekasarvabhāvagāyāpananṛtyāpanāhvāpanapraveśanasphoṭanāveśanādīni sarvakarmāṇi karoti (2770-2775)

atha sūkṣmajñānasādhanam ucchet / (2776)

tena vajrahūṃkārasamādhim abhyasatā tathaiva jāpayogena māsam ekaṃ sādhayitavyam / (2777)

tato 'nte tenaiva samādhinā sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tāvad yāvat prabhāte pañcābhijño bhūtvā sarvasattvānugrahanigrahakṣamo bhavati (2778)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2779)

atha karmasādhana icchet / (2780)

tena tathaiva japatā māsam ekaṃ sādhayitavyam // (2781)

tato 'nte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ sarvakarmāṇi sidhyanti / (2782)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2783)


tataḥ karmāṇi bhavanti //
sakṛd uccāritena manīṣitayā rakṣādīni sarvakarmāṇi karoti // (2784)

vajrakulopacāravidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (2785)


atha padmaklopacāravidhivistaro bhavati //:
tatrādita eva tāvac chatasahasraṃ japet /
pūrvasevākṛto bhavati // (2786)

tataḥ sādhanaṃ bhavati //:
paṭe bhagavantaḥ sarvajagadvinayādyāḥ kartavyās tasya sarvapārśveṣu caturmaṇḍalayogena mahāsattvacatuṣṭayaḥ kāryante ca devyaḥ / (2787)

tataḥ sa eva japavidhivistaro māsānte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ sarvajagadvinayo bhagavān āgacchati /
yathākālaṃ vajreṇābhipracārayati / (2788)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2789)

atha mudrāsādhanam icchet /
tena tathaiva padmavajrimudrābandhaṃ kṛtvā yathāvan muñcyāṣṭasāharikeṇa japena catuḥsaṃdhyaṃ japet / (2790)

tataḥ sakalāṃ rātriṃ mudrābandhena japet /
prabhāte siddhir bhavati /
tato mudrābandhena yathāvat sarvajagadvinayaṃ karoti / (2791)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2792)

atha samādhinayasādhanam icchet /
tena tathaiva māsānte sakalāṃ rātriṃ yathābhirucitena samādhinā japo dātavyaḥ /
tataḥ prabhāte sarvasamādhayaḥ āmukhībhavati // (2793)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2794)


atha karmasādhanam icchet /
tathaiva japya māsānte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ sarvakarmakṣamo bhavati / (2795)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2796)

padmakulopacāravidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // // (2797)


atha maṇikulopacāravidhivistaro bhavati // (2798)

tatrādita eva sarvatathāgatapraṇāmacatuṣṭayaṃ kṛtvā śatasahasraṃ japet /
tatas tathiava paṭe bhagavantaṃ sarvārthasiddhiṃ caturmudrāmaṇḍalayogena likhet /
tatas tathaiva pūjāṃ kṛtvā tathaiva sādhayet /
māsānte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet / (2799)

tataḥ prabhāte bhagavān sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaratna ākāśagarbho bodhisattva āgatyābhiṣekaṃ dadāti /
tenābhiṣekeṇa trisāhasramahāsāhasralokadhātau vidyādharacakravartī bhavati / (2800)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2801)

atha mudrāsādhanam icchet /
tena tathaiva dharmavajriprayogeṇa vajraratnamudrā yathāvat sādhyā sarvāśākarmakarī bhavati / (2802)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2803)

atha maṇijñānam icchet sādhayitum /
tena tathaiva vajraratnodbhavasamādhir yathānukramato bhāvayitavyaḥ /

	niṣvabhāvād ākāśāt kathaṃ ratnasaṃbhava iti
	ratnāc ca kathaṃ bodhisattvakāyasaṃbhava ity

imaṃ samādhiṃ catuḥsaṃdhyaṃ bhāvya japed yathopari / (2805)

tato māsānte tenaiva samādhinā sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ prabhāte sarvatathāgatair āgatya yathābhirucito 'bhyṣicyata (2806)

ity āha bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ // (2807)

atha karmasādhanaṃ bhavati /
tena tathaiva japatā māsānte sakalāṃ rātriṃ japet /
tataḥ prabhāte bhagavān ākāśagarbhaḥ sarvārthasādhako bhavatīti / (2808)

tataḥ sarvakarmāṇi kuryāt / (2809)

ity āha bhagavān āryavajradharaḥ // (2810)

maṇikulopacāravidhivistaraḥ samāptaḥ // (2811)



athāyaṃ sarvakulasādhāraṇasādhanopacāravidhivistaro bhavati //: (2812)

tatrādita eva sarvahṛdayopacāravidhivistaro bhavati // (2813)

hṛdayamanīṣitāni sarvatathāgatānāṃ sidhyantām ity uccārya hṛdayaṃ yathābhirucito japya sādhanavidhiḥ kartavya iti // (2814)

tatrāyaṃ mudropacāravidhiḥ //
sarvamudrā me priyā bhavantv ity uktvā samayamudrāṃ baddhvā yathābhirucito yathāśaktyā japet /
tato yathāvat siddhir iti // (2815)

tatrāyaṃ sarvamantropacāravidhiḥ //
niṣprapañcā vāk siddhir bhavatu /
sarvatathāgatasamādhayo me ājāyantām ity ukutvā mantraṃ yathābhirucito japet /
eṣā siddhir iti // (2816)

tatrāyaṃ vidyopacāravidhiḥ //
avidyāndhā bateme sattvāḥ sarvatathāgatāś ca vidyādhigamasaṃvarabhūtā ity uktvā vidyāṃ yathābhirucito japya sādhanam āvahet // (2817)

ity āha bhagavān āryavajradharaḥ // (2818)

atha sarvahṛdayamudrāmantravidyānāṃ yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā vajrajāpavidhivistaro bhavati // (2819)

	yasya sattvasya hṛn mudrāṃ mantraṃ vidyāṃ tu sādhayet /
	jāpārthatas tam ātmānaṃ sattvaṃ vā sādhya sidhyati // (2820)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2821)

sarvakulasādhāraṇajāpavidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // (2822)

athasarvakulasādhāraṇasiddhividhivistaro bhavati // (2823)

atrādita eva tathāgatakulasiddhayaḥ //
tad yatha, arthaniṣpattisiddhiḥ, ṛddhisiddhiḥ, vidyādharatvam, mahāsiddhiś ceti // (2824)

tatrārthasiddhiniṣpattir bhavati //
yatra nidhiśaṅkā bhavet tatra mudrāṃ baddhvā svasamādhinā tan nidhisthānaṃ vajradṛṣṭyā nrīkṣayet /
yadi vajrākāramūrtiścutaṃ paśyati tato jñātavyaṃ nidhir atrāstīti // (2825)

tato vajrasphoṭasamayamudrāṃ baddhvotkhanya yathākāmakaraṇīyatayā gṛhuṇīyāt / acirāc cāpnoti (2826)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2827)

tatra rddhisiddhiniṣpattir bhavati //

yāṃ mudrāṃ sādhayed vajrasddhir ity uktvā rddhisiddhiś caturvidhā bhavati / (2828)

[tad yathā]
jalasyopari caṅkramaṇaniṣīdanādikam /
tathāgatādisarvarūpasaṃdarśanam /
yāvad abhirucis tāvad adṛśyatvam /
ākāśagāmī ca [yo]janasahasramūrdhnam utpa[ta]ty adhastāc ca gacchaty āgacchati // (2829)

sarvadiśaś ca yojanasahasrād yathābhirucitavegaḥ paribhramyāgacchati /
yojanasahasrād adhvena sarvasattvamanīṣitāni jānāti // (2830)

sarvabhāvāni ca cakṣuṣā paśyati /
śrotreṇa śṛṇoti /
sarvadikṣu ca yojanasahasrād adhvena manobhirucitāḥ sarvastriyo 'ṅge samutkṣipyānayati // (2831)

sarvahiraṇyasuvarṇamaṇimuktādayaś ca sarvārthān apaharati //
na cāsya kaścit kiṃ cic chaknoti kartum /
yad vajreṇāpy adhṛṣyo bhavati, kiṃ punar apy anyaiḥ // (2832)

daśapuruṣasahasrabalī, nityārogyavān, nityaṃ sarvakāmopabhojī, sadā yauvano, divyarūpī, sarvatathāgatān savajrasattvān paśyan pūjayaṃś cānuttaravajrasiddhiś catvāri varṣasahasrāṇi jīvati (2833)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatavajrarddhi[siddhi]ḥ // (2834)


tatreyaṃ vajravidyādharasiddhiniṣpattir bhavati //

mudrāṃ sādhayan vajravidyādhara iti brūyāt //
siddhayā vajravidyādharacakravartī bhavati //
sarvakāmopabhogī sahasrabuddhakṣetram ekakṣaṇena paribhramyāgacchati // (2835)

sarvasukhāni paribhuñjan dviraṣṭavarṣavapur ākuñcitakuṇḍalakeśadhārimahāvajravidyādharaḥ sarvatathāgatān savajrasattvān paśyan mahākalpasthāyī bhavati (2836)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatavidyādharaḥ // (2837)


tatra mahāsiddhiniṣpattir bhavati //
svamudrāṃ hṛdayārthataḥ sādhayet /
svamudrāsattvarūpī bhavaty ekakṣaṇena daśasu dikṣu sarvalokadhātuṣu viśvarūpī viśvakriyāpravartakaḥ (2839)

sarvatathāgatān savajrasattvān dṛṣṭvā sarvākāravaropetābhiḥ sarvatathāgatapūjābhiḥ saṃpūjyāśeṣānavaśeṣasattvārthaṃ ca kṛtvā punar apy āyāti // (2839)

sarvalokadhātusarvakāmasarvasukhasaumanasyāni sarvākāravaropetāny upabhuñjan vajrasattvasamo mahābodhisattvo 'śeṣānavaśeṣamahākalpāyur bhavati (2840)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasiddhiḥ // (2841)


tatraitā vajrakulasiddhayaḥ //
tadyathā
trilokavijayasiddhiḥ /
sarvābhiṣekasiddhiḥ /
sarvasukhasaumanasya siddhiḥ /
uttamasiddhir iti // (2842)

tatra trilokavijayasiddhir bhavati //
trilokavijayamudrāṃ baddhvā maheśvaraṃ vā[mapā]denākramya sādhayet /.
tataḥ sā pratimā nādaṃ muñcati /
tato *hūṃkāraḥ (huṃkāraḥ, ed.) prayoktavyaḥ / (2843)

*hūṃkāra(huṃkāra-, ed.)prayuktamātre maheśvarādayaḥ sarvatrailokyādhipatayaḥ saparivārāḥ sādhakasya purata. āgatyājñāvaśyavidheyā bhavanti // (2844)

tataḥ prabhṛti sarvatrilokādhipatir vajradharo bhavati /
ākāśena gacchati /
sakalatrilokacakraṃ parikramyāgacchati /
duṣṭadevādayaś ca sarvasattvān *hūṃkāreṇa (huṃkāreṇa, ed.) damayati / (2845)

sarvatathāgatavajra*hūṃ(-huṃ, ed.)kārarūpī sakalatrilokam ājñayā vartayan sarvatathāgatān savajrasattvān paśyann ārāgayaṃś ca varṣasahasraṃ jīvati (2846)

ity āha bhagavān *vajrahūṃkāraḥ (vajrahuṃkāraḥ, ed.) // (2847)


tatreyaṃ sarvābhiṣekasiddhiḥ //

mudrāṃ sādhayet /
sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaratnamudrayā pūrvam ātmānam abhiṣicya sādhayet /. (2848)

tasya tasya siddhasya caturvidham abhiṣeko bhavati /
vajrābhiṣeko ratnābhiṣeko dharmābhiṣekaḥ karmābhiṣekaś ceti // (2849)

tatra vajrābhiṣeke labdhe sarvatathāgatānāṃ vajradharo bhavati /
ratnābhiṣeke sarvaratnādhipatir bhavati /
dharmābhiṣeke dharmarājo bhavati /
karmābhiṣeke laukikalokottarasarvakarmasiddhim avāpnoti (2850)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatābhiṣekaḥ // (2851)

tatreyaṃ sukhasaumanasya siddhir yad uta guhyapūjābhir nityaṃ sarvatathāgatapūjāṃ kurvan sarvatathāgatasarvasukhasaumanasya siddhim avāpnoti (2852)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasarvasukhasaumanasyaḥ // (2853)


tatreyam uttamasiddhiḥ //
yad uta vajradharasamo 'ham (2854)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2855)


tatraitāḥ padmakulasiddhayaḥ //
tad yathā
anurāgaṇavaśīkaraṇarakṣāpadmasiddhiś ceti // (2856)

tatrānurāgaṇasiddhir bhavati /
yathāvat padmarāgabhāvanayā sarvatathāgatādisarvasattvānurāgaṇakṣamo bhavati / (2857)

svaṃ lokeśvarānusmṛtyā tathaiva sarvasattvavaśīkaraṇasamartho bhavati / (2858)

maitryaspharaṇasamādhinā sarvajagadrakṣāvaraṇaguptikṣamo bhavati / (2859)

svaṃ padmasamādhinā padmaṃ hasena gṛhya sādhayan lokeśvararūpī sarvākāravaropetaś caturvarṣasahasraṃ jīvati (2860)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatapadmaḥ // (2861)


tatraitā maṇikuladiddhayaḥ //

tad yathā
sarvakulābhiṣekasiddhiḥ /
mahātejastvam /
sarvāśāprapūraṇam /
ratnasiddhiś ceti // (2862)

tatra sarvatathāgatābhiṣekasiddhiḥ /
yad uta svābhiṣekaniryātanapradīpadānapāramitāpāripūrir yathāśaktyā ratnasādhanaṃ cety ābhiḥ siddhibhiḥ sarvatathāgatān pūjayann acirāt sidhyati (2863)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataratnaḥ // (2864)

sarvakulasādhāraṇa[siddhi]vidhivistaraḥ parisamāptaḥ // (2865)


atha sarvakalpopāyasiddhitantram anuvyākhyasyāmīty āha bhagavān anādisattvaḥ // (2866)

((tatrādita eva hṛdayopāyasiddhitantram //)) (2867)

	yathā vineyo loko hi tādṛśīsiddhir iṣyate /
	upāyas tatra mudrā hi sarvasiddhipradaṃ mahat // (2868)

tatredaṃ mudropāyasiddhitantram //

	virāgavinayo loko mudrāsiddhis tu rāgajā /
	upāyo bhāvanā tatra sarvasiddhikarī varā // (2869)

tatredaṃ mantropāyasiddhitantram //

	loko 'yaṃ satyavibhraṣṭo mantrasiddhir na iṣyate /
	upāyo niṣprapañcas tu sarvasiddhikaraḥ paraḥ //  (2870)

tatredaṃ vidyopāyasiddhitantra //

	avidyābhiniviṣṭo 'yaṃ vidyāsiddhir na iṣyate /
	upāyas tatra tv anudāryaṃ sarvasiddhipradaṃ varam //

iti // (2871)

sarvakalpopāyasiddhitantram // // (2872)


atha sarvakalpapuṇyasiddhitantram anuvyākhyāsyāmīty āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataḥ // (2873)

tatrādita eva svahṛdayapuṇyasiddhitantram //

	kṛtvā caturvidhāṃ pūjāṃ mahāpuṇyam avāpnute /
	buddhapūjāsv apuṇyāpi sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ //

iti. (2874)

tatredaṃ mudrāpuṇyasiddhitantram //

	rakṣaṃs tu samayaṃ guhyaṃ mahāpuṇyam avāpnute /
	apuṇye 'pi hi sidhyeta śīghraṃ smayarakṣaṇāt //

iti. (2875)

tatredaṃ mantrapuṇyasiddhitantram //

	buddhanāmādivacanair mahāpuṇyam avāpnuyāt /
	dharmadānād apuṇye 'pi śīghraṃ siddhim avāpnute // (2876)

tatredaṃ vidyāpuṇyasiddhitantram //

	dānam agryaṃ hi puṇyānāṃ dadan puṇyam avāpnute /
	dānapāramitāpūrṇaḥ śīghraṃ buddhatvam āpnute //

iti. (2876)

salvakalpapuṇyasiddhitantram // (2878)


atha sarvakalpaprajñāsiddhitantram anuvyākhyāsyāmi // (2879)

((ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataḥ // )) (2880)

tatrādita eva hṛdayaprajñāsiddhitantram //

	a-akarṣapraveśena sarvākṣaravijñānatā /
	svavaktrāparavaktraṃ tu bhāvayan siddhim āpnuyāt // (2881)

ity āha bhagavān mañjuśrīmahābodhisattvaḥ // (2882)

tatredaṃ mudrāprajñāsiddhitantram //

	prajñā nairvedhikī nāma samāsiddhir iti kīrtitā /
	tayā tu mudrāḥ sidhyante bhāvayan sidhyati kṣaṇāt // (2883)

ity āha bhagavān prajñāgryaḥ // (2884)

tatredaṃ mantraprajñāsiddhitantram //

	prajñā ghoṣānugā nāma samādhir vākprapañcataḥ /
	tayā bhāvitayā śīghraṃ mantrasiddhim avāpnuyāt // (2885)

ity āha bhagavān vajrabuddhiḥ // (2886)

tatredaṃ vidyāprajñāsiddhitantram //

	vidyāmantraviśeṣāṇāṃ viśeṣā na hi vidyate /
	prajñayā bhāvayann evam āśu siddhir dhruvā bhavet // (2887)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataprajñājñānaḥ // (2888)

sarvakalpaprajñājñānasiddhividhivistaratantram // (2889)

atha sarvakalpasaṃbhārasiddhitantram anuvyākhyasyāmīty āha bhagavān vajrapāṇiḥ // (2890)

tatrādita eva sarvahṛdayasaṃbhārasiddhitantram //

	sarvapūjāṃ prakurvāṇaḥ saṃbhāras tu vivardhate /
	kuśalānāṃ tu dharmāṇāṃ tataḥ sidhyati saṃbhṛtaḥ // (2891)

tatredaṃ mudrāsaṃbhārasiddhitantram //

	bahucakrapraveśāc ca bahumaṇḍalakalpanāt /
	[saṃbhāraṃ pūrya mudrāṇāṃ] mahāsiddhiḥ pravartate // (2892)

tatredaṃ mantrasaṃbhārasiddhitantram //

	anumodanādiyogena saddharmapaṭhanāt tathā /
	bahujāpapradānāc ca mantrasiddhir dhruvā bhavet //

iti // (2893)

tatredaṃ vidyāsaṃbhārasiddhitantram // (2894)

	((avidyāsuprahīnatvād dānapāramitānayāt /
	saṃbhāraparipūrṇas tu śīghraṃ siddhim avāpnute //

iti. (2895)

sarvakalpasaṃbhārasiddhitantram // ))

sarvakalpavidhivistaratantraṃ parisamāptam // (2897)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvakulacihnasaṃbhavajñānatantram udājahāra //:
tatra kathaṃ vajrasaṃbhavaḥ ? (2898)

	sa eva bhagavān sattvaḥ sarvacittaḥ svayaṃprabhuḥ /
	kāyavākcittavajras tu dṛḍhaḥ sattvaḥ svyaṃbhuvām // (2899)

	sattvānām uttamaḥ sattvo vajrabhāvanayā hṛdi /
	vajrasattvā iti khyātas tasmin vajre pratiṣṭhitaḥ // (2890)

	sa eva jñānayogena buddhānām asamatviṣām /
	niṣkramya hṛdayād viśvo viśvarūpo bhavaty api // (2901)

	sarvadhāturajaḥsaṃkhyāḥ sa eva tu jino bhavet /
	tebhyo vai vajrakāyebhyo vajrasattvas tu saṃbhavet // (2902)

	tata evādisattvāt tu sarvacihnasamudbhavaḥ /
	cihnebhyas tu mahāsattvās tebhyaḥ sarvam idaṃ nayam //

iti. (2903)

	ya idaṃ śṛṇuyāt kaścic chraddhadhed dhārayed dhṛdi /
	bhāvayec ca sadā tuṣṭaḥ sa śīghraṃ siddhim āpnuyāt // (2904)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2905)

sarvatathāgatatattvasaṃbhavajñānavidhivistaratantram // (2906)


atha vajrapāṇir mahābodhisattvaḥ sarvakalpasaṃbhavajñānavidhivistaratantram abhāṣat // (2907)

tatrādita eva tāvat sarvatathāgatakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantraṃ bhavati //

	buddhānām avikalpaṃ tu jñānaṃ bhavati śāśvatam /
	avikalpāt tato jñānāt kalpanāt kalpaḥ udyate // (2908)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantram //

	yathāvikalpaḥ kalpātmā kalpyate kalpanodbhavaḥ /
	vajrasattvo mahāsattvaḥ tena kalpo nirucyate // (2909)

tatredaṃ vajrakulakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantram //

	yam ālikhya hi kalpante vidhayaḥ kalpasiddhidaḥ /
	tena kalpa iti prokto vikalparahitātmabhiḥ // (2910)

tatredaṃ padmakulakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantram //

	rāgo vikalpasaṃbhūtaḥ sa ca padme pratiṣṭhitaḥ /
	tatas tu kalpasthāyinyaḥ siddhayaḥ sa bhavanti hi // (2911)

tatredaṃ maṇikulakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantram // (2912)

((nāgovikalpasañjātaḥ sa ca padmapratiṣṭhitaḥ /)) (2913)
%% this has been caused by the eyeskip of the scrib
%% see \S\thinspace 2911

	maṇayo hy avikalpās tu prabhāvaiḥ susamucchritāḥ /
	evaṃ tu siddhayo divyāḥ saṃbhavanty avikalpitāḥ // (2914)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2915)

sarvakulakalpasaṃbhavajñānatantram // (2916)


[atha sarvakalpahṛdayādisaṃbhavajñānatantram //]

atha sarvakalpahṛdayasaṃbhavajñānatantram //

	manīṣitavidhānais tu sidhyate tu manīṣitam /
	samādhisādhano hṛtstho hṛdayaṃ tena procyate // (2917)

atha sarvamudrāsaṃbhavajñānatantram //

	duratikramo yathā 'bhedyo rājamudrāgraśāsanaḥ /
	mahātmacihnabimbas tu tathā mudreti kīrtitā // (2918)

((atha mantrasaṃbhavajñānatatram // (2919)

	anatikramaṇīyo hi durbhedyo guhya eva ca /
	mantryate guhyasiddhyarthaṃ mantras tena nirucyate // (2920)

atha vidyāsaṃbhavajñānatantram // )) (2921)

	avidyāvipraṇāśāyā vāgvidyāgraprasiddhaye /
	vidyate vedanā siddhis tena vidyā prakīrtitā // (2922)

ity āha bhagavān vajradharaḥ // (2923)

sarvakalpahṛdayādisaṃbhavajñānatantram // (2924)


atha sarvakalpajñānotpattitantram // (2925)

tatrādita e[va] hṛdayajñānotpattitantraṃ bhavati //

	hṛdayaṃ jāpya vijñeyam ātmano vā parasya vā /
	bhavyaṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati śṛṇoti ca // (2926)

tatredaṃ mudrājñānotpattitantraṃ bhavati //

	mudrām ekatarāṃ baddhvā yathāvad vidhim ātmanaḥ /
	kṛtvā nirīkṣel lokaṃ tu sarvaṃ jñeyaṃ yathopari //

iti. (2927)

tatredaṃ mantrajñānotpattitantram //

	sakṛd uccārayan mantraṃ brūyāj jihvāṃ svakīṃ tu yaḥ /
	bhavyaṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ satyam āvahet // (2928)

ity āha bhagavān avalokiteśvaraḥ // (2929)

tatredaṃ vidyājñānotpattitantram //

	sakṛd uccārya vidyāṃ tu vedayan manasā sa tu /
	bhavyabhūtabhaviṣyāni [vajrājñāvaca]naṃ yathā //

iti. (2930)

sarvakalpajñānotpattividhivistaratantraṃ parisamāptam // (2931)

atha sarvakulasādhāraṇaguhyakāyavākcittavajramudrāsādhanatantraṃ bhavati // (2932)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulaguhyakāyamudrāsādhana[tantra]ṃ bhavati //

	yathā tathābhiṣaṇṇās tu paryaṅkena tu sādhayet /
	yathā lekhyānusāreṇa mahāsattvaḥ prasidhyati // (2933)

ity āha bhagavān vajrasattvaḥ // (2934)

tatredaṃ vajrakulaguhyakāyamudrāsādhana[tantra]ṃ bhavati //

	pratyālīḍhasusaṃsthānaṃ yathā lekhyānusārataḥ /
	sādhayeta susaṃkruddhaḥ sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ // (2935)

ity āha bhagavān vajrahūṃkāraḥ // (2936)

tatredaṃ padmakulaguhyakāyamudrāsādhana[tantra]ṃ bhavati //

	vajraparyaṅkasaṃsthaṃ tu vajrabandhaṃ karadvayam /
	samādhikāyo bhūtvā tu sādhayet padmasaṃbhavam // (2937)

ity āha bhagavan padmasattvaḥ // (2938)

tatredaṃ maṇikulaguhyakāyamudrāsādhana[tantra]ṃ bhavati //

	utthito vā niṣaṇṇo vā caṅkraman vā yathā tathā /
	vajraratnābhiṣekeṇa sidhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ // (2939)

ity āha bhagavān vajragarbha // (2940)


tatredaṃ tathāgatakulaguhyavāṅmudrāsādhanatantram // (2941)

	nābhiṣpanditajihvāgrādantoṣṭhadvayasaṃpuṭā /
	sādhayet sarvakalpāni vajravāk svaravarjitā // (2942)

ity āha bhagavān vajravācaḥ // (2943)

tatredaṃ vajrakulaguhyavāṅmudrāsādhanatantram //

	meghaghūrṇita*hūṃ(huṃ, ed.)kārā krodhagambhīravāk sthirā /
	krodhasphuṭā mahāvajrā sidhyate vajrakrodhavāk // (2944)

ity āha bhagavān *vajrahūṃkāraḥ (vajrahuṃkāraḥ, ed.) // (2945)

tatredaṃ padmakulaguhyavāṅmudrāsādhanatantram //

	anucchvā[sam ivocchvā]saṃ (or ucchvasan vā anucchvāsaṃ)
	sūkṣmavā[cāpari]sphuṭam /
	sidhyate sarvajāpāni samādhijñānagarbhayā // (2946)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatasamādhijñānagarbhaḥ // (2947)

tatredaṃ maṇikulaguhyavāṅmudrāsādhanatantram //

	suparisphuṭayā vācā praṇāmaparamaḥ sadā /
	jāpate vinayaiś cāpi sarvam āśu prasidhyati // (2948)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgatapūjāvi[dhivista]rakarmā //


tatredaṃ tathāgatakulaguhyacittamudrāsādhanatantram // (2950)

	kāmo hi bhagavāñ chaśvat sarvasattvasukhapradaḥ /
	vajrasattvaḥ svayam[ātma i]ti bhāvyāśu sidhyati // (2951)

ity āha bhagavān kāmaḥ // (2952)

tatredaṃ vajrakulaguhyacittamudrāsādhanatantram //

	sarvasattvahitārthāya duṣṭānāṃ śāsanāya [ca /]
	buddhaśāsanarakṣārthaṃ krodhaḥ siddhikaraḥ paraḥ // (2953)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgata*vajrahūṃkāraḥ(vajrahuṃkāraḥ, ed.) // (2954)

tatredaṃ padmakulaguhyacittamudrāsādhanatantram //

	yathā padmam aliptaṃ tu vāsadoṣaiḥ surāgavān /
	tathā me rāgadoṣais tu bhave rāgaḥ sa sidhyati // (2955)

ity ahā bhagavān padmarāgaḥ // (2956)

tatredaṃ maṇikulaguhyacittamudrāsādhanatantram //

	kadā nu sarvasattvānāṃ sarvakāryārthasiddhaye /
	ratnavarṣāṇi varṣayaṃ siddhaḥ sann āśu sidhyati // (2957)

ity āha bhagavān āryākāśagarbhaḥ // (2958)

tatredaṃ tathāgatakulaguhyavajramudrāsādhanatantram // (2959)

	utthito vā niṣaṇṇo vā bhraman vāpi yathā tathā /
	vāmamudrāgrahakaraḥ sarvaṃ kurvan sa sidhyati // (2960)

ity āha bhagavān sarvatathāgataguhyavajrapā[ṇiḥ //] (2961)
